[kakawin sumanasāntaka,

*awighnama astu*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ hyaŋ-hyaŋ pinakādidewa ni karas para kawi makatattwa ŋ akṣara,
saŋ saṅkan paran iŋ palambaŋ atiduṙllabha kahanan ira n kawīśwara,
saŋ sūkṣma i kukus iŋ tanaḥ kinikiṙ iŋ kuku ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ aṅrĕgĕp laṅö,
māyākāra winimba nitya sinamādhi manurunana caṇḍi pustaka*

sambandhanya k aṅaṙccana i pada nira ahyun ajaṙ ajara milwa riŋ kawi,
yekī kāraṇa ni ṅhulun praṇata bhakti ri sira magawe namaskrĕti,
luṅgaḥ niŋ kalaṅön sapuṅgĕl asĕkaṙ kakawin inuparĕṅgan iŋ laṅö,
puṣpāñjalya ri jöŋ nira n sumanasāntaka caritakĕna astu sanmatan*

pūṙwwaprastuti niŋ kathā hana sira dwija taruṇa suśīla subrata,
śiṣya agastya sira prakāśa karĕṅö kasutapan ira nora tan wruha,
khyāti iŋ rāt trĕṇawindu nāma pinakesi niŋ ujaṙ-ujaṙ iŋ kadewatan,
sakweḥ niŋ hyaŋ anaṅśaya i hyuna nira aṅadĕha ri paṅadĕg surādhipa*

ndan saŋ hyaŋ suranātha mukhya pinakādi niŋ awĕdi manaṅśaya i hati,
lwiṙ tan duhkha sira ndan i twas awiweka riŋ aṅĕnana de niŋ olaha,
gūḍhākāra nira n wikalpa kadi tan hana panaha nahā nira alaha,
prāya i saŋ suyaśa n tĕka ŋ bhaya saka iŋ musuḥ awĕdi kaciṙyyana awĕdi*

wwantĕn rakwa warāpsarī linĕwiḥ iŋ sa haripada wagĕd wicakṣaṇa,
prajña dyaḥ hariṇīṅaranya tuwi waṅśaja wĕka-wĕka dewaputrikā,
sākṣāt hrū nikaŋ indracāpa subhaga iṅid iṅidan i hayunya dug siṅī,
aṅhiŋ sāra hiḍĕp hyaŋ indra śaraṇāśraya paṅalaha śakti niŋ tapa*

yekī rakwa kinon hyaŋ indra marĕka aṅucap ucapa rahasya riŋ taman,
śīghra anĕmbaḥ acum wulat nika sinuṅsuŋ iŋ ujaṙ amanis priyambada,
 Om  putrī saŋ anĕmwa kāṣṭaguṇan aṅhilaṅakĕna kaśaktin iŋ tapa,
aṅhiŋ māsku sinambhawa asiha paṅöbana niŋ aśaraṇa iŋ kadewatan*

wwantĕn brāhmaṇa siddhiśakti magawe tapa katĕka tĕka iŋ surālaya,
maṅde saṅśaya ni ṅhulun ndan alĕmĕḥ katĕṅĕra ri wikalpa niŋ hati,
saŋkṣepanya lumampaha anaku mamañcana maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
eñjiŋ māsku lumakwa wörakĕna riŋ hima sumiliba tan hana wruha*

nāhan de nira mojaṙ asru paṅutus nira lumarisa tan wruḥ iŋ bhaya,
kepwan dyaḥ hariṇī katon gĕgĕḥ i suṅsut ira yadin apakṣa laṅghana,
rĕs lāwan pagĕḥ iŋ kabhaktin ika kāraṇa niki n ubhaya n lumampaha,
paṅgil paṅhwata janma liŋnya sĕḍĕṅanya karahatana riŋ pamañcanan*

mantuk dyaḥ hariṇī manĕmbaḥ i surendra ri wijila nikā madandana,
eñjiŋ maṅkat akañcuga adarupa bhūṣaṇa nika pinasaŋnya tūt hĕnū,
tan kwa ambĕknya lumampa lampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kasusu laku nika aṅhade hade,
denya adhaṙmma ri de nira aṅutus amighnanana tapa tatan hana aṅrwaṅi*

ṅūni n pamwit i jöŋ surendra mamĕgĕŋ taṅis inimuṙ-imuṙ kinölakĕn,
maṅke n sāmpun adoḥ lakunya wĕnaŋ aṅṅpasakĕna taṅisnya riŋ hawan,
lagy-a anambatakĕn laranya kasihan pati sĕsĕl anĕsĕl purākrĕta,
tūt māṙggāmbara luḥnya tan papĕgatan drawa kadi titis iŋ maṇik bañu*

kāṅĕn denya katuhwan iŋ giṇa mamighnani tapa wipatha agawe hala,
yadyastun kawaśā pira ŋ sukha tĕmun yan amuhara hala ndya don ikā,
mwaŋ yan tan kawaśā katon tĕtĕp i śāpa nira paṅawaśanya tan wuruŋ,
kodāsīnan ira ika ta pwa pinalaṙ palaṙ ika siha saŋ hyaŋ īśwara*

mampĕḥ mātra laranya luḥnya pinakembuḥ i manis i matanya yan wulat,
luṅsuṙ-luṅsuṙ ikaŋ tapiḥ pinakatambĕḥ i raras i tĕṅaḥ nika alaris,
hrĕknya alwan ya samaṙ-samaṙ tuna tuna amuwuhi manis i de nika aṅucap,
aśrī waṙṇna nika aṅĕliḥ wĕnĕs ika aṅhalĕpi kadi wĕnĕs niŋ abrata*

luṅhā lampaḥ ika anĕlat ri hirĕŋ iŋ gagana hanan awās hanan samar,
rĕp mukṣa anusup iŋ rĕmĕŋ kadi wulan lumaku kasaputan lamad-lamad,
lwiṙ wintaŋ sumurup katonan ika riŋ wĕkasan asĕmu maṙmmaka i kapö,
rĕm niŋ megha tinūtakĕnya manicip nicipi jawuḥ awaṙṇna cātaka*

rāmyanya n pamĕgat laṅit lĕpas adoḥ tĕka ri sadawatā nikaŋ limut,
agyā de ni panas hyaŋ aṙkka karaṇanya n alisuḥ atawĕŋ tawĕŋ hima,
prāpta ŋ truḥ sumaput prabhāwa ni lakunya wahu mari huyaŋnya kāṅinan,
tūt gaṅga ahawan indracāpa tumurun lari nika sukha mampiṙ iŋ wukir*

watw-a anuṅgul amaṙwwata ahrit aguha atupis atiba tiban latāṅkura,
ṅkā teka n dumunuŋ lukaṙ ni darupanya pinahayu lugas siniṅsĕtan,
tistis tan hana tīṙthayātra wiku śakty-atapa katĕmu śūnya kewala,
aṅhiŋ handiwa handiwa agarawalan katĕmu marĕk anuṅsuŋ iŋ guyu*

priṅga atyanta ruhuṙnya mānuṣa paran wĕnaṅa mara ri doḥnya duṙggama,
ṅhiŋ saŋ paṇḍita saŋ huwus tumĕmu ŋ aṣṭaguṇa sira wĕnaŋ mara irika,
hetu dyaḥ hariṇī wĕnaŋ mara kajanman ika saphala dewakanyakā,
lĕṙ denya n tumurun sawaŋ garagatī tumurun ahawan antiḥ antihan*

tiṅhalnya abayaṅan mamet i patapan saŋ atapa parananya bañcanan,
riŋ windhyācala ri indrakīla salĕbak wukiṙ ika pinaran katuṅkulan,
mwaŋ riŋ rewatakāgra gandhamadanādri masamun apa tan hana atapa,
hetunya n bhramita apĕga akuliliṅan kadi pakalaṅan iŋ niśākara*

lambuŋ niŋ himawān kidul hana ta paṙwwata śuci patapan hañaṙ katon,
tumraŋ teja nika prabhāwa nira saŋ sutapa tilaka niŋ jitendriya,
aṅlīla aṅililan pahoman ira söḥ kukus ika maṅadĕg nirantara,
lwīṙ oṅkāra mawindunāda kadi hĕnwa nira hĕlĕm anĕmwa śūnyatā*

buddhi dyaḥ hariṇī tumiṅhal irikaŋ patapan asĕmu haṙṣa niścaya,
byakta awās trĕṇawindu ta pwa makapājaran iki liŋ ika anĕhĕṙ marĕk,
līla aṅambaḥ i hambal iŋ jalada saŋsaya samaṙ asamun hibĕk jawuḥ,
miṅsoṙ lwīṙ ahawan turun turunan iŋ gupura sukha hanan kadi inulur*

prāpta iŋ paṙwwata śūnya kaywan ika pakṣa wukiṙ asĕgĕḥ iŋ hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ,
haryan mwaŋ hujuṅan saka iŋ pisaŋ alasnya rumarasaḥ amet kalālatā,
sakweḥ niŋ wulakan sumaṅgraha bañunya walahaṙ ika pakṣa sāgara,
jaṅga aṅambĕki pakṣa kasturi waṅinya hinaturakĕn iŋ drĕs iŋ barat*

wahw-a aron anak iŋ pakis haji katon sukĕt i pasusupanya duṙggama,
sakweḥ niŋ kayu nora tan pagati de niŋ anila tĕka riŋ trĕṇāṅkura,
ndan trāsa asĕpi tan paron kapanasan paḍa ragas amalaṙ malaṙ jawuḥ,
waṅkal seṅwan alīt-alīt bataŋ agöṅa hĕlĕm i paṅadĕgnya riŋ juraŋ*

lwiṙ tan pahyaŋ ikāŋ alas hana giraŋnya wahu linawad iŋ warāpsarī,
tapwan maṙmma dahat panuṅsuŋ ika kewala kusuma yayā maweḥ sukha,
lumra akweḥ tumiba iŋ gĕluŋ kadi tinap sawaŋ aṅit-aṅitan sĕkaṙ taji,
kady-a aṅĕmbaŋ akon aṅantya pakamaṅgala nika tanĕmĕn ya dewatī*

lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ talaga anamaṙ tasik anak tuna-tuna kawi nora maṅṅṅĕŋ,
paṅgaŋ wwadnya kakumbaḥ iŋ bañu suluṙnya wahu mĕtu satuṅtuŋ iŋ tanaḥ,
i groŋ-groŋ i pasiṙ-pasiṙnya mawatu dyan aniru-niru piṇḍa niŋ karas,
līla aṅanti darā putiḥnya kadi śaṅkha maduluṙ aṅurambat iŋ hĕnī*

ṅkā ta dyaḥ hariṇī mara adyus amĕḍaṙ tĕṅaḥ abuṅaḥ amawwahan gaḍiŋ,
māliḥ ṣaṭpada niŋ saroruha maliwran i wĕtis ika kesisan tapiḥ,
romanya awilĕtan mara i susu nika aniru niru rakĕt iŋ lumut-lumut,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ kumuda aṅliliṙ kadi tinaṅhi winulatan ika aṅdadak mĕkar*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ri sāmpun ika mĕntas aṅliga ligā kadi taman aśarīra dewatī,
titis-titis ikaŋ wĕhaŋ satitis iŋ bañu wulakan anumbĕṙ iŋ paras,
lumöŋ amiluluk gaḍiŋ kahudanan susu nika kasarambahan bañu,
sirat ni bañu niŋ gĕluŋ kinirab aṅhiribi kukus i sāri niŋ puḍak*

titis ni madhu niŋ madhubrata baṅun lĕṅa waṅi humaḍaŋ hana iŋ śilā,
pawitra hana tīṙtha niṙmmala sumaṅgraha ri harĕp awaṙṇna pahyasan,
hrĕbuk-hrĕbuk i kĕmbaŋ iŋ sarasija asĕmu hawu-hawu muṅgu riŋ cupu,
hirĕŋ ni kucup iŋ trikañcu sumĕlat kadi sipat awawan puḍak-puḍak*

lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kaṅelan apa tan tahu mahas-ahas iŋ wanāśrama,
sĕkaṙ niŋ asana amayuŋ kuniŋ apiṇḍa mamayuṅana kāla niŋ panas,
paḍa aṅrĕs atatā ŋ wuluḥ kadi harĕp tĕkĕnakĕna tan intaṙ aṅhaḍaŋ,
gaḍuŋ kadi kamāsihĕn paḍa lumuŋ baṅun aharĕp anuntuna iŋ hĕnū*

huwus tĕka riŋ āśrama aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ry-ulaha nika mĕne n panĕmbaha,
nĕhĕṙ lumaku muṅgaḥ iŋ gupura saṅśaya manaha nahā mara i dalĕm,
aluṅguḥ irikaŋ bukuṙ paṅaraṅanya nĕhĕṙ asidĕha aṅure gĕluŋ,
cĕcĕk masahuran saka i wuri pinakpak ika pinakadūta niŋ hala*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

bhagawān trĕṇawindu sĕḍĕŋ ajapa nitya śiwasmaraṇa,
asamādhi kumöl katĕmu hĕniŋ i buddhi nira n humĕnĕŋ,
dwija śukla suśīla sira pinakadaṙśśana riŋ patapan,
kadi wꜽṣṇawawimba pawulatan ira n pamutĕṙ guduha*

i rare nira ṅūni hati nira hibĕk sukĕt aṅrahabi,
inĕnö ni rajaḥ tamaḥ ira karaṇanya n aron asĕwö,
atuha pwa sira wruḥ aṅaji guṇa niŋ guru nora kari,
hana sattwaguṇa amaṅani sukĕt i buddhi nira n patapa*

wijaya iŋ patapan dwijawara makasādhana yoga nira,
anukūla ri jöŋ nira sahana niŋ indriya nora wani,
aṇimā laghimādi kakaratala de ni samādhi nira,
kamumukṣuhan aṅhaḍa marĕk akĕliṙ swaśarīra nira*

ri huwus ni samādhi nira linĕsu rakwa harĕp mijila,
anĕlat rarab iŋ rĕrĕb aṅuraṅi tan panĕlĕs harĕpan,
larap iŋ kilat iŋ gagana kadi dinĕmwan aganti lumöŋ,
paṅapö ni gĕrĕḥnya kadi mamisiki n hana wāhu ḍatĕŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

mijil muniwara ahawan hĕniŋ i buddhi nira laku nira aṅhade-hade,
pijĕṙ mulat i posik iŋ jaladhi rāmya tĕpi nika katuṅku tuṅkulan,
ri tiṅhal ira riŋ bukuṙ saŋ araras winulatan ira maṅligā ligā,
ya kāraṇa nira n para agarawalan saŋ ahayu tumuluy-madan tapiḥ*

saŋ ugratapa niṙwikāra tamuyan wĕkas iŋ ahayu riŋ kadewatan,
salaḥ sĕmu manis-manis nira baṅun manis iŋ anĕmu mitra riŋ hĕnū,
dudū sukha nira n mulat paḍa lawan sukha niŋ atamuyan kadaŋ-kadaŋ,
ikaŋ turida rāga sāmpun amatĕḥ milu-milu mamiratyakĕn manaḥ*

aniṅsĕti hĕniŋ ni buddhi nira śuddha ni basahan ira n siniṅsĕtan,
subaddha daluwaŋ siṅī pinakabaddha nira pamadha riŋ rajaḥ tamaḥ,
samaṙ tura turaḥ ni bhasma nira paṅgĕsĕŋ ira wiṣaya atĕmaḥ hawu,
jamaŋ kadi mahā taraṅtaṅĕn i sampĕt ira huwus anampĕti indriya*

marĕk sira sulakṣaṇa adara maṅakṣama kamĕna nira n paluṅguha,
katon upaśama atalaṅkup aṅagĕm kayu kanaka supattralepana,
tamuy-nira masewa dhaṙmma pakatonan i manaḥ ika bhakti kewala,
prasiddha guru śiṣya rūpa nira kāliḥ i papupul ira irikaŋ bukur*

anĕmbaḥ ikaŋ apsarī mĕtu rarasnya tan asarag aṅambĕk ambĕki,
lĕmĕs ni luṅayanya kāliḥ ajajaṙ kadi pĕpĕsa kahambĕŋ iŋ susu,
laris ni jarijinya sāmpun atalaṅkup inayat inamĕṙ mara iŋ mukha,
amatyakĕn i raśmi-raśmi ni liriŋnya n api miṅay-aṅīrakĕn wulat*

lana aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt dwijeśwara tumon hayu nika winiweka riŋ hati,
tulis kanaka wahw-inuṅkaban aṅāśraya ri buṅaḥ ika n pabhūṣaṇa,
ahadyan ahĕnĕŋ nĕhĕṙ masidĕha asĕmu taruban i kāla niŋ gawe,
yadin haliwata iŋ sabhā tan alaraŋ halĕpakĕna maḍampa mās tatur*

sinaṅśaya nira aluma aluñuta madhya nika kulayĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,
suśūnya winaliŋ nira imwa gamĕlĕn ri kahiḍĕpan ika uṇḍuḥ oṇḍuhan,
wĕtisnya kadi maṙwwi maṅgarita paṅkwakĕna kahiḍĕpanya de nira,
mukhanya gumawaŋ ya rakwa tinaha alwaṅa hilaṅa ri kāla niŋ tilĕm*

hyaŋ iŋ nagara kālasan pawulatanya n anuruni rikaŋ wanāśrama,
madhubrata baṅun pinañjiṅan ika aṅidĕri salaga mĕtta riŋ sĕkar,
puḍak kadi panĕmpa nĕmpahan ika asĕmu maniliha lambay-iŋ ṭikā,
amānuṣa hayunya kenaka nika amulaṅunakĕna riŋ jitendriya*

kayogyan iŋ apiṇḍa ratna liniṅiṙ saparana nika ta pwa hĕmbanĕn,
hade kumĕḍapa n wulat yan aṅadĕg tĕhĕṙ aṅadĕga tan paluṅguha,
yadin lukara kenya tan wruḥ amahaywa kahalĕp ika denya n aṅligā,
sawaŋ-sawaŋ iŋ aṅhĕmū guyu kapantĕs ika pamapaganya riŋ wulat*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

Āścaṙyya buddhi bhagawān trĕṇawindu denya,
ndātan hana hyun ira mātra sumöṅa riŋ twas,
kewalya susthira manaḥ nira tan prapañca,
maswāgata amanis ujaṙ nira sāṙjjawa atwaŋ*

rakryan kṣamākĕna kami ibu paran kita ari,
strī tan wruḥ iŋ bhaya ri duṙggama niŋ wanādri,
aṅhiŋ katon kita wĕnaŋ mara niṙwikāra,
prāpta aṅĕnĕs maniluman baṅun indrajāla*

Āsĕṅka ni ṅhulun i māsku tĕkanta maṅko,
strī niŋ wiśeṣapuruṣa prabhu cakrawaṙtti,
tan saḥ kinuṇḍaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ niŋ aburwa burwan,
ndā ṅke n katĕmwa samayanta lawan priyanta*

strī tan padhaṙmma ta kunaŋ kita kāri śoka,
swāminta tan pahamĕṅan kawi tan pawastha,
ambĕkta wikwa manusup nusupa iŋ alas göŋ,
sambin hiḍĕpta wulikĕn palarĕn katĕmwa*

anwam kunaŋ kita katuṅhapan iŋ bapebu,
muṅgw-iŋ kadaŋ maṅupapīra maweḥ lara ambĕk,
māṙgganta lampus aṅusiṙ wanadeśa śūnya,
ahyun lumakwa wiku kilya rarā wiratya*

hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ āśrama kunaŋ kita diwyacakṣuḥ,
wruḥ riŋ jitendriya sadābrata tan kĕna iŋ strī,
buddhinta mogha mawĕlas mulat iŋ daridra,
prāpta anurun paran ikā paṅanugrahanta*

rakryan hiḍĕpku ri hayunta saka iŋ wanādri,
ambĕt ni sinwam iŋ aśoka mara i tĕṅaḥta,
molaḥ kadi inĕluk ĕluk luŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ mrik,
tan saḥ katon i luṅayanta lĕmĕs lĕmĕsnya*

amraŋ baŋ iŋ katiraḥ aṙjja hana i laṭinta,
tuñjuŋ birū mĕkaṙ alurw-akusū sugandha,
māliḥ lurunya mamanis kawawa i matanta,
mimba amarāśraya tikĕlnya hana i halista*

polaḥ nikaŋ kusumasāri hana i wiwalta,
maṅgiṣṭa wāhu rinĕmĕk tumiba i kĕcapta,
paṅhrĕŋ nikaŋ bhramara muṅgw-i taṅis taṅista,
hīs niŋ tusāra rumarab makajanma luḥta*

sandeha buddhi mami de ni halĕpta māsku,
dūra n manuṣya kita kewala dewaputrī,
de niŋ manaṙkka ri ḍatĕṅta mahāprabhāwa,
saṅka i hyaŋ indra mapa donta waraḥ kami ibu*

nāhan panaṙkka nira maṙmma dahat rasanya,
mambö tilam kadi huwus wruḥ i rumrum iŋ strī,
śrĕṅgāra dewaduhitā kawĕlad hatinya,
maṅgĕḥ ri buddhi bhagawān kĕna bañcananya*

<akrĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

suraputrikā sumahuṙ ādara mulat awiraŋ tumuṅkul anaṅis,
bhagawān rĕṅön pawaraḥ i ṅhulun aṅusiṙ aṅāśraya i kadi kita,
taha tan saka i surapati n ḍatĕŋ aṅĕnĕs amet pradeśa wĕgilĕn,
mwaŋ asambhawa n hyaṅa niŋ āśrama panaha nahā dwijeśwara hade*

tuwi tan manuṣya maniwi prabhu maduluṙ aburwa-burwa riŋ alas,
hayu ni ṅhulun taha tan antuk iŋ aṅalap alap saka iŋ giriwana,
riŋ apa n rara aharĕpa wikwa manusupa manĕmbaha iŋ wiku talun,
pisaniṅw-ajalwa kawi mūṙcchita layat alaṅö manambaŋ anadin*

bhagawān manĕḥta huniṅan humulunakĕn awaknya tan patĕbusan,
tuwi hetu niŋ mara ri jöŋ dwija taruṇa bhaṭāra dhaṙmma maṅutus,
i ratĕŋ nikaŋ brata samādhi kakawaśa tĕkapta sāmpun amatĕḥ,
mĕtu tan pasaṅkan inucap wulatana tariman ṅhulun phala nika*

hyaṅĕn i ṅhulun ri pada saŋ dwija taruṇa kaśuddhyana utus utusĕn,
pisanīṅw-anĕṅgaha mĕne n pasuruhana sĕkaṙ lawan bañu damu,
marĕka iŋ paturwan aṅisapwakĕna suku munīndra riŋ pakasutan,
tan asambhawa n hulun anaṅhuluna yan apuyĕŋ dwijaṙṣi majapa*

arĕnaḥ tĕkapnya n aṅucap kama riŋ ujaṙ amighnani brata tapa,
mata mesi luḥ saha taṅis winulatakĕn ikā wineḥ amanisa,
ajajaṙ pasaṅgraha nikā susu waṅi ni pipinya lāgi sumaji,
kadi pādapa aṅliḥ alaris tĕṅaḥ ika pasĕnāha ri dwijawara*

umĕnĕŋ dwijaṙṣi rumase wacana nika tĕkā waśa aṅhamu-hamu,
smaradūta kewala manisnya n aṅucap ataṅis lana amĕlas arĕp,
wĕkasan dwijendra wihikan ry-abhimata nika yan pamighnani tapa,
mĕtu kadwijātyan ira nora kawĕdi nira sāhasa anapathani*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

aḍā wipatha ko pakojaṙ iku dhūṙtta tan aharĕp i haywa niŋ tapa,
huwus wruḥ aku yan pakona suranātha karaṇamu ḍatĕŋ mamañcana,
ikaŋ hala gawemu tan wuruŋ amaṅsulana malĕsana iri ko mĕne,
manuṣya tĕmahamwa tan waluya riŋ surapada wĕkasamwa dewatī*

yadin śatasahasrabhāgan i sukhaṅku n ataki taki niṣparigraha,
tathāpi kapana n samaṅkana sukhaṅkwa k aṅusira sukha iŋ surālaya,
hana pwa sukha niŋ manuṣya masamāgama mapa ta gawe nika adhama,
lĕhĕŋ juga ŋ anĕmwa pātaka saka iŋ katuduhana kabañcana atapa*

nahan liŋ ira sāhasa aṅḍawuhi śāpa nĕhĕṙ anudiṅi i kiwa aṅdĕlö,
prapañca surakanyakā kahilaṅan hurip apĕga ri tan siḥ iŋ widhi,
ri doṣa nika rāga-rāga n aṅusiṙ sutapa pisaniṅūn kabañcana,
alum kadi gaḍuŋ pinuṅgĕl aṅayuḥ sĕkaṙ iŋ asana tan wuruŋ pĕjaḥ*

tumuṅkul i harĕp dwijaṙṣi makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ nira,
hanan kadi waśa aṅdĕlö nĕhĕṙ aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ surālaya,
mĕhāḥ salahasa atĕpak jaja manĕmbaḥ aḍĕkuḥ amalaṙ kasanmata,
apan harĕp iŋ antaśāpa karaṇanya n aṅucap amanis maṅañjali*

dwijaṙṣi huripĕn ṅhulun titisana amrĕta waluyakĕna iŋ kadewatan,
Ĕmās maṇik anekawastu kĕta ŋ enaka panĕbusa ni ṅhulun hurip,
ṅhulun pwa kasihan muwaḥ syapa pametana pirak i rikaŋ tapowana,
mataŋnya k anaṅis panĕmbaha ri jöṅta panĕbusa ri jīwa ni ṅhulun*

tuhanku bhagawānku hāḥ sipi lalista wulatana manĕḥta kāsy-asiḥ,
harĕp muliha tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ aṅantya ri kita-kita melik i ṅhulun,
unĕŋ niŋ abapebu tiṅhalana denta mapa karika hetu niŋ hĕnĕŋ,
kĕdö harĕp anona māti kĕna śāpa karika kita tan wruḥ iŋ wĕlas*

ahā mpu wihikan ṅhulun ri wuyuṅanta kalalarana śuddha niŋ tapa,
kṣamākĕna manĕḥta tan tugĕtananta sakasalaḥ i śīla ni ṅhulun,
prasiddha kita paṇḍita anumata riŋ wiguṇa wipatha tan wruḥ iŋ krama,
si sĕmbaḥ ika jampya niŋ kadi kita n lumĕkasa wuyuŋ iŋ kadi ṅhulun*

kucup niŋ asana aluru ndan amalaṙ karirisana ri taṅgal iŋ kapat,
gaḍuŋ lumay-aṅolakĕn tawaŋ aluṅluṅan amalaṙ anĕmwa rambatan,
hĕlaŋ midĕṙ anambayaŋ saha taṅis kapanasan amalaṙ drĕs iŋ jawuḥ,
ṅhulun pwa kalaran mataŋnya k amalaṙ turunana wara de dwijeśwara*

ahā pahalawö ta koŋ awakana ŋ kapalaŋ-alaŋ i demu n apsarī,
kadaŋ kadaṅa de bapebu pĕkulĕmwa paḍa kari sira iŋ kadewatan,
pĕjaḥ ṅaran iki syapa ika ta-taṅis taṅisana mulata asiha iri ko,
wĕlasku ri hayunya sis mapa tikī hamĕṅana niki yan pĕjaḥ mĕne*

bhaṭāra suranātha tiṅhalana de nrĕpati kasiḥ arĕp patik haji,
huwus kalĕmahan śināpa kapana n maluya muwaḥ i pāda saŋ prabhu,
hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥ surādhipati tan wuruṅa pĕjaha riŋ pamañcanan,
riŋ āśrama wĕkas ni jīwita patik haji wiphala pakon surādhipa*

prabhu-prabhu rĕṅön taṅis ni hariṇī kapĕgan aputĕk aṅhiḍĕp lara,
pĕjaḥ pinatiwaṙ kinonakĕn i tan kawĕnaŋ ika gawe dinohakĕn,
ikaŋ gati śināpa sis ya katahā ya katĕmu tuluṅĕn patik haji,
pati pwa balik iŋ hurip lara lalis pwa balika ni wĕlas surādhipa*

wijil sahana saŋ hyaŋ iŋ kusuma wāhu sumalaga nihan lawad ṅhulun,
hurip gĕlisa ni ṅhulun ya palakunta ri yatiwara haywa ta asuwe,
kunaŋ yan agĕgĕḥ dwijaṙṣi palalun sawuyuŋ ira sadenya saṅkulĕn,
tuhun kita lumĕṇḍwa lĕṇḍwa ri śawaṅku gĕsĕṅĕn i pañaṇḍi niŋ wuṅū*

manis ni mata ni ṅhulun labuhĕn iŋ jaladhi luḥ irikaŋ tasik madhu,
raras ni waja ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ śrigaḍiŋ i pucak iŋ gunuŋ gula,
lĕmĕs ni lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun lĕpasĕn iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅĕliḥ aṅolakĕn tawaŋ,
laris ni wĕtis i ṅhulun kĕkĕsananta kĕmitana ni dèwa niŋ puḍak*

kĕlab ni tapiḥ i ṅhulun suji ya teki pupulakĕn i posik iŋ sĕkar,
pataṅkis i giriṅsiŋ i ṅhulun aṅantya ri lĕṅĕŋ i kiriñciŋ-iŋ bañu,
pĕnĕd ni laku ni ṅhulun tan asarag waluyakĕna ri lampaḥ iŋ liman,
pĕpö ni panaṅisku tan kahuniṅā ḍawuhakĕna ri śabda niŋ cucur*

ameta maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kita pamorana ni kusut i roma ni ṅhulun,
ri mimba ni taman ta paṅṅpasananta ri rĕṅu ni halisku yan tikĕl,
gĕmuḥ ni susu ni ṅhulun wahu mijil tuhañaṅakĕna riŋ pucaŋ gaḍiŋ,
wĕnĕs ni mukha ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ wulan inĕmukan iŋ lamad-lamad*

pamādapa ni madhya ni ṅhulun aros kirimakĕn iŋ aśokapādapa,
Ĕbun hana ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ trĕṇalatāṅkura patuwawana i luḥ i ṅhulun,
lawan pañuriga inunus ni paṅawakku rakĕtakĕna denta riŋ tulis,
luṅid ni kuku ni ṅhulun turuŋ aṅanya ri jaja-jajaṙ iŋ sĕkaṙ taji*

nahan śruti ni de nika anaṅis atuṅtuŋ ucapan amĕlas mĕlas harĕp,
samasta para dèwa sūkṣma humĕnĕŋ tinaṅisan ika tan hana aṅlawad,
arĕs hawa hawākĕna awĕdi kumöl wruḥ i gĕgĕḥ i wuyuŋ dwijeśwara,
paḍa aṅrĕs anaṅis naṅis taṅis ikā piniturun ika muṅgu riŋ waneḥ*

taṅis-taṅis i dèwa niŋ kusuma sūkṣma tinaṅisakĕn iŋ madhubrata,
taṅis niŋ amarāśraya iŋ wulan awā tinaṅisakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur,
taṅis-taṅis i dèwa niŋ jalada cātaka manaṅisakĕn hana iŋ tawaŋ,
taṅis-taṅis i dèwa niŋ masa kapat tinaṅisakĕn i gĕntĕṙ iŋ patĕr*

muwaḥ dyaḥ anu mojaṙ asrĕt ucapanya tuna-tuna sinambaṅan taṅis,
mpu ḍaŋ hyaŋ apa tāḥ inanti ni manĕḥta paṅuṣadha ri duhkha ni ṅhulun,
yatan hana hineṙ manĕḥ dwijawara asiha humuripana ṅhuwus pĕjaḥ,
kṣamākĕna magöŋ ṅhulun mpu warahĕn duga-duga mara tan harĕp-harĕp*

nahan rasa ni de nika anaṅis aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ kadewatan,
udhāni bhagawān paṅawruhana de nira mulat amanis wawaŋ lipur,
apuy-siniram iŋ jawuḥ paḍa ni suṅsut ira tan agĕgĕḥ wawaŋ paḍĕm,
sĕrĕḥ waṅi lawan duḥ iŋ wwaḥ aramĕs ri waja paḍa ni de nira aṅucap*

paran karika tan sihaṅkwa ri kita anaku kita karika apan uttama,
manuṣya tuwi sāwakanya yan atön mara-mara hiniḍĕp kadaŋ-kadaŋ,
kunaŋ saŋ agawe laranta paramāṙtha nira sira bhaṭāra śaṅkara,
lukat ni kapalaŋ nikaŋ sukrĕta māṙgga ni kapalaŋ i denta dewatī*

priyanta riŋ anādijanma dadi mānuṣa lituhayu sūṙyyawaṅśaja,
narendra raghu rakwa mānak aniru prakaśita subhaga iŋ purāntara,
apañjy-aja dhanuṙddhara anwam isi niŋ raghunagara turuŋ smarātura,
tuhun kita dine bhaṭāra yugalanya muwaḥ akurĕna asiha i kita*

kunaŋ pwa siha ni ṅhulun ri kita tan kalawasana dadinta mānuṣa,
aṅālihana kaprabhun kita lawan saŋ aja sukha sarājya tuṅgalĕn,
tuhun pamĕkasanta wīja sawiji irika kita maluya iŋ kadewatan,
sĕkaṙ sumanasa antakanta ya tika amĕgatakĕna ri śāpa ni ṅhulun*

huwus pwa kita mantuk iŋ surapada anaku katĕka tĕka iŋ wwaluŋ tahun,
samaṅkana narendra saŋ kawĕkas iŋ nagara muliha riŋ kadewatan,
apaṅgiha muwaḥ lawan kita tumĕmwakĕna phala nikaŋ kadigjayan,
mataŋnya pahayun manaḥta sukhamāṙgga matĕmahana rājaputrikā*

nahan rasa ni de nira amĕgati śāpa nira tĕhĕṙ ajaṙ satorasiḥ,
ri mūla ni dadinya len tĕmahananya tinalataḥ ira agalaṙ taṅan,
kunaŋ pwa wĕkasan hiḍĕpnya ri kaśāpa nika kadi wineḥ anugraha,
unĕŋnya matĕmaḥ luḥ adrĕs i kapö lara turida nika atĕmaḥ taṅis*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

hāḥ saŋ mukṣa ri luḥku tan pahamĕṅan namu-namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pasaṅgaman,
maṅke pwa ambĕka niŋ prahāsana bisa aṅhari hariḥ iŋ arĕs pinaṅkwakĕn,
ṅūni n hyaŋ kita riŋ surālaya manĕḥta milu matĕmahan warāpsarī,
maṅke pwa aṅdadi rājaputra kita heṙ ṅhulun atĕmaha rājaputrikā*

hāḥ swāmiṅku dudut ṅhulun ri juraŋ iŋ lĕpihan alal aṅölakĕn laṅö,
hĕmban riŋ wwat aśokapādapa tĕṅaḥku pagamĕlana luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
suṅsuŋ riŋ maṅunĕŋ galuḥ lulut unĕṅku ri kita kaka tan wĕnaŋ kinas,
riŋ paṇḍan haḍaṅĕn ṅhulun lumaku śoka laku-laku ṭika ahawan puḍak*

nāhan ṅrĕs-ṅrĕs i samba-sambat ika kāsihan alal apasaḥ lawan priya,
tan siḥ niŋ widhi mogha tan patuluṅan karaṇa nika manĕmwakĕn lara,
de niŋ gyānya tumĕmwa janma saŋ aniṅgalakĕn iriya riŋ kadewatan,
amwit matya manĕmbaḥ iŋ dwijawara anĕhĕṙ aṅusapi luḥnya riŋ sabuk*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

huwus praṇata bhakti tan paśaraṇāśraya mati lumaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,
humuŋ taṅis i sundarī nikaŋ alas hinariwuwu ni śabda niŋ gaguŋ,
rĕrĕb kusumasāri tan papĕgatan kĕtug i tĕḍun iŋ eṙttali iŋ juraŋ,
luŋ iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅindracāpa humaḍaŋ hawana nika madadya mānuṣa*

hyaŋ agni hana riŋ śarīra mijil aṅgĕsĕṅi śawa nika agilaŋ-gilaŋ,
kasiddhyan ira saŋ dwijaṙṣi gumawe dilaḥ ika karaṇanya n ujwala,
bukuṙ pamiḍaran ndatan milu gĕsĕŋ kadi jalada rinĕṅgan iŋ kilat,
samantaji paḍĕm tuhun hana kukusnya kari sakukus iŋ damaṙ pĕjaḥ*

hayunya milu bhasmibhūta tĕka riŋ gĕluŋ ahawuk amiṇḍa riŋ kukus,
lumöŋ wa nikaŋ asthi mātra kadi śeṣa ni luru ni matanya yan wulat,
baṅun tura turaḥ nikaŋ sipat ikaŋ latu-latu tumibā paḍa ahirĕŋ,
hilaŋ siniriṙ iŋ samīraṇa hawunya tumuluy-anarīra riŋ hrĕbuk*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ hyaŋ niŋ suraloka tan pahamĕṅan namu-namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,
sūkṣma aṅjanma mara iŋ widaṙbbhanagarī sira ta pinakasāri niŋ sarāt,
putrī śrī krathakeśikeśwara nĕhĕṙ hayu nira kadi ṅūni n apsarī,
khyāti śri indumatī panaṅgaḥ i sira n pamukha kadi śaśaṅka pūṙṇnama*

lwīṙ iŋ swapna wijil nira adbhuta karĕṅwan i wali nira riŋ kadewatan,
rĕmrĕm taŋ daśadeśa de ni sahab iŋ jaladakusuma muṅgu riŋ tawaŋ,
lĕŋlĕŋ de ni gĕrĕḥnya ṣaṭpada maliwran apupul irikaŋ limut hrĕbuk,
sumyuk taŋ madhupuṣpawaṙṣa maduluṙ jaya-jaya ri jayā nrĕpātmajā*

ṅūni n tuṅgal anak nareśwara lawö manaḥ ira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā,
ndātan pembuḥ ikaŋ sukha i sira baṅun bañu humidĕŋ aṅanti riŋ ranu,
maṅke n pembuḥ anak nira ahayu sinambhawa maṅadĕha lakṣmi niŋ purī,
embuḥ göŋ kadi sāgara rwab amĕpĕk sukha nira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā*

rakryan saŋ pinakeña rakwa kulawaṅśa wĕka-wĕka kadaŋ-kadaŋ haji,
aśrī waṙṇna nira araras kadi saroja kinĕlabakĕn iŋ ṙyyak iŋ bañu,
de niŋ mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki sabhāwa nira tĕka hirĕŋ kineriṅan,
suswan bāhwan agasyak aṅhalĕpakĕn wruḥ iŋ aṅinakana i tuhan-tuhan*

lāwan towi nira ahalĕp marĕka hadyana kunaŋ asawaŋ priyambada,
ndan paṙṇnaḥ kaka de nira iña nira kaṙwwa sira paḍa suśīla wīṙyyawan,
kāliḥ-kāliḥ ira aṅharis haris anuswani rahina wĕṅi i suputrikā,
saṅka iŋ swaṙgga hulun tuha aṅgĕḥ ira ṅūni ri hana nira riŋ kadewatan*

wwaŋ ri jro juru niŋ mĕṅĕs pinarĕk iŋ wagĕd amirit i hatwik iŋ manis,
sakwan selwan atūt manaḥnya kalawan kabayan iŋ arĕja iŋ kaguṇḍikan,
tuṅgal riŋ katĕkāsihan lawan ikaŋ pinuji pinakagusti riŋ raras,
rūm rakryan nrĕpaputrikā mawa hayunya tuhu ratu ni raśmi niŋ prajā*

strī māwak caturaṅga sabhya tan athāni panagara tĕka ahawan ratha,
prāya apāmbĕkan aśwasañcari lakunya wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ liman,
nistanya n wiparīta rūpa nika tan kasaḥ i pada narendraputrikā,
himpĕṙ peka minantryakĕn huwus abhūṣaṇa hinalĕpakĕn yaya ahala*

rakryan rājasuta anwam eṅgal atuha aṅiṅĕt iṅĕtakĕn aṅdĕlö tawaŋ,
aṅliṅliŋ kinahaṙṣan iŋ kaka  kaka amwaṅi sira rinĕbut pinaṅkwakĕn,
kahyun-hyun kumurĕb kurĕb kumĕdal asriŋ aniru-niru putra niŋ pĕñu,
wahw-a ahuntw-aputiḥ katon sĕḍĕŋ ira asĕmu guyu baṅun aṅhĕmū mĕnur*

solaḥ bhāwa nira amaṅun siḥ aṅĕwaḥ bapa-bapa juga de nira aṅucap,
yan paṅjaṅkaḥ aṅaṅguḥ aṅguhi gumoḥ lumaris asĕmu lĕmbu kanyakā,
moga ahyaŋ sira yan maluṅguḥ ararĕm tumiru tiru paluṅguḥ iŋ gaṇa,
yan sore mulat iŋ wulan wruḥ awawā wulan anuduhi wimba niŋ wulan*

endaḥ buddhi nikaŋ waneḥ mamitaṅis-mitaṅis i sira haṙṣa riŋ taṅis,
eṅgal mary-anaṅis pinakpak amanis wulat ira sinawe pinaṅkwakĕn,
len tekaŋ harĕp iŋ hala ahala halan mamalaku hala hāsyakāraṇa,
maṅkin tībra raras narendratanaya ahayu ri huwus ira n paweḥ ala*

anwam tapwan apa asarik hayu nira an inaṅĕtan apupuk ri wunbunan,
tan paṅde hala tambĕḥ iŋ hayu bajaŋ-bajaŋ ira mata niŋ lawak bulu,
pantĕs yan pagĕlaŋ lawe wĕnaŋ i kāla nira kapĕjahan rare bajaŋ,
tambā niŋ sĕgu tuṅtuŋ iŋ sĕrĕḥ aṅimbuhi manis ira yan hana i rahi*

ndi nyū danta paḍā mĕne n lĕwiha yan marĕk i sira sĕḍĕŋ pinaṅkwakĕn,
lāwan ketaka dūra n aṅhiriba nista nika n inuparĕṅgan iŋ ṭikā,
sakweḥ niŋ kusuma awĕnĕs pinakataṇḍiŋ ira wawaŋ alum saka iŋ taṅan,
maṅgĕḥ de niŋ anuswani i sira dudū lawan anak anakan sinuswakĕn*

eṅgal wruḥ tinitaḥ bisa ataratayan wĕgig aṅadĕg adĕg wawaŋ tibā,
guywan wruḥ makukuk bayan tinañakĕn kahanan ira bisa atukup mata,
sora isuk malĕbū lĕbū cala kinon ahuwusana ya saṅkan iŋ taṅis,
haṙṣa anon gigirĕn sira aṅgyat anĕpak bisu-bisu nĕhĕṙ aṅgigiṙ gigir*

dudw-aṅkĕn wĕṅi de nira n wruḥ aṅucap mari bisu-bisu saŋsaya abĕnĕr,
sāmpun rakwa sira apupak pinakapūṙwwaka nira n aṅaji i munīśwara,
prajña wruḥ ri kalīṅa niŋ pada kadi wruḥ alawas anulus wicakṣaṇa,
eṅgal pathya ri kaprayogan i rusit niŋ aji kadi tĕmaḥ saraswatī*

umwat śīghra tuwuḥ nira ahayu sawaŋ salaga niŋ asana aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
tapwan wruḥ riŋ iraŋ dahat kalukaran tapiḥ awuda wuda agĕlaŋ-gĕlaŋ,
tan pendaḥ lĕṅĕŋ iŋ wuluḥ gaḍiŋ i kāla ni pamilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mambĕt madhya nira awĕlū buṅaḥ i waṙṇna nika kadi giliŋ-giliŋ kuñit*

niṙwā tan paguṇa ŋ pupuṙ pinakapahyas ira tĕwas aweḥ kram iŋ mukha,
dūra aṅhaywana tan padon sipat ira aṅṅtuhi ri hĕniŋ-iŋ mata abiru,
lāwan taŋ paṅĕluk lĕṅĕn wiphala yeka karaṇa ni halis nira n tikĕl,
wyaṙtha aŋ tūlahana anukĕṙ nukĕri tan wuruŋ amaṅunakĕn srĕt iŋ susu*

sumraŋ sraŋ mata wahw-atön ri lĕṅĕŋ iŋ gĕrĕḥ aṅirim irim lawan riris,
aṅlūd ry-ambĕk ira n rimaŋ taṅis ikaŋ bhramara kalilipĕn saḍĕk hrĕbuk,
yan sore ri huwus nira ahawu-hawu wruḥ amawa kalaṅön ira iŋ natar,
aṅhĕmban karas esi bhāṣa pinakānak anakan ira tan saḥ iŋ tanaḥ*

piṇḍa dwādaśawaṙṣa kāla ni wijil nira rumara rara n hana i dalĕm,
yan paṅhyas hyasi mogha tan kawanĕhan tiniru tiru sade nira aṅhyasi,
sotan ta ṅhyaŋ iŋ indraloka kapana n tan apĕnĕda tĕmaḥnya mānuṣa,
lakṣmī niŋ nagara ahulap mulat i rūpa nira n ahayu katwaŋ iŋ tulis*

miṅkil tapwan agöŋ payodhara nira aṅṅwihi buṅaḥ i tuṅtuŋ iŋ gaḍiŋ,
hyaŋ hiŋ tāman aṅiṇḍarat sĕmu ni rūpa nira n ahayu muṅgu riŋ taman,
tistis lālana tan hana aṅiriṅakĕn laku nira kadi tan tuhan-tuhan,
molaḥ sumpiŋ ira asana alum awĕnĕs baṅun awĕdi ri luñcip iŋ mata*

paṅrāt niŋ kalaṅön tinurwakĕn ira iŋ watu karaŋ aṅilo wway-iŋ ranu,
tan śobhā humiriŋ lumaḥ makakaraŋ hulu lĕṅĕn ira mūṙcchita aṅligā,
paṇḍan raṅkaŋ aṅöbi tan panisi mātra ri sira n apulaŋ lawan hrĕbuk,
amrĕm kaṙwwa karas lĕṅĕŋ kadi ṭikā piniturun inamĕṙ saka iŋ puḍak*

maṅkin maṙmma narendra māsiḥ anĕkāni samaṅinakana i manaḥ nira,
buddhi śrī parameśwarī sukha makānak i sira samanaḥ nira inariḥ,
maṅke n tan hana wahw-atakwan ahiḍĕp nrĕpati tĕka sira aṅhĕmū guyu,
maṅgĕḥ buddhi nira ajajaṙ lawan anak nira baṅun aṅabehi jīwita*

saŋ bhoja anak ira atuha apagĕḥ ikaŋ guṇa ri sira paṅawruḥ iŋ ratu,
sākṣāt prāṇawa Īśwara nrĕpati kāsiḥ ira sira suśīla nītimān,
aṅhiŋ rakwa pakö nareśwara ri bhūmi nira sira sadā janapriya,
maṅgĕḥ rowaŋ ira aṅadĕg ri hiḍĕp iŋ mulat i sukha nira n paḍa apagĕḥ*

ndan griŋ saŋ prabhu saŋsaya abwat atĕlĕb maṅinak inaki tan tulus waras,
tĕṅrān iŋ hurip iŋ śarīra paḍa rūkṣa mawaraḥ i tĕkā nikaŋ pati,
yekā hetu nira aṅutus marĕka riŋ dwijawara rĕṣi śꜽwa sogata,
mwaŋ mantrī winĕkas wĕkas nira n anak nira sumiliha ratwa haywa len*

sakweḥ saŋ winĕkas wĕkas paḍa tĕñuḥ twas ira kahĕnĕṅan mulat juga,
de niŋ duhkha tumon i kāsy-asiḥ i saŋ kawĕkas ira dumeḥ sira asiha,
mojaṙ mātra pĕgat-pĕgat wĕkasan amriḥ asayut amĕlas-mĕlas harĕp,
luḥ lāwan sĕkĕl iŋ taṅis duluṙ i de nira sumahuṙ i śabda saŋ prabhu*

he nāthaṅku huwus kapaṅku wacana nrĕpati rasa nira awĕkas wĕkas,
an saŋ bhoja gumantya ratwakĕna yadyapi pĕjaha mĕne nareśwara,
ndan lwiṙ wyaṙtha ḍawuḥ ni śabda naranātha ri sama marĕk aṅlawad-lawad,
Āpan ṅhiŋ sira keṅĕ keṅĕt alawas kumalilirana kaprabhun haji*

śaktin de naranātha haywa lĕsu saŋ prabhu tahapana wedya kinkinĕn,
śrī dewi indumatī katoliha katon uwuḥ uwuha nira n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ bhoja sira anwam aṙddha kapalaŋ wĕkasakĕna narendra riŋ prajā,
ndān amriḥ mriha saŋ prabhu syapa parāśrayana sama marĕk mĕne n kari*

nāhan liŋ sama maṅlawad lawad i saŋ prabhu lara nira membuḥ aṅlare,
wahw-a aṅlumpuhi saŋsaya amaṅĕti roga nira wawaŋ alum sira awĕnĕs,
tan polaḥ sira tan kĕḍap ṅuni-ṅuni n paṅucapa sira kewala aturū,
ṅhiŋ maṅguḥ kalawan miṅĕl sahuṙ ira n tinaña tañan i de nira alara*

satya śrī parameśwarī tan awĕdi iŋ pati tumuta ri līna saŋ prabhu,
ndan dewi indumatī tinoliḥ ira kāsy-asiha nira mĕne n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ bhoja paḍa anwam anwam anaṅis paḍa wihikan i tībra saŋ prabhu,
kāliḥ-kāliḥ ira apupul tinaṅisan pinĕkul ira nĕhĕṙ sinuṅkĕman*

Ꜽ bhojaṅku wĕkaṅku haywa tan asiḥ kita bapa riy-arinta kāsihan,
putrīṅkw-indumatīṅku bhaktya ri kakanta kita sarika sambhawa asiha,
anwam kāri tuhanku deṅku kawĕkas riŋ iña lawan uwa amalaṙ tuha,
himpĕṙ hantiga niŋ manuk taḍahasiḥ sy-anaku tinuwawākĕn iŋ waneḥ*

wuṅsw-amwīta bibinta matya tumuta i kapati saŋ ahulun ṅhulun tuhan,
lwa ambĕk māsku saŋ apriha iŋ bhuwana sĕmbahĕn iŋ amawa rāt kita anaku,
Ꜽ putri indumatīṅku māsku t ahurup tapiḥ alaḥ ibu kenku kenakĕn,
soṅsoṅaṅkwa tapiḥta kaṙwwana lawan haji lĕpasa mamukṣa mukṣana*

sĕmbaḥ ni ṅhulun alpadhaṙmma ri padadwaya paramawiśeṣapaṇḍita,
pun dewi indumatī kayatnakĕna de wiwudhapati bapebwa māsiha,
mwaŋ saŋ bhoja muwaḥ wuruk-wurukĕn iŋ nagara palaṙ aniṙwwa saŋ prabhu,
waṙṣājñāna para adhipaṇḍita dumadyakĕna kawijayanya riŋ prajā*

nāhan liŋ parameśwarī tucapa saŋ prabhu kasiḥ arĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,
saŋ hyaŋ jīwa hana i gulū nira lawan kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira saŋsaya asamun,
sāmpun kāku pasāra-sāra ni waraḥ yatiwara rinĕgĕp nareśwara,
tan simpaŋ kadi de nira aṅayatakĕn panaḥ aṅĕnani de nira aṅhiḍĕp*

trĕṣṇābandhana riŋ śarīra pinĕgat nira manaḥ ira kewala ahĕniŋ,
sadyotkranti linakṣyakĕn pataṅananya tumutupana simpaŋ iŋ hĕnū,
lāwan mantra nikā ndatan dwa sira saŋ prabhu wibhu riŋ awak wawaŋ mĕsat,
kewalya aśraya sūkṣma māri kahiḍĕp mamarĕṅi śiwamāṙgga dug mĕṅā*

sāmpun māti nareśwara atri sakaḍatwan anaṅisi pĕjaḥ nira alara,
śrī dewi indumatī muwaḥ tinaṅisan kapati lumay-awak nira awĕnĕs,
mādan śrī parameśwarī marĕk anĕmbaḥ i śawa haji satya sādara,
mājaṙ yan sira milwa matya pawaraḥ nira karaṇa ni luḥ niŋ aṅrĕṅö*

he nāthaṅku nihan ṅhulun praṇata bhakti tumuta saparanta tan saha,
yadyastun kita dewata athawa manuṣya huluna pakĕnaṅkwa de haji,
putrī putra rarā sĕḍĕŋ mĕrĕ-mĕrĕḥ kathamapi tan ikā katoliha,
patrĕmta prabhu yeki haṇḍĕmana ni ṅhulun amaḥ aku suṅsuŋ iŋ hĕnū*

nā liŋ śrī parameśwarī nĕhĕṙ apatrĕm amĕkasi hurip sira asĕgu,
himpĕṙ waṙṣa tibā nikaŋ luḥ i widaṙbbhanagara humilī mawaḥ wahan,
sambat-sambat ikaŋ sarājya gumĕrĕḥ kadi kĕtĕṙ i gĕrĕḥ niŋ ampuhan,
tawwan riŋ kusuma aṅjraḥ iŋ masa kapat paḍa ni taṅis ikā n rinĕṅwakĕn*

prāpta ŋ truḥ kadi sĕmbu-sĕmbuṙ i jaja aṅawara ri gĕmuḥ iŋ payodhara,
waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ apiṇḍa pupuk i rahi keṅgutan halis,
polaḥ niŋ kilat iŋ tawaŋ kadi kĕḍap niŋ asamaya kapaṅgiha iŋ taman,
his hīs niŋ bañu muṅgu riŋ tarĕtĕpan kadi luḥ iŋ anaṅis pinaṅkwakĕn*

muṅgw-iŋ maṇḍyusa kāli-kāliḥ ira mogha kadi kinasut iŋ pasaṅgaman,
keṅĕṙ mātra gulū narendramahiṣī kadi cala-cala tan panūt kinol,
piṅgiṙ niŋ kanin iŋ jaja asĕmu miraḥ kadi karagĕt i tuṅtuŋ iŋ kuku,
rāhĕn siñjaŋ ira n lume miṅay-awaṙṇna wahu kawawa de nareśwara*

śrī dewi indumatī lĕwĕs lara nira n panaṅis asidĕha aṅure gĕluŋ,
mambĕt madhya nira aṅgaluṅgaŋ araras tĕṅaḥ ira sumawe ri saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tan kewran lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ wijil i luḥ nira tan inusapan hana i mukha,
sambat-sambat ira aṅrĕmĕk hati rasanya karaṇa ni taṅis niŋ aṅrĕṅö*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ahā bibi haji ndi siḥta winaliṅku ta kita tulusa asiha i ṅhulun,
muwaḥ bapa haji ndi siḥta palakunkwa tulusa ni wĕlasta ri ṅhulun,
ujaṙtta kita ṅūni kāsihana niŋ jagat anaku sadā pakāśrayan,
jagat karika māsiha iry-aku kita pwa paḍa tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn*

prabhuṅku kita kāliḥ ĕndi parananta pawuṅu sakarĕŋ waraḥ ṅhulun,
yan iŋ śiwapada athawa iŋ haripada athawa lĕpasa kunaŋ saka irikā,
ṅhulun tumutura apa don iŋ ahurip wiphala yan apasaḥ lawan kita,
patiṅku hawanaṅkwa muṅsiṙ i padanta bapa tañakĕna iŋ kadewatan*

pulaḥta humĕnĕŋ diṅaryan asagaṙ ndi kari culu-culuḥta ri ṅhulun,
nihan ṅhulun anakta paṅkwakĕn aḍa atiśaya bapa kita n huwus pĕjaḥ,
prayojana ni deṅkw-asambat akusā baribinana kita n paḍa aturū,
palaṙ-palaṙ awuṅwa de ni panaṅisku nĕhĕṙ ajara māsku cĕp tuhan*

nihan tĕtĕlakĕn hatiṅku bibi muṅgaḥ akĕsĕl ahĕnĕk tĕka i jaja,
muwaḥ priḥ i mataṅku tīsana rahup rahupana bibi bawwa-bawwana,
pilī  piliṅan i ṅhulun dumadak aṅhĕlu pupukana tulya tulyana,
guluṅku kadi meḥ kahötana rasanya n anaṅis i patinta sĕmburĕn*

ri kāla ni huripta ṅūni bibi sāhasa kita sahasa aṅabĕt ṅhulun,
hasiḥ bapa haji i ṅhulun tĕka sira anuluŋ aṅusapi luḥ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mataŋ ya bibi maḥ palu ṅhulun alaḥ pawuṅu sakaharĕp ṅhulun habĕt,
ndya sī yan anuluŋ muwaḥ bapa haji i ṅhulun atĕhĕṙ ataṅguha i kita*

syapa ika śaraṇāśrayaṅkwa ri pĕjaḥta bapa haji nihan dudut ṅhulun,
apan kaka turuŋ wĕnaŋ śaraṇa ni ṅhulun apituwin anwam iŋ wayaḥ,
kadaŋ-kadaŋ adoḥ sira asiḥ alĕba amihutaṅanana sī kadi ṅhulun,
mataŋ yan anakanta riŋ suruwayan ṅhulun alaḥ alapĕn maran pĕjaḥ*

aḍā hyaŋ aparan ta koŋ widhi ṅaranmu tan awĕlas adĕṅky-anon sukha,
bapaṅku sira māti demu mapa doṣa nira huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
lawan bibi tumūt prasiddha tika ko muwaḥ amĕjahi tan pakāraṇa,
mataŋ ya wĕtu ko rwa sānak aku patyani saha bala demu hĕntyakĕn*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nāhan sambat ira anaṅis kaḍĕḍĕtan lara hati nira tan wĕnaŋ kinöl,
simsim wāhu hilaŋ maṇiknya kalĕbū paḍa-paḍa nira niṣprabha akucĕm,
dady-a ateja katonan iŋ rahina tan parawi wĕṅi tiniṅgal iŋ wulan,
saṅka i rūpa nira asawaŋ karĕbahan gunuŋ alara ri līna saŋ prabhu*

paṅde niŋ widhi tan wĕnaŋ winadha tiṅhalana kasiḥ arĕp suputrikā,
kāry-anwam ri pĕjaḥ nareśwara samaṇḍyusa sira kalawan nareśwarī,
de niŋ duhkha kĕdö sira amalaku milwa maṅatigana maṇḍyusa i dalĕm,
patrĕm wahw-inunus nira inayatakĕn ri jaja kaka kaka akrak aṅrĕbut*

maṅkin ghūṙṇnita śabda niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis wĕdi kaluputana iŋ nrĕpātmajā,
Āpan buddhi nira aṅhuwus-huwus apakṣa pĕjaha tumuta i nareśwara,
göŋ trĕṣṇa asiḥ arāma rena kapĕgan kapati pati sira alara anaṅis,
drāk siddha anĕmu duhkha niŋ dadi manuṣya paṅawaśa ni śāpa saŋ rĕṣi*

saŋ bhoja prihati n tumon kasiḥ arĕp ny-awak ira kari de nareśwara,
kady-agriŋ sira de ni duhkha nira tan saḥ anaṅis i dagan narādhipa,
Āśābhūta marambĕhan wĕtu ni luḥ nira mulat i narendrakanyakā,
maṙmma amaṅku pĕgat-pĕgat sapitutuṙ nira tuna-tuna de nikaŋ taṅis*

rakryan haywa wiraṅrwaŋ induŋ ĕnĕbĕn ta pamanas i laranta tīsakĕn,
riŋ swaṙggastha narendra sāmpun atuha apituwi huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
pakṣa kṣatriya rāka rakryan apagĕḥ wĕnaṅa śaraṇa rakryan iŋ hayu,
ṅhiŋ yan māti kakanta mamriḥ iŋ ayun kita pĕjaha tumūta ri ṅhulun*

haywa aśa alara duhkha yan bapa haji mwaŋ ibu haji pĕjaḥ sira adulur,
yāwat janma ṅaranya tan hana tuwuḥ watu kaluputa saṅka riŋ pati,
tan pendaḥ kadi cakra niŋ ratha tĕka ŋ dadi niyata midĕṙ puriḥ nika,
saṅka iŋ mrĕtyu tĕka ṅhurip kunĕŋ ikaŋ pati niyata mijil saka iŋ hurip*

māyākāra hana iŋ crĕmin paḍa nikaŋ dadi sahana hananya tan sthiti,
himpĕṙ pādapa tan wuruŋ manirara amĕkasi tuha tuwuḥnya tan lanā,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ hurip iŋ manuṣya juti tattwa nika tan alawas wawaŋ hilaŋ,
kintw-i ikaŋ pati jāti tattwa nika tan kṣaṇika pinakadhaṙmma niŋ dadi*

eman ṅwaŋ lumĕkas mamet pati saka iŋ lumĕkasa ri kapetan iŋ hurip,
pöṅpöṅĕn ta huripta yogya dadahanta makahuluna de munīśwara,
Āpan yan wruḥ i bheda saŋ rwa kalawan wruha ri pasamudāya niŋ tiga,
icchā nora kasaṅśaya iŋ hala lawan hayu niyata luput saka irika*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hayu nikaŋ hayu yan gawayĕn,
ri wruḥ i saŋ rwa bhineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn,
kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hala nikaŋ hala yan gawayĕn,
ri wruḥ i saŋ rwa bhineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn*

siṅgiḥ ujaṙtta ri saŋ krĕtasamaya wiśeṣa paṅawruḥ ira,
kweḥ nira riŋ nagara iŋ acala paḍa tikā pinakoṅgwan ira,
ndin rakĕta ŋ sukhaduhkha ri sira satata abrata tan palabuḥ,
lokaparāśraya kāraṇa nira magawe hayu tan wipatha*

saŋ wruḥ i saŋ wĕkas iŋ samaya winuni de paramādiguru,
kewala śuddha manaḥ nira linĕtu lĕtuḥ kapana alĕtuha,
wāhyaśarīra pinuccha nira ri tĕka niŋ pati tan ginĕgö,
jñāna wiśeṣa śarīra nira taya śarīra nira iŋ wĕkasan*

wwaŋ magawe hayu yan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hayu,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hayu-hayu ni gawe nika tan wiphala,
wwaŋ magawe hala yan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hala,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hala-hala ni gawe nika tan wiphala*

wwaŋ magawe hayu tan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hayu,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhayu-hayu ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ,
wwaŋ magawe hala tan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hala,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhala-hala ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ*

saŋ wiku gūḍha nihan wulatana mamaṅan tĕḍa riŋ pahĕhan,
tan tĕḍa tan śuci ta pwa sahana-hana niŋ pinaṅan liŋ ira,
hetu nira ambĕk alokika winulatan ajrĕm apiṇḍa kasop,
śuddha nikaŋ pratipatti makalarapan uttama niŋ samaya*

māsku mataŋnyan ikaŋ hayu gawayakĕnanta sĕḍĕŋ mahurip,
paṇḍita towi yayā sira maṅulahakĕn brata tan kaluṣa,
buddhy-ahĕniŋ brata yoga tapa taki-takinta maran kawaśa,
gĕgwana rakryan anĕmwakĕna wara waraḥ paramādiguru*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

anĕmu nĕmu kĕta ikā saŋ sāmpun krĕtasamaya,
wihikan i rasa saŋ hyaŋ tattwajñāna kalĕpasĕn,
tan uliḥ-uliḥ iŋ aṅdoḥ saṅka iŋ pāda muniwara,
uliḥ iŋ asaṅu tasyan bhakti iŋ paṇḍita matuha*

aṅinak inaka taŋ wwaŋ yāwat jñāna pinakadon,
syapa ta sira mamaṅgiḥ tattwajñāna dudu gawe,
hana satata masewā tan byaktanya pinihanan,
sukrĕta juga maṅinte lāwan duṣkrĕta maṅiriŋ*

hana sira guruputra anak niŋ paṇḍita nagara,
sahana nira ta rakwa adrĕwya ŋ jñāna pakagurun,
taha tan ika paniddhan wet niŋ paṇḍita matuha,
amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ tattwa iŋ uṅgwana rahayu*

anak iŋ apirak akweḥ ṅūni i nwamnya paḍa sukha,
sahana nika ta rakwa anirw-akweḥ apirak ika,
taha tan ika paniddhan wet niŋ śreṣṭha panariman,
amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ śrī tan siŋ kahanan ira*

kita yayi sĕḍĕŋ anwam priḥ saŋ hyaŋ rasa kawikun,
pira karika musuḥ niŋ wikw-aṅhiŋ nĕm ikaŋ akas,
alahakĕn i dalĕm twas pet siŋ soṅgwan ika raraḥ,
alaha pĕjaha rakryan ya iki swaṙgga ṅaran ika*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

nā de nira awara waraḥ ri narendraputrī,
tapwan tĕtĕs tinuna sandhi nikaŋ prayoga,
anwam suśīla guṇamanta krĕtopadeśa,
saṅka i paṅajyan ira kawruḥ ira adhiguhya*

śrī putrikā kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕŋ tumuṅkul,
sāmpun bhinasmi śawa saŋ prabhu de munīndra,
muṅgw-i i taman sira cinaṇḍi lawan sudewī,
sampūṙṇna bapra nira ratna mahāprabhāwa*

saŋ bhoja sāmpun aṅadĕg ri widaṙbbharājya,
swasthā sabhūmi nira bhakty-anukūla sādhu,
mawwat paḍa amarahakĕn ri sukhanya rakwa,
anwam muwaḥ nrĕpati liŋnya muwaḥ manĕmbaḥ*

sāmpun sira ayugala ratna wiśeṣaputrī,
rājāṅkura awilĕt ikaŋ pakurĕn sawandhu,
soluṙ lulut sahati lĕŋlĕŋ aluṅluṅan kuŋ,
saśrī sakĕmbaŋ alaṅö sakurā sawīja*

kaywan ragas paḍa nikaŋ nagari i widaṙbbha,
riŋ wrĕddharūpa haji dewata lahru sākṣāt,
maṅke n prasiddha kadi kaywan aron akĕmbaŋ,
śrī bhoja maṅdani sira anwam apiṇḍa rĕŋrĕŋ*

wet niŋ krĕtā ri paṅadĕg haji nora duṣṭa,
rāmya ṅhĕnū tĕgal ayun tĕka riŋ wanādri,
wāni ŋ wwaŋ aṅhaliwati iriya tuṅga-tuṅgal,
aṅhiŋ gaḍuŋ luŋ ika maṅhabĕt asriŋ oliḥ*

mantrī nira atuha tuha dwija śꜽwa boddha,
kāsiḥ kapaṙccaya narendra wĕnaŋ mara i jro,
prajña iṅgitajña ginulaŋ halu riŋ wiweka,
sojaṙ niŋ āgama tinūt nira tan wimāṙgga*

söḥ śāla dhaṙmma kuṭi kīṙtti narendra riŋ rāt,
wwaŋ śreṣṭhi dhaṙmma ginawe nira sāri-sāri,
wwaŋ duṣṭa mogha kapitūt milu dhaṙmmabuddhi,
solaḥ swabhāwa haji tan dadi tan tinūtnya*

śrī bhoja sāmpun apagĕḥ siniwi iŋ kaḍatwan,
okĕṙ tumiṅhal i saŋ indumatī hana i jro,
Āpan samāsa niŋ akaṙmma wayaḥ nira agöŋ,
aṅhiŋ swayĕmbarakĕna iṅĕt iṅĕt narendra*

nā de nira aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt kalawan sudewī,
sāmpun wināhyakĕn ira i kulawandhu ri jro,
riŋ saṙwwasiddhi tuwin amrĕtayoga tĕmbe,
höman haji inarahakĕn para taṇḍa mantrī*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

eñjiŋ śri indumatī kinon marĕka kāliḥ saŋ sunanda aṅiriŋ,
lāgy-a amūṙṇnama mopawāsa ya ta maṅde suṅkawā niŋ hati,
tistis meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu lumampaḥ tan kwa de niŋ harip,
mukṣa lwīṙ amarāśraya i mukha nira śrī niŋ wulan tan lumöŋ*

sāmpun prāpta sira i dalĕm praṇata maṙmma atwaŋ ri jöŋ saŋ prabhu,
lāwan śrī parameśwarī sira sinambaḥ māsiḥ aṅliŋ rĕsĕp,
 Om  rakryan pada nīlakaṇṭha kinabhaktyanta astu dīṙgghāyuṣa,
swasthā tuṅgalĕn iŋ manuṅgali jagat māskw-i ibu nā liŋ nira*

mojaṙ saŋ prabhu māsku tan tugĕta niŋ twasta an inundaŋ mami,
rākanta prihati n harĕp mamituha i māsku ndan ewĕḥ juga,
saŋ ratw-a asiha len sasambhawa muwaḥ yekī pinet ni ṅhulun,
kady-amrat mrati mās juga ṅwaŋ amagantākĕn puriḥ niŋ dadi*

yāwat dhaṙmma ṅaranya riŋ dadi manuṣya awās hiwĕḥ yan pinet,
lwiṙ sūkṣmā maganal bhaṭāra gumawe tiṅkaḥnya yan maṅkana,
yadyastun jalu jalw-ameta sawawanya iŋ janma haywa asali,
byakta iwĕḥ niki kimpunaḥ kita yan iŋ strī-strī n mameta priya*

saŋkṣepanya kita swayĕmbarakĕnaṅkwa anugrahaṅkwa i kita,
sakweḥ saŋ ratu hundaṅĕn pilihananta asiŋ sayogya i hati,
yadyan hyaŋ palakunta māsku yugalanta amriḥ mrihaṅkwa aṅhyaṅa,
aṅhiŋ yan hyaŋ anaṅga kahyuna hade tan pāwak ewĕḥ pinet*

na ajñā saŋ prabhu yogya paṅkwakĕna de saŋ mās maṇik niŋ purī,
Āpan māsa nira n prapañca saputĕn riŋ rāga de hyaŋ smara,
tan wruḥ riŋ sahura awiraŋ mata sira n paṅyogyana i saŋ prabhu,
tan maṅguḥ sira tan miṅĕl kadi liṅiṙ mās aṙcca paṅhyaŋ hyaṅan*

tan saṅka iŋ awalepa kāraṇa nira n lwiṙ tuhwa monabrata,
kepwan buddhi nira atĕgĕg maṅucap agyā gyān harĕp mantuka,
wahw-a adandan anĕmbaha i nrĕpati mojaṙ saŋ sunanda aṅjawil,
 Om  yan  Om  huwusĕn huwus liṅa ni māskw-a alaḥ tuhan mājara*

tan kewö pitutuṙnya de nrĕpasutā mantuk sira iŋ pamrĕman,
strī-strī mājaṙ ajaṙ gumanti humatuṙ prāpta iñjiŋ akweḥ marĕk,
moliḥ tīṙtha binuṅbuṅan winalun iŋ handoŋ saka iŋ paṙwwata,
maṅde śuddha ri buddhi saŋ prabhu sukhā sāmpun sira acāmana*

<puṣpacāpa> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓ : 20

prāsāda sphaṭika alaṅö ri tĕṅaḥ iŋ nūsa araras pañcuranya,
strī stry-a amaṅku puḍak winimba makaranya lwiṙ lĕṅĕŋ de ni kuŋnya,
kady-ahyun namahaywa luṅsuṙ i tapiḥnya n maṅligā yan hana wwaŋ,
lāgy-a anaṅga suśūnya saṅka ri pacuṙ niŋ wwꜽ ya ta aṅde ṅĕliḥnya*

ri prāsāda hana aṙcca ratna ri dalĕm ndān aṙddhanārīśwara ahyaŋ,
wimba śrī naranātha dewata lawan dewī nira arok śarīra,
ṅkā saŋ bhoja maṅaṙccana pratidina aṅabhyāsa ri swastha niŋ rāt,
kady-a amakpak aṅastwakĕn ri jayaśatrwa śrī narendra n pamūjā*

saŋ bhoja wruḥ i tattwa niŋ japasamādhi n dhāraṇa dhyānapūṙwwa,
mwaŋ tiṅkaḥ niŋ adehaśuddhi pinakānuṣṭhāna yan recakādi,
sāmpun kālap ulaḥ dwijeśwara mamūjā pathya riŋ brahmamantra,
saŋ hyaŋ kūṭarahasyamantra jinapākĕn de nira atūt gaṇitri*

tatkāla nrĕpati n paṅuccaraṇakĕn mantra stuti i saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,
tan polaḥ wiṣaya aṅhiḍĕp ri sira saṅyogānta riŋ yogya yogan,
maṅgā tan lĕpara ŋ japastawa sĕḍĕŋ niŋ jñāna n enak tĕtĕpnya,
simpaŋ niŋ hati yeki kāraṇa nira anaṅhāra saŋ hyaŋ śiwātma*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

ri huwus ira mamūjā līlā śuddha manaḥ ira,
aṅusapi mukha saśrī de niŋ candana karakĕt,
mijil aṅinaŋ aṅicchā riŋ wwꜽ niŋ ranu maṅilo,
nĕhĕṙ anisigi danta i tuṅtuŋ niŋ gagaŋ inapi*

tucapa ta para mantrī śꜽwa brāhmaṇa sugata,
parĕŋ apupul asewa ṅkāna i jro paḍa humatur,
nrĕpati sira maluṅguḥ riŋ siṅhāsana kanaka,
aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt i siddhā niŋ kāṙyya n gawayakĕna*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ndin kāṙyya iwĕha riŋ wicakṣaṇa sujanma lituhayu kawi priyambada,
bhakti iŋ hyaŋ prabhu śakti dhꜽṙyya saha wāndhawa saha bala kośawāhana,
yadyan sāgara tambakĕn satakĕna athawa wukiṙ alihĕn ratākĕna,
byakta awās kawaśanya de nira saŋ uttamapuruṣa wiśeṣa riŋ jagat*

śrī bhoja pwa sira n prasiddha guṇamanta saphala sira bhūmipālaka,
prajñā śāstrawit iṅgita wruḥ iŋ apālapan aṅinaki buddhi niŋ marĕk,
akweḥ drĕwya nira aprameya kadi sāgara papupulan iŋ wway-iŋ nadī,
wany-a anindita riŋ parākrama yan iŋ naya kadi bhagawān wrĕhaspati*

maṅke pwa n hana rājakāṙyya gawayĕn kakaratala tĕkap nareśwara,
śrī dewi indumatī swayĕmbarakĕna amiliha  ratu sasambhawa i sira,
sāmpun saŋ prabhu motusan maminaṅa i para ratu samayogya hundaṅĕn,
lāwan saŋ haja milwa winwitakĕn iŋ nrĕpati raghu katon tĕkā nira*

sāmpun höman ira irikā ta para taṇḍa sama-sama sama aṅharĕp  gawe,
sora isuk gumĕrĕḥ makakrĕtug abaṇḍuŋ asahuran aganti loṙ kidul,
len taŋ wwaŋ maṅusuŋ lakaṙ-lakaṙ ikā winaca wuhaya de nikaŋ mulat,
akweḥ wwaŋ ka gĕrāḥ arĕp mulata wāhu mĕtu sinurakan muliḥ pacĕḥ*

abwat hajyan ikaŋ humuŋ saha garantuŋ atabĕ tabĕhan paḍa asĕlur,
agyā lagy-aṅuhuḥ sira i harĕp alaḥ laku-laku liŋ ikaŋ hana i wuri,
tuṅgul paṅharĕp osik akrĕp asinaŋ kumuliliŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ,
lwiṙ guntuṙ kamarĕkrĕkĕn kayu pĕtuŋ priŋ asalĕsĕk agĕṇṭaḥ iŋ lĕbuḥ*

ewĕṙ nora lĕga aŋ apaṇḍay-anulis para lukis asipĕt mwaŋ aṅjahit,
sakweḥ niŋ ginĕlaṙ wruha aṅanam anam wruḥ i suruhan ikā siliḥ tuluŋ,
solaḥ niŋ tama tan hana ataña ṅaranya huwus adu kabeḥ dinadyakĕn,
paprāsan winaṅun paḍa acarita paṙwwa piniturun atuṅgalan kathā*

<widyutkara> 
– – – |⏑⏑– |⏑– ⏑|⏑⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏓ : 25

embuḥ bhūṣaṇa niŋ tĕkĕn wuwuŋ apūṙwwa karacanan ikā tĕka iŋ pamanisan,
lāwan tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ paṅastryanan apaṙppat ahalĕp akilā paḍa ahayu hayu,
de niŋ mās pinakopacāra sinisik pĕñu pinakawuwuŋnya kumram asinaŋ,
lwiṙ digdāha riŋ astapaṙwwata sĕnö nika murub apadĕlwan iŋ kṣititala*

aśrī rāmya ni de nira amahayu rājya kaliliran apūṙwwa kādbhuta dahat,
miṅgaṙ bapra nika i dalĕm watu hitĕm kuṭa nikaŋ i yawā lumaṅkuŋ ahirĕŋ,
kulwan wetan agopura atiśaya loṙ kidul agupura piṇḍa maṙppat aruhur,
krĕṣṇākāra paḍa aṅlunaŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukus i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ dara awrĕg aputiḥ*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

luṅhā ŋ wrĕtta ri kāṙyya saŋ prabhu paḍa adbhuta sahana nikaŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,
wwaŋ-wwaŋ pora ḍusun-ḍusun paḍa harĕp wihikana mulata iŋ swayambara,
tan samwas raray-aṅhwan iŋ tĕgal atakwan i tĕka ni gawe nareśwara,
salwiṙ niŋ baṇija iŋ pĕkĕn taliṅa lintaḥ anaḍaḥ ucapan gawe nika*

sāmpun prāpta samotusan humatuṙ iŋ nrĕpati sĕḍĕŋ ira an hana iŋ sabhā,
enak buddhi narendra de ni panuwal para ratu rasa tan wuruŋ tĕkā,
lumrā ŋ wrĕtta tĕka i dalĕm ri ḍatĕṅa aṙyya raghusuta mara iŋ swayambara,
twas niŋ strī sakaḍatwan aṅdadak aluŋ turida paḍa rumūpaka i sira*

strī-strī haṙṣa pinöm pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara ri pamihaŋnya riŋ yayaḥ,
tan haṙṣa iŋ kawi rakwa rena nika monaguṇa pisaniṅūn tumiṅhala,
ndan rakwa iki hinuṙnya matya saka riŋ tuluyakĕna susatya riŋ priya,
liŋnya n kewala tan hinanti ni papaṅgiha nika pĕjaha iŋ panambaṅan*

tapwan māri taṅis-taṅisnya n inalap hinaturakĕn i jöŋ suputrikā,
wrā niŋ roma maṅekadeśa ri piliŋ piliṅan ika baṅun pameṙ i luḥ,
enak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥnya mamalaṙ-malaṙ i pada narendraputrikā,
Āpan swāmi nikā karĕṅwan i parĕknya ri saŋ aja tĕwĕk nika apasaḥ*

antuk saŋ priya maṅdawākĕn inalĕm para kawi sumĕnāha riŋ kajaŋ,
yeki n rakwa kinonya kady-aṅucapa amaḥ aku tuhan alap waca ṅhulun,
mogha nyan ya kinonakĕn wacan ikā ri pamaca nika maṅdadak lumuḥ,
swāminya adadi pustaka anuturakĕn hiḍĕp ika pinapagnya riŋ taṅis*

ṅūni i kāla nika n turuŋ marĕk i jöŋ nira ṅaran ika ken madhūdakā,
saŋ mambaŋ madhusūdana priya nikā kawi taruṇa marĕk ri jöŋ haji,
widhy-a amidhyani kāraṇanya wiraha inalapan alara luḥnya tan pĕgat,
ndaḥ rakryan jayawaspa teki wĕkasan ṅaran ika satĕwĕk nikā marĕk*

<abhikrĕti> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 25

para prabhu kaḍaṅhanan turida rāga nira sinaput iŋ smara amulaṅuni,
huwus katĕka kuŋ nira ahawan ujaṙ tuhun amĕlas arĕp riniptakĕn ira,
lawan punagi kesy-anambaha ri jöŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā hana hyuna nira,
akiṅkiŋ aṅalap kasoṙ paḍa tan aprabhu sahana nira arĕbut kahulunan*

wawaŋ nrĕpatiputrikā rinĕbut iŋ hiḍĕp inaṅĕn aṅĕn raras-raras ira,
hanan kahiḍĕp iŋ madhubrata rĕṅiḥ rĕṅiha nira n arĕs kapaṅkwa harasĕn,
lĕyĕp hayu nira n linaṅwakĕn amūṙtti kakawin inapus wineḥ amanisa,
hana i hati kinubdha kady-apĕga kāraṇa nira mijil iŋ puḍak dadi ṭikā*

adandan asĕnāha sañjata para prabhu ḍatĕṅa mara i widaṙbbhanagara,
lana aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt ri pahyasan ira aṅinakana ri manaḥ narendratanayā,
hana aṅdadak anat śarīra manahap nahap aharĕp alantasa n winulatan,
paḍa aṅalap-alap sipat jĕnu mĕnuŋ hawu karaṇa suputrikā n aharĕpa*

muwaḥ saŋ aja sāmpun aṙppat akire lumarisa makamaṅgala dwijawara,
sahasraśatakoṭi wīra winidhi nrĕpati tumuta śakti sāmpun ayaśa,
pĕnuḥ sahana niŋ lĕbuḥ tĕkap i sañjata nika kumaluŋ pinañjĕṙ aṅadĕg,
ikaŋ nagara denya kady-akalaṅan wihaga saŋ aja moliha prabhusutā*

mijil sira śinaṅkhapāṇyan i karaŋ ni patiga niŋ aśoka wahw-asalaga,
ikaŋ bhramara haṙṣa riŋ kusuma muṅgw-i taṅan ira mara aṅisĕp tan awĕliŋ,
laki stry-aliwĕran hañaṙ-hañaṙ apaṅgiḥ aduluṙ akaraŋ karaŋ sĕkaṙ arūm,
katampwan i kucuṙ nikaŋ wway-atawiŋ-tawiŋ i lawĕ lawö nikaŋ sarasija*

i sāmpun i kaśaṅkhapāṇyan ira mañjiŋ i dalĕm aduluṙ lawan dwijawara,
anambaḥ aṅusap ri jöŋ nrĕpati mamwit i ḍatĕṅa nira iŋ widaṙbbhanagara,
sinuṅsuŋ iŋ ujaṙ prahāsana nĕhĕṙ jumaya jaya jayā nira i paran ira,
ahum hanaku saŋ pakolihĕn i tiṅhal iŋ ahayu dumĕlwa jalwa rasika*

kunaŋ pawĕkasaṅkwa haywa ta bapaṅku tan apĕnĕd iŋ ambĕk iŋ para-paran,
rare mara kita ndatan raraya de niŋ amawa manaḥ atwaṅa iŋ wwaŋ atuha,
inuttama dhanuṙddhara anaku tathāpi tan ika paṅayāya riŋ kadi kita,
ikaŋ guṇa ya tan paraṅkĕpana maryada rahayu lawö hananya kapalaŋ*

ikaŋ sakahawan ri bhūmi ni bapaṅku pahayu kita rakṣaka aṅanumata,
sapawwat ika hantusākĕna sasambhawa haturakĕnanya māsku tariman,
ujaṙku pituhunta haywa kita sāhasa maṅalapa wastu mūlya tinĕṅĕt,
prasiddha kadaŋ iŋ jagat kita dumadyakĕna sukha nikā mataŋnya pahayu*

pamitran alawas rĕsĕp karaṇa niŋ wĕnaŋ aṅalapa wastu tan pamalaku,
yan iŋ wiṣayarāmajātaka puriḥnya karaṇa niŋ anĕmwa mās pirak ika,
karāsikaguṇan ya kāraṇa niŋ oliha raras i manaḥ niŋ adyaḥ araras,
kaśaktin abhimāna kāraṇa niŋ aṅraraḥ aṅalapa rājya niŋ ripukula*

sirat-sirat i de narendra raghu mojaṙ amanis amadhaṙmmakĕn ri saŋ aja,
minuṣṭi pinakādidewa hiniḍĕp rasa nika kinayogyakĕn pinituhu,
putus niŋ adhamā tan ahyuna rumĕṅwakĕna ri pitutuṙ nira ahayu dahat,
ya kāraṇa narendraputra makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ narapati*

ri sāmpun ira mamwit iŋ nrĕpati saṙwwi laku nira mara i narendramahiṣī,
hana aṅhaḍaŋ aweḥ sĕrĕḥ saha taṅis wagĕd ahayu hinĕmban iŋ kaka-kaka,
kataṅgamaŋ aweḥ sĕpaḥ nrĕpatiputra nĕhĕṙ amuhun amriḥ aṅhari hari,
tapiḥ saŋ araras pininta nira mūlya basahan ira raṇḍi paṅhurup ira*

byatīta ri huwus nira aṅucap ucap tĕka sira ri taman narendramahiṣī,
lĕṅĕŋ kadi kadewatan halĕp ika apan ajuraŋ awukiṙ mapājaṙ ajaran,
maeṙttali pinañcuran jinalatuṇḍa tinalaga ri soṙnya kādbhuta dahat,
ikaŋ kaka kaka anwam adyus anĕṅaḥ lawan anak-anakanya ketaka miṅiŋ*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

kalpadruma taruwara pārijāta winaṅun bwat asana sakapat,
abhra asinaŋ asĕmu saka iŋ kadewatan ululnya kanaka pinahat,
jinriṅjriŋ-iŋ anak anakan maṇik cinaturaṅga lumarap amiraḥ,
mās jaṅga katiraḥ awilĕt pralĕmba nika riŋ tarĕtĕpan alaṅö*

ṅkānā nrĕpatisuta marĕk ri rena nira sādara satiru tirun,
amwit lumarisa ḍatĕṅa iŋ widaṙbbhanagarī bibi nira wihikan,
maṙmma asiḥ awĕlas asĕgĕḥ mamakpak amapag riŋ ucapan amanis,
niṙwighna kita bapa jaya iŋ swayambara sada aṅalahakĕna ratu*

rakryān aṅinaṅa tanayaṅku māsku mapa hetu niŋ awak akuru,
agriŋ karika kita lawan waneḥ brata kunaŋ karaṇa niŋ awĕnĕs,
haywa anaku kaluṣa kita ahyun iŋ kajayaśatrwan anuta ri harĕp,
akweḥ phala nika kaki saṙwwawighna niyatanya hilaŋ alaradan*

ndan rakwa kadamĕlan ikaŋ swayambara kahop riŋ anakĕbi rara,
sakweḥ para ratu pininaŋ ya teka pilihĕn sakaharĕp alapĕn,
de ni ṅhulun ahiḍĕp i buddhi saŋ rara kapan harĕpa riŋ atuha,
ṅhiŋ kahyuna nika ratu cakrawaṙttitanaya aguṇa kawi taruṇa*

rakryan pwa saphala wĕka cakrawaṙtti tuwi śakti wihikan aṅaji,
siṅhākrĕti tuhu-tuhu siṅhaputra wĕnaŋ uṅsirĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,
byakta anaku mamĕnaṅa riŋ swayambarasabha aṅalahakĕna ratu,
tan sĕṅgahĕn aṅalĕm anak syapa ika kadi māsku lituhayu wani*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

tatkāla i paṅucap narendramahiṣī tucapa ta para ratnakanyakā,
osik tan pakawanwan agyaŋ i ḍatĕŋ saŋ aja kadi hañaṙ-hañaṙ mulat,
tan pātmā kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn kalukaran gĕluŋ asidĕha tan hana aṅucap,
kady-a ahöm turidanya n osaḥ akĕcap lwiṙ anicipi manis nrĕpātmaja*

wwantĕn lwiṙ śaśiwimba wāhu mijil aṅḍaḍari hayu nika anwam iŋ wayaḥ,
aṅgöŋ mabrata śuklapakṣa nika paṅlwaŋ i manaḥ ika tan wĕnaŋ licin,
rāganya n dadakan tumaṅgal i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasuta kadi tambwaŋ iŋ wulan,
krĕṣṇākāra tĕṅaḥnya de ni tapak iŋ suḥ asĕmu  sĕmu rāhw-añumbana*

len taŋ lwiṙ pranita adagaŋ kira-kiranya sumikĕpa wĕkas nrĕpātmaja,
kapraŋ rwa ipu kataṇḍĕgan turida tan patahĕnan aṅagĕm pralāpita,
toḥ-toḥ nya an iŋ agĕgwan ambĕk apagĕḥ mapa tiki n alaḥ aṅgĕgö smara,
aṅlampwa aṅusira i padadwaya nira an panikĕlakĕna tuṙ humaṇḍĕma*

strī saŋsāra sarāga mohita sawaŋ wana gahana kalahrwan iŋ kapat,
trāsa twasnya kakiṅkiṅan ginĕsĕṅan pinarawaśa tinunwan iŋ smara,
nora anīsi manaḥnya kewala panasbaran alisuḥ aṅölakĕn lara,
maṅke pwa n karĕṅö gĕrĕḥ saŋ aja mañjiŋ aluŋ asĕmi kuŋ nika asĕwö*

endaḥ buddhi nikaŋ waneḥ tĕkap ika amawa turida luput linakṣaṇan,
muṅkuṙ tan huniṅa i ḍatĕŋ saŋ aja mañjiŋ asila ri harĕp nareśwarī,
ndan denya ahyas apahyasan dudu dudū hiniraṅakĕn ika i nrĕpātmaja,
sūkṣmākāra ni raśmi-raśmi ni wulatnya n araras apadĕlwan iŋ crĕmin*

kanyā rwaŋ siki rāmya kāliḥ aṅisapwakĕn anak-anakanya ketaka,
tuṅgal mājaṙ i putra putran ika māsku saŋ aja sira rakwa maṅkata,
ndan haywa akilayū tuhanku niyata ṅhulun inucap ujaṙ nika akalib,
maṙmmanya apasaḥ ambĕk eṅgal apadudwan aṅuwahi pamitran aṅdadak*

strī-strī sukṣĕka wahw-agātra turidanya mijil i wijil iŋ payodhara,
tan saḥ riŋ salukat gawe nrĕpatiputra sinalukatakĕnya tan humuŋ,
ramya arūm karĕṅö manisnya sinameni pamawan ika riṅraŋ iŋ hati,
tan samwas ginarut garutnya hiniḍĕpnya saŋ aja sahasa aṅisapwakĕn*

sakweḥ niŋ kumĕmit prapañca ni hatinya kumĕkĕsi taṅisnya riŋ karas,
Āpan buddhi narendraputra kadi tan tulusa duga duga aṅhalimbaṅa,
bhakty-a anĕmbaḥ i jöŋ ni rena nira mĕṅgĕp amanis agawe wulat maliŋ,
luṅhā tan pracura anĕhĕṙ nĕhĕrakĕn manaḥ iŋ ahayu kāri sukṣĕka*

<abhikrĕti> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 25

mijil saŋ aja kādbhuta abhinawa rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ apan paḍa ahyaŋ ahalĕp,
ikaŋ gaja ratha aśwa sañjata sabhūṣaṇa nika dumilaḥ kasĕnwan aruṇa,
sumaṅgraha humerakĕn widhi nira n lumarisa kumisik pasaṅgha niŋ ujar,
baṅun jalada tan pakāla gumĕrĕḥ ri taya niŋ aṅin aṅḍapuṙ saha kilat*

payuŋ  payuṅan iŋ lĕbuḥ kadi sĕkaṙ sinawuŋ apan anekawaṙṇna sumĕkar,
ikaŋ paṅuṅaṅan huwus winalunan wĕḍihan inuparĕṅga riŋ tulis ĕmās,
rara anwam inĕgĕḥ parĕŋ mijil amaṅguŋ asĕmu sĕmu lakṣmi niŋ masa kapat,
paḍa alal asĕnāha tiṅhal amanis wulatakĕna ri raśmi-raśmi saŋ aja*

hana iŋ gupura tan wawaŋ sira lumampaḥ ataña ri gĕnĕp ni sañjata nira,
sama asila hana iŋ lĕmaḥ muni manuk marahakĕn i wijilnya tan hana kari,
sira iŋ palukayan kinon ira kumona ri para juru yan lumakwa rumuhun,
samaṅkana sira n lumampaḥ aḍarat harĕp iŋ ulaḥ awās yayanyan ahalĕp*

ri lampaḥ ira ghūṙṇnita ŋ paḍahi paṅharĕp ira kumisik maṅeṙttali tibā,
saru swara nika abaruŋ binaruṅan tabĕ-tabĕhan agĕnturan kadi gĕrĕḥ,
humandaru tibā gubaṙ kumĕtug asriŋ aniru kĕtug iŋ hudan wahu ḍawuḥ,
arūm uni ni ghaṇṭa niŋ liman aṅuṅkaŋ asahuran i paṅhrik iŋ kuda bisir*

dwijāti rĕṣi śꜽwa boddha śuci sojaṙ ira maṅabhiwāda muṅgu ri harĕp,
yathākrama paḍa adara ahalĕp agöŋ i wĕtĕŋ ira lawan huwan riŋ atuha,
lumampaḥ alaris malaḥ ya tan arampaka ri sadawatā nikaŋ lĕbuḥ agöŋ,
humuŋ tĕkap ira n paṅuccaraṇa mantra kadi madhukara aṅisis humaliwat*

kĕliŋ wani wani iŋ usāna pamarakṣa nira mamawa bhindiwāla palaga,
baṅun rinawisan wĕhaŋnya kalawan ḍaḍa nika paḍa wok tĕka iŋ suku wulun,
hibĕk tatu rujit-rujit kadi tinambalan awak ika waṙṇna bĕntaṙ inawĕt,
agöŋ paḍa kabhīma-bhīma kadi dānawa mukha-mukha dꜽtya piṇḍa cawiri*

ikaŋ marĕk i jöŋ narendratanaya anwam aguṇa paḍa daṙśśanīya taruṇa,
titik nagara nora tan wruha n anak wĕsi haji tuwi mūlya kawwaṅan ika,
watĕk madana maṅdadi wwaŋ ujaṙ iŋ mulat i lituhayunya n ahyaŋ araras,
kunaŋ saŋ aja kāmadewa sakala anurun ucapan ikaŋ kapūhan i sira*

samaṅkana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan haṅu haṅun arĕbut mulat ri saŋ aja,
hanan kadi harĕp siliḥ galaha riŋ susu manĕwĕka riŋ nakha akas aluṅid,
paḍa akira kira akĕkĕs mata maliŋ-maliŋ aṅiriṅi kāladeśa sumilib,
katon kadi siliḥ praṅa iŋ halis arĕṅw-inayat ayatakĕnya maṅkin araras*

ikāŋ amawa pawwahan lituhayu prakaśita kawi mambaŋ uttama rare,
hañaṙ tĕka saka iŋ widaṙbbhanagarī layat inalapan aṅhañaŋ hañaṅakĕn,
rarānya kawĕkas pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara marĕk i jöŋ narendratanayā,
ya kāraṇa ni luḥnya mantĕn amalaṙ malaṙ i saŋ aja moliha i sira hĕlĕm*

manis ni kakawinya mūla ni papaṅgiḥ ika lawan ikaŋ rinuddha winalat,
pinet pĕjahana asĕnötan i kadaŋnya winuni karaṇanya yan lĕpas adoḥ,
paḍa apalarasan lawan jaruman amriḥ aṅaliḥ ahawan wĕṅi iŋ awa wulan,
tinūt i paṅaran ṅaranya kawidoṣa wĕkasan i ḍatĕŋnya riŋ nrĕpasuta*

ya tīka tan adoḥ ginĕgwan ira bāhu nika winisikan tinakwanan ira,
syapa ika paḍa saŋ swayĕmbarakĕna prakaśita pinakādi niŋ wwaŋ ahayu,
ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ bwat indrawanita ahyas ika pahawasĕn ta ya n sama hirib,
kĕcapnya n aṅĕsaḥ miṅĕl ya pawaraḥnya ri saŋ aja wawaŋ rĕmĕk hati nira*

hana aṅuṅaŋ anuṅga  nuṅgal aṅisapwakĕn anak-anakanya ketaka miṅiŋ,
maha aṅjĕlagakĕn hayunya makapaṅhaḍa buṅaḥ i mukhanya tan patalutuḥ,
ri kāla saŋ aja aṅinaŋ winulatanya ri wulat ira löṙ matanya lumiriŋ,
baṅun hañaṙ anūt harĕp sĕpaḥ awĕdy-aṅucapa tumiliŋ miṅe kadi cala*

rara anwam akire wulat dudu dudū saŋ aṅĕsaḥ i kisapwan iŋ kaka-kaka,
tupis-tupis i de nira aṅĕnahakĕn manaḥ ira tumiba i narendratanaya,
wagĕd-wagĕd aniṙwwa niṙwakĕn i de nira gamĕl inamĕṙ nira i taṅan ira,
tĕkāsiḥ atabĕḥ sĕrĕḥ saha pucaŋ nika dalihan ira aṅawe ri saŋ aja*

i soṙ niŋ asana asĕkaṙ hana sira aṅuṅaŋ araras aliṇḍuṅan kaka-kaka,
ṅĕliḥ-ṅĕliḥ iŋ ekacitta ri narendrasuta ṅĕliḥ ira ahuyaŋ pinĕpĕtan,
sawaŋ-sawaŋ i denira amawa wulat-wulat iŋ asamaya awĕdi n katĕṅĕra,
mulat pwa saŋ aja aṅdadak sira miṅe sĕmu niŋ awaraha i katĕmwana nira*

muwaḥ wwaya sira ahalĕp rara sujanma pinawulaṅakĕn hana iŋ paṅuṅaṅan,
gaḍiŋ pinakaputra putran ira tan saḥ inarĕk arĕkan saka i nrĕpasuta,
ya teka tumurun hinĕmban iŋ iña amawa sĕrĕḥ arĕnaḥ marĕk ri saŋ aja,
bapa aṅinaṅa rakwa liŋ ra bibi liŋ nikaŋ aṅujarakĕn waśa asĕmu guyu*

pratāpa naranāthaputra kumutug pracalita kadi paṙwwata agni dumilaḥ,
ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ baṅun kusuma sālas anĕḍĕŋ ika kāri tan papĕgatan,
manaḥnya ginĕsĕŋ tĕka iŋ turida rāga nika paḍa hilaŋ syuḥ aṅdadi hawu,
ya teka hinañutnya riŋ nrĕpatiputra sakala sira pöḥ niŋ aṙṇnawa madhu*

manis niŋ ucapan kaka dyaḥ ari liŋnya sinĕpuhan i raśmi niŋ wulat arūm,
ya teka kinabehan iŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ mrĕdu lalita rasanya rāgakaraṇa,
raras-raras i denya miṅgĕk aṅĕnāni n aṅucap api tan wruhĕn hana mulat,
halisnya minahānya molaḥ amaṅun gĕt unĕŋ arĕṅu maṅlare ri saŋ aja*

<indrabajra> 
– – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 11

strī stry-a aṅucap sojaṙ ikā yinuktyan,
liŋnya i narendrātmaja mūḍhabuddhi,
akweḥ sira ṅke nagarī ry-ayodhyā,

yadyan tĕkā dlāha sira i widaṙbbha,
tan suṅsuṅĕn riŋ kakawin wilāpa,
tan kewwa riŋ rāga tĕkap suputrī,
bhagnapratijñā muliha iraŋ eraŋ*

nāhan wuwusnya i naranāthaputra,
ndan rakwa paṙṇnaḥ jaruman gatinya,
wwantĕn suputrī paṅadunya yogya,
maṙmmanya duhkha i saŋ aja n tan ahyun*

paṙṇnaḥ kakanya asrak atuṅga ya ujar,
antĕn hade denta tĕka ujaṙ apyak,
putrī paran tan harĕpa i tuhanku,
hyaŋ niŋ purī towi yayā sira ahyun*

maṅko n mara i śrī naranātha bhoja,
ambĕk nira śri indumatī pakādin,
ghāra apan atyanta wiśeṣaputrī,
sāmantaputrī sira tā maṅadyaḥ*

nāhan sahuṙnya i paṅucap ny-arinya,
bhāwanya miṅgĕk tumikĕl halisnya,
koŋ aṅdĕlö solaḥ ikā n asĕṅhit,
göŋ krodha sojaṙ nika kaṙṇnaśūla*

wwantĕn kili wrĕddha sahuṙ nira atwaŋ,
sajña ibu ni ṅwaŋ kṣama ta ṅhulun dyaḥ,
buddhinta kewalya sumorakĕn saŋ,
sāmantaputri indumatī wiśeṣa*

tan soṙ sira iŋ janma karājaputryan,
riŋ wīṙyya siṅgiḥ sira tan paḍa aḍaḥ,
ndan yogya ghāra apa hiwaŋ nira ibu,
mūlya n minūlyan krama niŋ dadi wwaŋ*

nāhan sahuṙ saŋ wiku wrĕddharūpa,
mĕṅgĕp pratuhw-a asĕmu pakṣapāta,
milw-a ahadeni i sira yan lumampaḥ,
rowaŋ nira agoṣṭhi wulatnya hewa*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

tucapa ŋ wwaŋ i paṅguŋ ika kadi wayaŋ jinajaṙ kinudaŋ,
sakunaŋ-kunaŋ iŋ taliṅa larap i hintĕn ika n kumĕñar,
hana ta aṅadĕg an hayu nika kahiḍĕp kadi modahita,
i kasiṅkab i kenya hana kadi gibaḥ winuluŋ sinurat*

paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ sahana niŋ aṅuṅaŋ mawagĕd wagĕdan,
amanis manisan mata nĕhĕṙ araṅin raṅinan paṅawak,
arupit rupitan susu nĕhĕṙ alĕmĕs lĕmĕsan luṅayan,
sira saŋ sinajinya saŋ aja juga nora muwaḥ kinire*

nrĕpaputra sĕḍĕŋ sapawulatan aweḥ lĕṅĕṅa iŋ aṅuṅaŋ,
tadanantara meḥ lĕpasa laku nira wĕkas iŋ nagara,
amanis kadi tan pĕgata wulat ira i salawaŋ-salawaŋ,
amalaṙ hana niŋ wwaŋ ahaliṅana kori mĕṅā sasisiḥ*

araras rinasan patĕmu nira wulat rasa tan lĕpara,
kalawan saŋ akūŋ alawas i sira kady-awarĕg warĕgan,
apatūtan unĕŋ kasiḥ arĕp inatīta tiniṅgalakĕn,
i layat nira kāri saŋ ahayu wulatnya tinambaŋ ira*

nda atīta sira n kajĕnĕkan akurĕn wulat esy-akadi,
asalin wiṣaya n lĕpas i mukha nikaŋ lĕbuḥ iŋ nagara,
kuṭi śāla lumaṅkuŋ i tĕpi niŋ ayun tirisanya pĕnuḥ,
panĕḍĕŋ ni wuṅūnya mamituturi rāga nira iŋ aṅuṅaŋ*

kadi waḥ surasindhu bala saŋ aja kātatakut gumuruḥ,
ratha rĕṅga padāti kadi parahu söḥ aduluṙ humilī,
gajaḥ aṅgala ghūṙṇnita piraŋ iwu kady-asibū gumuluŋ,
sagĕḍaŋ kahilī gaḍiŋ ika tulalenya lumintaḥ awās*

paḍa bhakti hĕnū nira sakalihatan paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ,
walahaṙnya lawan pahatan asaji mīna sayub cumaḍaŋ,
amapag waṅi niŋ kusuma winawa niŋ pawana mrik arūm,
bhramara asĕmu maṅhaturakĕn i gawenya kiduŋ ri sira*

kadi maṇḍala rāmya ni papupul ikaŋ kayu kayw-asĕkar,
waṅunanya wuṅū sĕḍĕŋ asinaŋ añaṇḍi minerw-aruhur,
humilī wulakanya paḍa caluṅana ika katon humaḍaŋ,
hulu kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕpĕrakĕn ri narendrasuta*

patapan kĕna rāga kayu manis ikā sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,
amapag mata jāti ni mata ni wuluḥ nika tan wriŋ iraŋ,
aḍahĕm haḍawanya rumara rara haṙṣaja denya mulat,
pajajaṙ ni pabañwan ika kapahiriŋ milu kady-aṅaraŋ*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

saŋ aja sira kaṅelan muṅgaḥ riŋ ratha wĕkasan,
saŋ agajaḥ aturaṅga anuṅgaŋ sabhya ciha-ciha,
mwaŋ agiliṅan arampak wwaŋ sāmānya tan ahalĕp,
saŋ aḍarat alara iraŋ kagrĕk grĕk magarawalan*

nrĕpasuta lĕpas eṅgal prāpta iŋ thāni kuluwutan,
satĕka-tĕka ni lampaḥ niŋ wadwa anamun adulur,
i harĕp i wuri lumra anĕṅkw-a ayun manasa nasar,
hawan arupĕk inambaḥ membuḥ lwā kadi tinĕpa*

wukiṙ ajajaṙ ahaṇḍap-haṇḍap śūnya maṅililan,
kadi kukusan amuñjuŋ puñcaknya aṙṇnĕb inululan,
hana talaga riŋ agra ndan wwꜽnya ahaṅĕt ahasin,
pinara paran iŋ adyus baryan landĕp awukiran*

suku-suku nika duṙgga atyanta iwĕḥ nika pinaran,
pinĕga tinĕpa de niŋ molaḥ ṅūni riŋ alawas,
sahaja maliwat i jro ṅka an līla amĕkasi parab,
dadali nika laki strī prāpta anambĕṙ asahuran*

lura-luraḥ aparĕk lwaḥ guṅguŋ wwꜽnya ḍinawuhan,
papupulan ikaŋ aṅhwan ramya aḍöm aṅariŋ-ariŋ,
paḍa marĕk adum uṅgwan yan wwaŋ śreṣṭhi humaliwat,
asila-sila ri piṅgiṙ niŋ māṙgga amalaku sĕrĕḥ*

umaḥ atiśaya denya aporaŋ mĕṅgĕp aṅililan,
wwaŋ ika paḍa humöt riŋ buddhy-a alumbuŋ alit-alit,
tĕka ri sapi nika alit nora akral-kral amĕḍusi,
talaga nika juga alwa aṅlaṅhuy-laṅhuyakĕn agöŋ*

hana ta baṅun amet wwaŋ doṣa n krūra lĕkas ikā,
amawa tali lawan kris pamraŋ mraŋnya habalaṅan,
sapi nika sinikĕpnya aṅrĕñcal maṅlawan agalak,
ri huwus ika katalyan keṇḍit dinwal iŋ aṅulaŋ*

nrĕpatisuta kaluṅha adoḥ śīghra n saha śakaṭa,
karaṇa nira n araryan mwaŋ sakweḥ ni bala nira,
amarĕki pĕkĕn alwā thāny-a agöŋ pakulĕmana,
pira ta puluḥ i dūwanya akweḥ söḥ paḍa winĕgil*

saŋ aja kadi hana i jro rājya apan sira kinĕmit,
sahana-hana nikaŋ saṙwwāstra lwiṙ pinakapagĕr,
ratha turaga tiniṅkaḥ bapra aṅrakṣa sana sini,
makagupura halĕp niŋ mātaṅga aruhuṙ ajajar*

tucapa para kadūwan tuṣṭa n paṅhinĕpan ira,
sahana-hana ri deśanya aneka ŋ paḍa pamapag,
nrĕpasuta sira muṅguḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,
sama humatuṙ aṅanti i soṙ niŋ wāṇḍira magĕlar*

wiku haji jĕnĕk aṅheṙ iŋ śūnya alawas amarāt,
wruḥ aṅaji sira santoṣa aṅdo dohi narapati,
nĕhĕṙ amarahi sāmpun wrĕddha aṅgöŋ ulaḥ alaṅö,
atuha-tuha kadi brĕm santĕn kāku manis ira*

sira ta marĕk aluṅguḥ milw-iŋ dāyaka humatur,
kinasĕgĕhan apan wruḥ ṅūni iŋ rājya sira kabeḥ,
apituwi paḍa rowaŋ-rowaŋ niŋ maṅikĕt-ikĕt,
mukha niŋ aṅucap aśrī de niŋ mojaṙ akakawin*

kṣamakĕna bapa pawwat niŋ grāmya adhama kaluṣa,
padapa hima lawan centĕn mepa alpa lihatana,
sama duwĕga ri rakryan yan twak haywa hali halin,
pinakabañu-bañu ṅke ṅhiŋ yan len juga yan ikā*

wulatana kakudeśanya athāni i gĕgĕṙ asĕpi,
ya tuna-tuna sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ tĕkwan tan hana dinadak,
palapat alas agaryaŋ-garyaŋ tan sawĕgilana,
linĕṅĕṅakĕn iŋ ambĕk maṙmmanya n rĕsĕp alaṅö*

aluru wahu kalahrwan kaywanya n śrawaṇamasa,
asĕpa humuraŋ awyaŋ rurwan ronya kapawanan,
analukati tĕlā wwad niŋ saṙwwatrĕṇa riŋ ayun,
pĕjaḥ amĕkasi kiṅkiŋ luŋ niŋ jaṅga kapanasan*

tĕwĕk i ragas i kaywanya n kaṙwwa araras alaṅö,
tĕṅaḥ i tal ika mambĕt-mambĕt kāṅinan aṅĕliḥ,
manis i lahaŋ ika aṅhiŋ panraŋ-nraŋ wulat amanis,
tiniru tiru niŋ ahyas ronya aṙjja apataḥ akiris*

sĕḍĕŋ iŋ asujimāsa atyanta iŋ kaṣṭa gatarasa,
karikil ika kumĕṇḍĕŋ tūt māṙgga amacĕki suku,
saha panas i hĕnunya adoḥ wwe nora pinalaku,
tuhun amuhara ramyā sakweḥ niŋ wwaŋ ika jĕnĕk*

jalada kadi pĕtĕŋ yan tĕmbe niŋ kapat alaṅö,
jawuḥ amĕkasakĕn rĕm riŋ kaywan hañaṙ asĕmi,
wahu mari panaṅis niŋ kālaṅkyaŋ sukha sumayab,
asiga kadi tinambaŋ wahw-i inantukan agiraŋ*

trĕṇa taru paḍa mĕltik wījanya n masa kalima,
wawaŋ aluru kapiṅrĕs tūt māṙgga aṅĕliḥ alume,
linaran i kĕñaṙ iŋ wꜽ yan luṅhā ŋ rĕmĕŋ anisiḥ,
kadi pamanas i kuŋ niŋ kanyā dūra n atĕlĕba*

hañaṙ abañu tĕgalnya n kānĕm tapwan acarĕcĕḥ,
kadi sinipatan apriḥ māṙgganya aracĕk abĕnĕr,
turaḥ i wĕrĕḥ ikaŋ waṙṣa asat kāri kasarakat,
asĕmu pupuṙ areḥ tūt piṅgiṙ niŋ halis inamĕr*

brata nika ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ māgha adyus rahina wĕṅi,
jawuḥ aṅapitu tan pāntya adrĕs maṅkin akĕcĕhan,
aṅura ṅuraṅi teja hyaŋ candra aṙkka kaginĕman,
sukha salabuḥ ikaŋ luṅlūṅan māri kapiṅĕliḥ*

lĕbug i palĕmahanya ajro riŋ phālguna puraci,
patuna tunahan iŋ lĕmbw-a asaŋsiŋ tahi papuṅĕn,
dwijawara sira baryan rĕŋrĕŋ mogha humaliwat,
sumĕpĕṙ anasi pöhan maṙmmanya n śuci wĕkasan*

masa kasaṅa tĕka traŋ ndan mātra anĕlani jawuḥ,
ya karaṇa ni latĕknya atiṅgaṙ wahw-asat anisiḥ,
sapapikatana göṅĕn tĕmbe niŋ manuk agalak,
tuhun asĕpi hĕnūnya lwīṙ agriŋ paḍa caciṅĕn*

kusuma sahana māywan yan wꜽśākha paḍa wijaḥ,
sĕkaṙ iŋ asana kantun kady-ahyun kalarakĕna,
paṅirim-irim ikaŋ waṙṣa aheṙ weḥ ayu ḍumawuḥ,
kadi jaruman aṅinte rāga anīs amawa taṅis*

muwaḥ asĕkaṙ alasnya jyeṣṭha amiṅrwani sahapit,
tuhun aṅuraṅi rurwan de niŋ waṙṣa wahu muliḥ,
tura-turaḥ i gĕrĕḥnya agupyan meḥ amĕkasana,
tuna-tuna kadi pamwit niŋ haṙṣa amĕkasi taṅis*

analahasa laṅönya iŋ āṣādha aṅlarani kawi,
paḍa gumigil aṅinkin tiṅhalnya aniliṅi tawaŋ,
kamaḍiḍiṅĕn aṅepw-i i roganya aṅgĕgĕs aṅĕsaḥ,
kadi kahapit aṅunṅun muṅgw-iŋ śūnya kakilatan*

nahan ucapan ira mpuṅkw-aṅde haṙṣa ri saŋ aja,
wĕṅi mara sakamantyan prāpta aneka taḍaḥ ira,
dwijawara sira māliḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,
para wiku juga kāry-a agoṣṭhi mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya*

paḍahi marĕk agupyan śabdanya amanis inamĕr,
kadi paṅucap ucap niŋ muṅgw-i jro jinĕm akule,
apituwi sinameni iŋ gīta śrī nrĕpatanaya,
rasa nika winiweka aneka ŋ pālapan amanis*

tucapa bala nira akweḥ bhāwanya n paṅinum inum,
aṅigĕl aṅiduŋ asraŋ twaknya akweḥ kadi humilī,
paḍahi nika gumĕntĕṙ sinraŋ niŋ tabĕ tabĕhan,
kadi baribina saŋ hyaŋ riŋ swaṙgga atukupa kapö*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

luṅhā ŋ māsa piliḥ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi tiḍĕm sahana niŋ aṅinum paḍa aturū,
tistis nora mumik tuhun saŋ aja tan mrĕm amaṅu-maṅu tan kĕna iŋ turū,
aṅhiŋ rāmya rinĕṅwakĕn panalimuṙ nalimuṙ ira ri kiṅkiŋ iŋ hati,
gĕṇḍiŋ walyan arūm swaranya karĕṅö sawĕṅi kiniduṅan kiduŋ buwun*

loṙ wetan pamalantĕnan kaparĕk iŋ lwaḥ adalĕm asamīpa paṅdyunan,
wwaŋnya awuṅw-amasaŋ damaṙ wruḥ i masanya n amalu-malu meḥ tibā ṅĕnĕm,
tan paśrī swara niŋ palu dyun asarag tĕwas amaribini ŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,
endaḥ mwaŋ palu wastra rāmya kadi de niŋ amalu daluwaŋ rinĕṅwakĕn*

aṅdyun kaṙwwa rabinya tan padiwasa awiḍiṅan awurahan siliḥ cacad,
nitya ŋ śabda paḍa iṅgal asrak amalĕs hinalan uliḥ ika agawe ghaṭa,
strīnya amet parihāra tan wĕdi kadūṣana n ahala gawe nikā paṭa,
kahyun-hyun kadi śꜽwa sogata mapaṅghaṭapaṭa juga hetu niŋ humuŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ baṇija iŋ tĕpas paḍa sumambutakĕn i sagawe nika alawas,
nora apĕk paḍa lobha lābha kaharĕpnya n akuṭa kaṭikan paḍa adamar,
saṅkĕp dwalnya huwus ratĕŋ paḍa sumaṅgraha wijila niki n mara iŋ pĕkĕn,
asyaŋ-syaŋ karĕṅö humuŋ saṅa saṅanya sĕmu niŋ aharĕp katumbasa*

eñjiŋ wāhu huwus ḍawuḥ pitu muni ŋ paḍahi baṅun akon adandana,
sakweḥ niŋ prajurit paḍa amuṅu ri paṅhawin ika kamĕnanya maṅkata,
aṙddha iñjiŋ pwa hiḍĕpnya tĕkwan apuyĕŋ ya ta karaṇa nika aturū muwaḥ,
ṅhiŋ maṅkat saŋ aja akĕmul kĕmul alañciṅan aṅarahakĕn saka iŋ ratha*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ ri sira marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
prajñā tan kasilib ri tiṅkaḥ iŋ asewaka maṅinakana iŋ tuhan-tuhan,
wruḥ riŋ yogya kahĕnwa de nira tinūt sapawaraḥ ika rāmya tūt gĕgĕr,
yekā rakwa hĕnūnya ṅūni n aṅaliḥ saha jaruman ika amĕgat gunuŋ*

śūnya aporaŋ ikaŋ gĕgĕṙ hana guhā rĕbaḥ adalĕm arĕs twas iŋ mulat,
tan pātmā ŋ aṅuṅaŋ hanan kadi hana aṅduhuṅakĕna tĕkā saka iŋ wuri,
tistis nora mara aṅṅṅĕŋ ri pataninya paḍa kadi sinaṅgan iŋ kawi,
ṅhiŋ raṅrö gumĕrĕḥ tinūb niŋ aṅin adrĕs aniru gĕrĕḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat*

ṅkāna i lĕmbaḥ ika alaṅö pamaḍĕkan wwaŋ ika wija wijaḥ paḍa aṅayar,
lumra akweḥ aputiḥ wuyaḥnya kasawuṙ sumarasaḥ anamaṙ wway-iŋ jawuḥ,
awrā tampĕṙ ika agĕlaṙ kasarakat sarakat asĕmu sāri niŋ puḍak,
haṙṣa ambĕk saŋ aja n tĕka awuya wuyaḥ mata tuwin aharip kadi inusap*

tambak-tambak akaṇḍa loṙ kidul i pomahan ika kadi piṇḍa niŋ sawaḥ,
wwaŋnya arampak amet wĕlut kadi pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ aṅurit katiṅhalan,
pakṣinya agĕŋ agĕŋ humuŋ kadi kĕbo paṅulaḥ awurahan siliḥ buru,
yan kawrĕg paḍa möṙ gumĕntĕṙ anamaṙ gĕrĕḥ iŋ adurugan paḍa awĕrö*

abhrā lwiṙ sĕkaṙ iŋ laṅit braja katon pamĕwĕḥ i supit iŋ sahiŋ-sahiŋ,
aṅjraḥ tan kahanan lĕwas pasuŋ ika asira-sira kadi kĕmbaŋ iŋ karaŋ,
lwiṙ luŋ niŋ katiraḥ miraḥ ni suṅut iŋ huraŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ mara iŋ lumut,
tūt māṙgga aharĕmis pĕjaḥ kadi mĕnuṙ saka salawĕ lawö sumamburat*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

sāmpun lĕpas ratha narendrasuta apan adrĕs,
saŋ brāhmaṇa i wuri lawan rĕṣi śꜽwa boddha,
agyā paḍa anututi tan hana kāry-araryan,
muṅgw-iŋ gaja aśwa ratha masraŋ alumba-lumba*

lwaḥ naṙmmadā katĕmu de naranāthaputra,
saŋ brāhmaṇa asabha sabhā ri ya sāri-sāri,
atyanta niṙmmala paṅawruhana i śucinya,
maṙmmanya n uttama wijilnya saka iŋ śaśāṅka*

söḥ puṣpa laywan iŋ atīṙtha hana i hĕnīnya,
kuntul paḍa aṅadĕg adĕg ri pacaṙ-pacaṙnya,
līlā ḍarā ri kalakānya wijaḥ paḍa adyus,
akweḥ mayūra maṅigĕl ri pasiṙ-pasiṙnya*

ṅkāna n pararyan arahup naranāthaputra,
muṅgw-iŋ aśoka sira tan mari śokacitta,
nyū danta medi ri manaḥ nira keṅin-eṅin,
kāṅgĕk sira anĕmu puḍak maṅuḍoḍa riŋ wwꜽ*

nya ŋ cakrawāka paḍa rāmya mahimya himyan,
ṅkāna i saroruha wĕkasnya lawan priyanya,
manda swaranya karĕṅö nira tan sphuṭa arūm,
winrĕg nira apa ta kalīṅa ni de nira amrĕg*

haṅśa aputiḥ ri tĕṅaḥ adyus aṅumbaŋ-umbaŋ,
kombak tinūb iŋ aṅin adrĕs aṅiṅgĕk iṅgĕk,
moga araras-raras arūm karĕṅö swaranya,
kady-a awaraḥ yan alaṅö ri hananya riŋ wwꜽ*

wadwā nira aduluṙ i piṅgiṙ aḍanta-ḍanta,
akweḥ lĕpas paḍa kahañjuṙ adoḥ lakunya,
maṅsul muwaḥ saha padāti tinuṇḍa pājar,
Āpan kinonakĕn aṅantya makuwwa  kuwwa*

śīghra agawe grĕhalatā mrik arūm sĕkaṙnya,
nora akawö paḍa wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅwan,
andul wuṅū mwaŋ asana aṅjraḥ i piṅgiṙ iŋ lwaḥ,
ramya alaṅö pinarĕkanya hanan pamaṅguŋ*

ndaḥ riŋ samantaji hana adbhuta mūṙtti niŋ hyaŋ,
mātaṅgarūpa pinakāṙggaḍa riŋ wanādri,
siṅha aṅḍapuṙ wĕdi manambaḥ arĕs tumon ya,
Ꜽrāwaṇa anurun ujaṙ niŋ anaṙkka naṙkka*

ri lwaḥ sabhānya sĕḍĕŋ adyus ahilya hilyan,
nora ŋ bhaya iriya putus wuhaya aluṅa aṅlwaŋ,
aṅlaṅhuy-adrĕs anamaṙ gajamīna mĕtta,
himpĕṙ karaŋ liman i kāla nika aṅalimpuŋ*

ambö ni meda ni gajaḥ naranāthaputra,
sākṣāt inambuŋ ika hetu nika bhramanta,
abyūran iŋ lwaḥ alĕtuḥ kakĕbuṙ bañunya,
wit niŋ saroja kadahut kalawan sĕkaṙnya*

mĕntas pwa ya aṅadĕg aṅuṅgul i tīra niŋ lwaḥ,
gaṅgĕŋ lawan sarasija aṅhibĕki ry-awaknya,
mĕtta awĕrö nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ aghaṇṭa kambaŋ,
abhrā katiṅhalan ikā kadi nāgapuṣpa*

meww-i iwu saṅkhya ni gajaḥ naranāthaputra,
ndātan pamaṙppati ri göŋnya lawan guṇanya,
awrĕg saka i taṅan alaḥ ḍyam api n rinukrak,
Āpan swabhāwa niŋ alit juga ta n tinaṅgĕl*

strī-strī paḍa aṅhili lawan raray-anwam-anwam,
adrĕs lakunya karikil kawĕdinya ṅūni,
maṅke n tĕka iŋ bhaya sukĕt rwi yayān inambaḥ,
wet niŋ takut pati susup-susupi iŋ alas göŋ*

akweḥ mara iŋ tahĕn anuṅtuŋ amet upāya,
watw-i inuluṙnya sagĕnuk sawaluḥ salumpaŋ,
tĕṇḍas nikaŋ liman awās tinujunya tan len,
tog toṙ ndatan dwa katibān dan ikaŋ śilā syuḥ*

krodha ŋ liman mata nika aṅdrĕŋ anon wwaŋ akweḥ,
riŋ kāywan aṅhabalaŋ iŋ kayu kayw-aganti,
yeka n tumandaŋ aṅayuḥ paŋ agöŋ katuṅkul,
syāk pok rĕbaḥ ri walakaŋnya baṅun rinĕṅgan*

wadwā nrĕpātmaja masĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,
sāra akusāra śaraṇāśraya wāni riŋ praŋ,
krūra akihal-kihal agöŋ karawalya timbul,
śūrabrata asira siran paḍa tan dadi jriḥ*

yeka aṅlawan paḍa marĕk pinupul sĕmutnya,
kweḥnya apramāṇa satasik ya ta paṅhaḍanya,
ambĕk nikaŋ gaja mamatyana nora wāni,
göŋnya aprameya sagunuŋ ya ta paṅgajaḥnya*

māsö hana iŋ ratha narendrasuta aṅagĕm hrū,
laṅkap hana i kiwa huwus pinasaŋ talinya,
sāmpun minantran inayat saha hastiśikṣā,
saṙ cĕb tiba aṅĕnani kumbha nikaŋ gajendra*

sāmpun kĕna amriḥ aṅusī pulihan tumandaŋ,
ndan saṙwwasandhi ni śarīra nika agraḥ aṅrĕs,
yeka n paṅohan aṅadĕg mati tan pasāra,
goṙ bhoḥ tibā kadi śilādri rĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*

waṅkenya sakṣaṇa hananya kadi iŋ paṅipyan,
teja prakīṙṇna dumilaḥ tĕka tan pasaṅkan,
widyādhara ahalĕp adĕṇḍa hana i tĕṅaḥnya,
utpatti niŋ dwirada māti mahāprabhāwa*

kalpadruma mrik inalapnya pamuṙṣitanya,
lwiṙ puṣpawaṙṣa tumiba i naranāthaputra,
Āścaṙyya buddhi nira sādara de nira aṅliŋ,
hyaŋ-hyaŋ paran kari kita syapa tā ṅaranta*

<waṅśastha> 
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏓ : 12

kĕnoḥ patakwanta ri tiṅkaḥ i ṅhulun,
ṅhulun kasaṅkhya n maṅaran priyambada,
swaputra saŋ citraratha prakāśita,
sira adigandhaṙwwapati i kadewatan*

ṅhulun saka iŋ swaṙgga wiśāta lālana,
anuṅga nuṅgal mahas iŋ wanāntara,
tĕka iŋ pasiṙ tan hana tan kalaṅlaṅan,
laṅö niŋ ambĕk saparan tinūtakĕn*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

ṅke naṙmmadā ṅhulun acaṅkrama sāri-sāri,
kañcit kapaṅgiḥ aṅadĕg bhagawān pataṅga,
pakṣa adyusa apatĕlĕsan tumuluy-mara iŋ lwaḥ,
mogha ṅhulun tumurun aṅruhuri i sira adyus*

göŋ krodha wākcala sira n panibāni śāpa,
oyuḥ gajaḥ tĕmahanamwa maran mari hyaŋ,
ṅke ta uṅgwanamwa tan adoḥ ya saka irikiŋ lwaḥ,
nāhan wĕkas ni paṅucap nira kaṙṇnaśūla*

tan mithya ri ṅhulun ikaŋ gajamĕttarūpa,
byakta an asaṇḍuta ŋ ujaṙ yan anĕṅgaḥ alwā,
saṅka iŋ amaṅgiḥ i wuyuŋ bhagawān pataṅga,
tapwan śināpa tumuluy-matĕmaḥ gajendra*

an maṅkana bwat i wuyuŋ bhagawān pataṅga,
kāruṇya buddhi nira riŋ wĕkasan sira asiḥ,
Āpan ṅhulun marĕk anĕmbaḥ apinta kāsiḥ,
maṅhyaŋ ry-anugraha nira i rikaŋ antaśāpa*

mojaṙ sira asĕmu manis tĕkap iŋ tumiṅhal,
 Om  haywa saṅśaya ri siddha niŋ antaśāpa,
tan lupta yan tĕka hĕlĕm saŋ aja ahawan ṅke,
tuṅtuŋ ni sañjata nikā hawananta mantuk*

sāmpun sira amĕkasakĕn wacana antaśāpa,
luṅhā sira ṅhulun aṅanti humeṙ tĕkanta,
sowenta tan tĕka ya kāraṇa niŋ bhramanta,
mĕtta awĕrö pira piraŋ tahunĕn byamoha*

maṅke n ḍatĕŋ kita saha aśwa sahasra saṅkhya,
ṅke naṙmmada awija wijaḥ sawatĕk watĕkta,
mātĕṅga papraŋ aṅiriŋ paḍa sāra śūra,
mawrĕg rĕbaḥ binuru ni ṅhulun iŋ paḍöman*

aṅhiŋ kita amanaḥ anuṅsuŋ iŋ astra tīkṣṇa,
syuḥ kumbha ni ṅhulun ikā tinut iŋ paratra,
ndātan paniṣphala wawaŋ maluya adadi hyaŋ,
sākṣāt kita amrĕta wijil nikaŋ antaśāpa*

atyanta göŋ ni hutaŋ i ṅhulun apramāṇa,
saṅmohana ŋ pamalĕsa i kita diwyaśāstra,
gandhaṙwwaśāstra pinajöŋ hyaŋ asañjata ika,
jñānanta maṅṅpasakĕn saha mantra siddhi*

atyanta yogya yan ajinta ya kawruhanta,
kārādhananya saha mantra saha indikanya,
pöṅpöŋ ṅhulun wruḥ i wĕkas ni rusit-rusitnya,
śaktinya kawruhan anambĕhana i guṇanta*

ndātan pamatyani guṇanya yadin guṇanta,
śatrw-a adhama apituwi tan mati denya mūṙccha,
mogha aturū sahana niŋ ripu tan wri rātnya,
nistanya maṅkana yayā kita yan jaya iŋ praŋ*

he saŋ priyambada kita n paṅutus paṅajya,
mogha awiraŋ hulun apan gumawe laranta,
ṅūni i sĕḍĕṅta matĕmaḥ gajamattarūpa,
tan len ṅhulun kaṅaranan karaṇanta māti*

hā-hāḥ hade saŋ aja denta manaṅgaḥ eraŋ,
an sāhasa amĕjahi ri ṅhulunĕn gajendra,
Āpan prasiddha kita maṅhwatakĕn kajanman,
atyanta göŋ i hutaŋ i ṅhulunĕn maluy-hyaŋ*

yadyan sabhūṙ bhuwaḥ ikaŋ guṇa kawruhanta,
tātan sadoṣa yan atambĕha wīṙyya saswaḥ,
ndā maṅkanā kita n aṅajya wimohanāstra,
taṅgap nihan hila-hila ŋ tumulak paweweḥ*

an saŋ priyambada kĕdö maṅutus maṅajya,
mary-a awiraŋ saŋ aja sāmpun atiṅkaḥ uṅgwan,
loṙ saŋ priyambada kidul saŋ aja atalaṅkup,
saṅmohana inaji nira iṅgal apan widagdha*

sandhinya kāku saha śakti ni dewatanya,
saṅyoga niŋ śarawara mwaŋ ikā tujunya,
sāmpun tama stuti nikā saha kūṭamantra,
saṅhāramantra paḍa kawruḥ ira prabheda*

wruḥ saŋ priyambada ri haṙṣa narendraputra,
an pembuḥ astra śara sūkṣma mahāprabhāwa,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ apraŋ inucap nira mogha jambat,
amwit sira asĕmu manis baśa de niŋ ojar*

he mitra mantuka kakanta lumarya maṅke,
siddhā ŋ prayojana kita n ḍatĕṅa iŋ widaṙbbha,
nāhan wuwus nira nĕhĕṙ maṅagĕm sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,
luṅha ahawan gagana mĕltuk apan sira hyaŋ*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

sāmpun prāpta sira iŋ surālaya wicitraratha paḍa sukha n tumon sira,
ndan saŋ kāri kamānuṣan hĕla hĕla aṅucap ucap i sĕḍĕŋ nira apupul,
nistanya n tama de nira aṅaji tathāpi salahasa ri saŋ priyambada,
yan tĕṅhā kadi tan tumuṅkula sawet ni karakĕtan ira aṅdĕlö tawaŋ*

sandhyākāla pasaŋ damaṙ nrĕpatiputra manaḍaḥ i huwus nira ajapa,
eñjiŋ pūṙwwaka saŋ priyambada ginoṣṭhi nira mahuwusan tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,
wahw-amrĕm tumuluy-tinaṅhi sira maṅkat asalĕsĕk i tīra niŋ nadī,
gĕntĕṙ ni grit ikaŋ ratha amĕkarakĕn kucup iŋ asana rāmya tūt hĕnū*

eñjiŋ kāla nira n tĕka iŋ pasiṙ alasnya pĕtĕŋ asĕmu śeṣa niŋ wĕṅi,
lwiṙ haṙṣā gagana asĕgĕḥ pawulatanya gĕrĕḥ ika kadi priyambada,
mogha aśrī kumĕḍap kilatnya nĕhĕṙ aṅluru-luru kadi medi maṅdu lor,
kady-a anĕmbahakĕn sĕkaṙ niŋ asana anisi huyaŋ i riris nika aṅdadak*

mambö sāgara rāmya niŋ laṅit awaṙṇna tali hurut urutnya tan pĕgat,
