kālaṅkyaŋnya baṅun jukuŋ niŋ amayaŋ lĕyĕp i lari nika amaḍĕm ḍarat,
kuntul möṙ kadi tuṇḍan iŋ banawa kāri tan ilu kajahat lana alayar,
saŋ hyaŋ candra baṅun bahitra ḍatĕŋ iŋ kulĕm amawa śaśā mara i jawa*

megha lwiṙ karaŋ iŋ laṅit kadi wĕrĕḥ limut ika ri sare nika aputiḥ,
wahw-a amīt i kuwuŋ-kuwuŋnya sawaneḥ karĕrĕban akucĕm pĕgat-pĕgat,
gĕntĕṙnya awurahan humuŋ kadi katunwan i larap i kilat nikā murub,
runtuḥ piṅgiṙ ika atĕmaḥ jawuḥ anūtakĕn aṅin alaṅö tiba anisiḥ*

rāmya lwiṙ siluman karaŋ ri mukha niŋ muhara paḍa paḍa aṅhapit bañu,
alwā tiṅkaḥ i mekhalanya ri tĕṅaḥ paṅadĕg adĕgan iŋ mara aṅṅṅĕŋ,
kaṙwwa anuṅgul apāntaran sapaṅuhuḥ kadi gupura śiwak saka iŋ adoḥ,
lwiṙ hambal sphaṭika aŋ alun turunan iŋ kawi pĕjaḥ atuha aṅhañut laṅö*

priṅga ahrit tĕpi niŋ samudra kadi paṅhinĕpan i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ labuḥ kapat,
lwiṙ prāsāda pukaḥ karaŋ ni paraṅanya hana kadi siluṅluŋ iŋ kawi,
Ꜽṙttambaŋnya baṅun wwit iŋ truḥ asĕwö kilat awilĕt alūŋ awaṅkawa,
lumra awaṙṇna rĕṅit kukusnya sinawat sawat inidĕran iŋ guruṇḍaya*

miṅgut piṇḍa nikaŋ karaŋ liman anuṅkuli paraṅan i piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik,
lwiṙ molaḥ tulale nika amijilakĕn bañu kadi paṅanak niŋ eṙttali,
kahyun-hyun kumucuṙ parĕŋ rwa tumĕḍun lĕṅĕŋ aṅĕnani tiṅhas iŋ karaŋ,
rĕmpū syuḥ amĕniṙ-mĕniṙ kadi tinapyan iŋ aṅin aputiḥ sumamburat*

paṇḍan māti lĕṅĕŋ sumuṇḍay-akaraŋ hulu karaŋ i sare nikaŋ pasir,
sakweḥ niŋ bhramara anaṅis paḍa sumuṅkĕm aṅarĕki sĕkaṙ huwus lĕwas,
dinyūs iŋ truḥ i saṅhub iŋ jaladhi saŋsaya lĕṅĕŋ arurub rurub limut,
hemanya anwam arūm puḍak nika tumūt pĕjaḥ i turuŋ ika atulis ṭikā*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

nyū danta asĕpi tuṅga tuṅgal aṅadĕg muṅgw-i i rĕṅat niŋ trĕbis,
lĕŋlĕŋnya n hana riŋ pasiṙ siliḥ awe lāwan ṙyyak iŋ sāgara,
tan wruḥ yan tinulis parab sahana niŋ wwaḥnya akĕmul nīrada,
de niŋ laṅw-anaput katuṅkul i laṅö niŋ nūsa mukṣa n rĕrĕb*

<śikhariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ : 17

mahantĕn sāk riñcuŋ lĕṅĕŋ i tĕpi niŋ sāgara lĕyĕp,
palambaŋnya akweḥ nora wĕnaṅa wacan śīṙṇna lamukĕn,
tulisnya anuṅgal wikw-acĕpuḥ atalaṅkup katuruhan,
tumuṅkul bhāwanya aḍĕku ḍĕkuḥ apiṇḍa anasi hatĕp*

ikaŋ prāsāda syuḥ karahan apa teka amarikala,
tiba i piṅgiṙ niŋ sāgara kasiḥ arĕp hyaŋ gaṇapati,
katampwan de niŋ ṙyyak mata nira kumĕmbĕŋ kadi lumuḥ,
mulat kady-ahyun wuṅwakĕna sira yan kāla hasila*

karaŋ sawwaŋ muṅgw-iŋ jaladhi mapa mūlanya ta kunaŋ,
wilĕt niŋ megha ry-a awak ika sagibaḥ tan pinahuwus,
winaswās kady-a anabraṅa sĕmu nika aṅlaṅhwiy-anĕṅaḥ,
baṅun bhrānta amaṅgiḥ pasiṙ aharĕp aṅlimbaṅa laṅö*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

banawa kajahat iŋ lod biṅkas de niŋ alun agöŋ,
tihaŋ ika gumalaṅgaŋ muṅgw-iŋ tuṇḍan ika marĕk,
kadi ta pamĕkulanya n māsiḥ tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ,
sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ līṅanya n wruḥ aṅucapa*

wukiṙ anak anĕlat riŋ wwꜽ niŋ sāgara ri tĕṅaḥ,
kadi sakadaṅa lāwan wwaŋ mūṙcchā kawi pasisi,
sĕmu-sĕmu nika sānak lāwan ṙyyak jĕnĕk aharas,
pili-piliḥ abapenduŋ truḥ-truḥ māṙgga nika lĕṅĕŋ*

layaṙ iŋ amayaŋ akweḥ ṅkāna i soṙnya humaliwat,
karahan aburu maṙmmanya n kedĕṙ nĕhĕṙ awĕlaḥ,
dhwatala rayuŋ ika anraŋ lumrā söḥ paṅanan ika,
bañak aṅidĕri nūsā kāraŋnya n midĕṙ alaṅö*

patani kadi jamuṙ syuŋ rūpanya amanis atulis,
kalimutan i siluk niŋ groŋ-groŋ iŋ paraṅan arĕs,
kakawin ika palambaŋ riŋ lambaŋ cinacahakĕn,
cĕcĕk ika hana tan saḥ muny-asriŋ baṅun amaca*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

māry-a amet lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ nrĕpatiputra lumaris ahawan gunuŋ-gunuŋ,
ambö niŋ pakis ĕṇḍaḥ iŋ walahaṙ aṅṅwihi waṅi ni gandha niŋ pupur,
mogha arūm sirarā nikaŋ kayu ragas kadi hulĕs apulaŋ lawan burat,
sakweḥ niŋ kahalintaṅan rumimaŋ ambĕk ira winulatan paḍa alaṅö*

paṇḍan suṇḍay-asoŋ latāṅkura paranti para kawi mahas lana apikat,
paŋ niŋ campaka śuddhi guṇḍik aṅilo ri harĕp ika maṅuṅkul uṅkuli,
luṅlūṅanya tikĕl-tikĕl katitihan papikatan agĕnĕt hibĕk hĕlar,
tan śobha ŋ kitiran jaraḥ pili piliḥ luput alara kasambĕt iŋ habĕt*

wwantĕn rāmya kadewagurwan aṅuṅaŋ jaladhi kadi kalaṅwan iŋ tulis,
saŋ muṅgw-i iriya tan wĕnaŋ lumagani indriya nira kawĕnaŋ binañcana,
paṅliṅgāna sawaŋ-sawaŋ ni hayu ni idĕman ira sĕmu niŋ warāpsarī,
kady-a aṅanti ri sāmpunanya n apatūtan aniliba mara iŋ surālaya*

ṅkāna iŋ bwat halu sāk durenya kahanan nrĕpatanaya tumiṅhal iŋ tulis,
heman waṙṇna nika asamun katuruhan lutuṙ asamun inambaḥ iŋ cĕcĕk,
ṅhiŋ dewī kawĕkas lawan kili paḍa aṅadĕg adĕg abĕbĕd bĕbĕd hati,
kady-a aminta tumūta rūpa nika buddhi saŋ aja hiḍĕpan kamānuṣan*

ṅkāna i rĕmbaṅan iŋ juraŋ mpu tapa rāmya mamuluku katuṅku tuṅkulan,
wuṅkal kedĕran aṅjĕlag sadĕdĕg iŋ sapi kaparĕk i piṅgiṙ iŋ galĕŋ,
lĕmbunya an ahĕle hĕli n palayanan pawulatan ika de nikaŋ watu,
asrak waṅsulan iŋ kiya atrĕt alaṅö lĕṅĕŋ araras aniṙwwa niṙwakĕn*

nyāsa lwiṙ minahā gunuŋ pinakapājaran aṅadĕg i madhya niŋ juraŋ,
lwīṙ apwī kumukus miraḥ ni kayu teja nika kasaputan hima aputiḥ,
wwꜽ saṅka iŋ paraṅan ya kadrĕsan aṅin kadi siniramakĕn sumamburat,
saŋ wrĕddhaṙṣi katon iŋ agra sawaŋ aṙcca lamukĕn alaṅö kasaṅhuban*

siṅgiḥ kottaman iŋ wanāśrama sabhā saŋ ataki-taki niṣparigraha,
kaywanya awruḥ acandana apriḥ atĕṅö jawa huwi kusuma aṅjraḥ iŋ talun,
kālaṅkyaŋnya lĕyĕp wiśāta baṅun ahyun atapa riŋ aṅin huwus lĕpas,
saŋ hyaŋ lek sumĕnö prakāśa śuci śukla pinakasuluḥ iŋ hana iŋ wukir*

tan saḥ riŋ daluwaŋ kukap nika subaddha sĕkaṙ ikaŋ uluṙ paḍa ajaṭā,
wrenya aṅalwaŋ ikaŋ warāha wana tan parabi sukha manambi riŋ tahĕn,
mwaŋ saṙppa atapa tāpan abrata lana aṅaluṣa puyuḥ ika akipū-kipū,
niṙdhūma ŋ balĕman lumöŋ barĕbĕk iŋ kayu pinaṅan ika n hana iŋ alas*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

buddhi nrĕpatisuta jĕnĕk ya kāraṇa nira aṅrĕwĕŋ alas akulĕm,
sakweḥ nira saŋ ajaṙ-ajaṙ marĕk saha kilaŋ hinaturakĕn ira,
ramya aṅucap i sakaharĕp nira iŋ phala nikaŋ tapa ginawayakĕn,
eñjiŋ sira tumurun atūt alas wahu tinoṙ pinakapatalĕsan*

deśa asĕpi hawan ira kālasan sipi kaniṣṭha nika gatarasa,
aṅluḥ wwaŋ ika pinanasan ḍinaṇḍa sinipat layat apalarasan,
akweḥ pahutaṅan i sawaḥ gaganya paḍa tan hana maṅinak-inak,
lumbuŋnya kasiḥ arĕp aninya ya n milu katuṅkĕb alawas aṅariŋ*

akweḥ wray-anusup anukĕt nukĕt baṅun amet kayu parĕŋ adulur,
ḍaṅḍaŋnya lumĕkas aṅatĕṙ sĕsĕḥ kaṅĕlihan sawaŋ aṅipil-ipil,
pakṣinya palatuk amaduŋ-maduŋ kahiḍĕpanya n amahayu kuwuŋ,
wwaḥ niŋ kamalagi tumatiŋ katon kadi caluk niŋ anutu nutuhi*

kācāṙyyan alawas inatīta śīṙṇna pamicāran ika katuruhan,
riñcuŋ saka nika sasisiḥ siliḥ jaga murantak aṅĕmuki parab,
nora akṣara kakawin i paṅlarinya paḍa tan hana katĕmu lĕbur,
ṅhiŋ candana kasirat agātra mātra ri tawiŋnya kari kadi panu*

jöŋ niŋ giri gahana kadewagurwan ahalĕp lura-luraḥ arĕnĕb,
strī-strī dwijakula śuci śuddha saŋ pinakamaṅgala niŋ anaruka,
tūs niŋ wulakan aṅali mekalanya śatapattra nika mĕkaṙ arūm,
sakweḥ niŋ amaṅan i lumutnya rakwa cinacad puru-puru katalu*

<śikhariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ : 17

byatītan meḥ prāpta iŋ nagara saŋ aja aṅel bala nira,
araryan ṅkāna i jro kuṭi katĕmu sakweḥ para wiku,
tinamwī tamwī riŋ sĕḍĕṅan amanis de nira mulat,
apan prāya ŋ wastw-alpa maṅinaki yan riŋ sĕḍĕŋ aṅel*

wiwakṣan sakweḥ saŋ para ratu hinundaŋ paḍa tĕka,
paḍa akuṇḍaŋ gĕṇḍiŋ gumĕrĕḥ asĕluṙ tan papĕgatan,
tuwin paṅhrik niŋ tuṅgaṅan asahuran lāgi karĕṅö,
ikaŋ sattwa alöŋ śabda nika baṅun asyaŋ syaŋ aṅuhuḥ*

kaḍatwan saŋ bhoja atiśaya mara göŋnya aparamita,
yaya ahöt maṅke kāṙyya nira ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ para ratu,
pĕnuḥ tamwī tamwi i sahana para taṇḍa alana ṅiwö,
tĕka iŋ māṙgga agöŋ nora pinakapahidwan paḍa hibĕk*

ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ sāgara kahibĕkan wwaŋ kadi bañu,
karaŋ mātaṅga akāra ni liman ika aneka majajar,
baṅun ṙyyak polaḥ niŋ dhwaja kagurilap kadrĕsan aṅin,
curik wahwas patrĕm lumarap asĕmu praŋ-praŋ agalak*

sanistanya n tan waspada wiṣaya niŋ śabda karĕṅö,
tĕkap niŋ gĕṇḍiŋ mwaŋ grĕbĕg i laku niŋ wwaŋ mapapagan,
yaya ataḥ wrĕtta śrī raghusuta karĕṅw-an sira tĕka,
wulat herĕn taŋ wwaŋ sanagara paḍa alaḥ rĕṅĕ rĕṅön*

lumampaḥ saŋ bhoja amapag i saŋ aja apan sira tĕka,
kasuṅsuŋ riŋ māṙgga aṅucap-ucap aluṅguḥ paḍa sukha,
parĕŋ maṅkat ramya aduluṙ iniriŋ iŋ wwaŋ sanagara,
ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ bĕntara mukha nika an aṙddha marupĕk*

umaḥ niŋ taṇḍa agöŋ pinakapasĕnāha i nrĕpasuta,
kulĕm saŋ hyaŋ sandhyā diwasa niŋ amūja ajapa-japa,
tĕka ŋ pamyāpāra i sira wijil ikaŋ sāgara wukir,
ndatan waṙṇnan tiṅkaḥ ni panaḍaḥ ira akweḥ cinarita*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

tiṅkaḥ śri indumatī n kapiŋ tiga nira n piniḍuḍuk i dalĕm kathākĕna,
akweḥ pañcabale ri wiṅkiṅan ikaŋ pamiḍuḍukan i soṙ huwus hibĕk,
de niŋ strī paḍa hinyasan cumuriga inunus awak ika waṙṇna sañjata,
byakta akūṅa kalĕṅgaka iŋ panulisan puḍak ikaŋ anulad raras nika*

twas niŋ megha dinadyakĕn waṅunan uttama pinahuwus iŋ labuḥ kapat,
tumpaŋ pitw-aruhuṙ sinaptabhuwana aparimita kalaṅönya riŋ tawaŋ,
truḥ-truḥ mwaŋ larap iŋ kilat hatĕp ikā karaṇa nika lana akuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
gĕntĕṙnya aṅdadi kumbaŋ edran anaṅis hana lĕṅĕŋ aṅurambat iŋ tĕtö*

ṙyyak niŋ tīṙtha sinrĕṣṭi wastra tinulis pinakatiba tibān linaṅwakĕn,
tustus niŋ maṇi sūṙyyakānta dumilaḥ rahina wĕṅi dinadyakĕn damar,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ cirapattra kalpatarupuṣpa sadĕdĕg aṅadĕg tigaŋ siki,
māyā niŋ wulan iŋ samudra madhu śuddha saphala ginawe laṅit-laṅit*

byakta abyakta nikaŋ tulis wuwuḥ i kādbhuta nika tulis iŋ huwus tama,
yan kĕmbaŋ kadi mambwa rūmnya kadi molaha winilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mwaŋ yan wwaŋ wwaṅan aṙjja kady-aṅucapa asĕmu-sĕmu guyu de nikā mulat,
wimba hyaŋ smara śuddhi de niŋ anulis lwiṙ amanaha manaḥ nrĕpātmajā*

ṅkā ta uṅgwan nrĕpatiputrikā piniḍuḍuk tuhu-tuhu sira janma dewatī,
tan sāmānya mahāprabhāwa tĕka riŋ kaka-kaka kadi dewakanyakā,
aśrī pahyas ira bwat indrawanita amuwuhi halĕp ira n hana iŋ sabhā,
ḍaŋ saṅgha aguñĕpan bhaṭāra karika aṅrakĕt ujaṙ ira yan tumon sira*

sakweḥ-kweḥ nira saŋ kadaŋ haji huwus kili marĕk atatā paḍa atuha,
mambö paṙwwata pājaran halĕp i de nira humalĕpakĕn suputrikā,
endaḥ mwaŋ sira saŋ rare hañaṙ ataṅkil ahayu hayu wahw-amekhala,
mambö maṇḍala riŋ sabhā paṅuparĕṅga ni halĕp ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā*

strī-strī wāhu cumampaka asĕmu hijo pamulu nika pinantĕs iŋ sabhā,
sampiṙnya iŋ jaja tan paniṣphala hananya muwuhi halĕp iŋ wulaŋ tatur,
tuṅgal denya mawa ambĕk abwat atuhan ri parĕk ika ri jöŋ nrĕpātmajā,
lwiṙ dewī humatuṙ saka iŋ surapada anrahakĕna halĕp iŋ surālaya*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

praḥ-praḥ nrĕpawaraduhitā ri guṇḍik ira len i kaka-kaka nira,
yan wruḥ-wruḥ agamĕl aṅiduŋ lawan wruḥ aṅawat ya linĕṅĕnan ira,
embuḥ pwa guṇa nika siniṅhĕlan kinaluṅan ya kinalĕwihakĕn,
sāmpun pwa ya kawi paḍa kāku siŋ guṇa samaṅkana ya kinarahan*

sakweḥnya paḍa marĕk anaṇḍaŋ anwam araras rara rahayu wagĕd,
sabhya amanis aṅucap ikāŋ asiṅhĕl akaluŋ wahu kawi kakawin,
ndan rwaŋ puluḥ ikaŋ akaraḥ jitākṣara wicakṣaṇa naṭakagiṇa,
ṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayaluḥ ikaŋ inuttama asisik ĕmās maṇi nĕhĕṙ amawa*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

prāpta ŋ rātri yayan katon hayu ni waṙṇna nira ri wijil iŋ niśākara,
hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ madhumāsa rūpa nira yan kasaṅa kasapuluḥ tiniṅhalan,
maṅke n māsa kapat hyaŋ iŋ masa kapat kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ mulat,
cañco strī liṅa niŋ tumon sira mĕne n huwus atĕmu lawan nrĕpātmaja*

lumra amintaŋ ahöm ri bāhu lumarap jĕnu nira kanaka aṅhulap hulap,
embuḥ söŋ ni tutup gĕluŋ nira murub maṇik ika kadi motaṙ otaran,
de niŋ kostubha nīla kādbhuta sĕkaṙ taji nira sumĕnö kapañjutan,
Ūṙṇnā śuddha huwus hana iŋ rahi nira asĕmu paṅawaka tĕṅran iŋ hurip*

ndin ṅgānya ŋ wwaŋ anĕmwa rūpa kadi rūpa nira n ahayu rājaputrikā,
wwaŋ riŋ rājya yayan kapūhan aṅalĕm ri sira kadi hañaṙ-hañaṙ mulat,
aśrī waṙṇna nira n tuhan saphala yogya n adĕgakĕna ratwa niŋ tulis,
tan samwas lawaŋ iŋ kaḍatwan inucap milu-milu kawĕṅān tiniṅhalan*

paṅkun mesya ṭikā kayogyan i wĕtis nira damarana teja niŋ wulan,
pantĕs yan makasumpiṅĕn kikirĕn iŋ kuku-kuku nira kosapa iŋ laṭi,
rekhan riŋ kakawin wilāpa kahalĕp ni susu nira parantya niŋ parab,
tan sāha iŋ ratu śakti kenaka ni soca nira yan ikĕtĕn sĕkaṙ taji*

ekĕl roma nira araras kadi katona rumaraba saka iŋ gĕluŋ lukar,
akweḥ mahyun aṅuḍwa de nira yan ahyas anisigi waja aṅhĕmū guyu,
yogya asaṅkan aṅin dumadyakĕna polaḥ i tikĕl i halis nira n cala,
byakta agatgat ataṅhya taṅhya manaḥ iŋ mulat i mukha nira n pasaŋ damar*

ndin putry-a ahayu  hayw-amaṅpaṅa hayunya ri hayu nira n ahyas aṅḍiri,
sakweḥ niŋ wwaŋ ahadyan akryan asawaŋ hinayu marĕk i jöŋ nira alawas,
pahyas niŋ para pora maṅhiribi pahyas ira hinayu cihna niŋ manūt,
ekacchattra raras-raras nira paṅöban iŋ ahayu sujanmakanyakā*

sakweḥ saŋ ratu tan wĕnaŋ sahasa kewala humĕnĕŋ aṅantyakĕn pariḥ,
aṅlampū sumĕsĕl śarīra nira tan wĕnaŋ anĕkani senaka i hati,
moga anaṅgĕl arĕs rumĕṅwakĕn i kādbhuta ni hayu narendraputrikā,
mawwat rāga wilāpa cihna niŋ akūŋ alaḥ alĕḥ akirim-kirim ṭikā*

akweḥ pahyas ira arĕbut kahulunan kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ marĕk,
rorw-aŋ campaka rāmya māyun ayunan ri jaja nira n amaṅya maṅyani,
lāwan pādapa tan wĕnaŋ saḥ i sira amĕpĕti gaway-ika n sĕḥ iŋ gĕluŋ,
tañjuŋ muṅgw-i kapö nira n mrik inaṅit marĕk araras anulya nulyani*

prāpta uliḥ kalaṅön ikāŋ asana rāmya pinakakalasā nira aturū,
mwaŋ roṇḍonya tinap rinūpaka tilam sinalinan i sĕḍĕŋ nika aluñut,
maṅgā sĕmpalĕn aṅkĕn eñjiŋ alapĕn humatura śayanā nira n rimaŋ,
swaṙgga n māti kakiṅkiṅan huwus akīṙtty-amihutaṅi laṅö ri jöŋ nira*

moliḥ waṙṣa sipat nira arahat i solaḥ ika tĕka hirĕŋ hana i mata,
kālanya n kahĕmū sĕpaḥ nira baṅun pinakaliḍaḥ ira n hana i tutuk,
kāsiḥ-kāsiḥ ira alawas karika puṇḍutan ira kasĕlap hana i hati,
ṅhiŋ kĕṇḍit nira mās tumūt i parahasyan ira wahu marĕk sinanmata*

tambe rakwa sira n swayambarakĕna amiliha sakaharĕp nira prabhu,
ndān ambĕk nira kewala awiraŋ i līṅa niŋ umulat anĕṅgaha ahaṅan,
Āpan tan hana ṅūni kewala sira amuṅari pinakakabwatan hañar,
yekā hetu nira awiweka kalawan kaka-kaka wihikan riŋ iṅgita*

ndātan kaṙkkaśa de nira aṅucap ucap ri pasĕluṙ iŋ ujaṙ sira aṅucap,
ndi ŋ paṙwwa ndi kita aṅrĕṅö n hana kadi ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ sabhā,
yadyastun hana maṅkanā niyata ta pwa wiraŋ ika kadi iraŋ i ṅhulun,
saŋkṣepanya huwus katon widhi nareśwara dinuluṙ i tan siḥ iŋ widhi*

Āpan kenaka niŋ kadi ṅhulun aṅanti ri kaka haji yan sira asiha,
heṙ herĕn palarĕn hana asiha bhaṭāra tumĕkakĕna dhaṙmma ni ṅhulun,
prāpta anomaha yogya liŋ nrĕpati sambhawa kaharĕpa ni ṅhulun muwaḥ,
yadyastun layata ṅhulun pi tawanĕn ry-ubhaya haji paran kasaṅśaya*

lāwan yan hana ratw-anomaha marā ta sira humatura i nareśwara,
ndātan kahyuna ni ṅhulun sira tuhun kaka haji sira kewala aharĕp,
haywa amidhyani ta pwa siḥ siha nira amawarĕṅĕha ri buddhya ni ṅhulun,
ndak ton duhkha nikaŋ kinĕdwakĕn apaṅgiha wiphala yan tan paḍa aharĕp*

yan kāṅĕn sukha niŋ licin dumadak ahyun adaluwaṅa haṙṣa riŋ jamaŋ,
denya n kilya rarā makāśraya nareśwara kumĕmita kāla niŋ rare,
yan wrĕddha ajara dhaṙmma riŋ giriwana amagĕhakĕna ri dhaṙmma saŋ wiku,
rāmya ŋ waŋ guru loka saṙwwa tĕka yan lumaku laku rinampak iŋ kili*

maṅke pwa n ḍumawuḥ widhi nrĕpati tan pamawarĕṅĕḥ i buddhi ni ṅhulun,
ṅwaŋ dūra n wĕnaṅa ajñalaṅghana tuhun rasa pĕjaha tiba iŋ paluṅguhan,
ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp kalīṅa ni manaḥ nira yan aharĕp iŋ swayambara,
maṅga aṅdadya limut ṅhulun ri wiraŋ i ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ sabhā*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

tuhan i ṅhulun akṣamakĕna paṅucap ni manĕḥta rĕṅön,
widhi saŋ prabhu sambhawa kĕkĕsakĕna i hati yogya dahat,
dumadak pwa hade n katĕkana rinasan ri manaḥta tuhan,
pira haywa nika aṅucapa n ahala yan hiniḍĕp mahala*

pituhun widhi saŋ prabhu tuhan anipis kawiraṅta hade,
paḍa wāhu ḍatĕŋ sahana hana nikaŋ pariwāra marĕk,
amahuṙ hurakĕn ri para ratu pinetnya sira iŋ wĕgilĕn,
sira saŋ kinabehan inalĕm ika rĕṅwakĕnanta tuhan*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ nātha iŋ magadha prabhāwa nira tan patĕpi kadi laṅit maṅambara,
lwiṙ widyādhara daṙśśanīya pakatonan i bala nira śūra dug siṅī,
ahyaŋ solaḥ ira amanis kawadi de nira lituhayu tan pasiṅsiṅan,
sākṣāt indra saka iŋ surālaya kaweni tumuta mijila iŋ swayambara*

krūrākāra saŋ aṅganātha sanirukti sira yan aruhuṙ sulakṣaṇa,
sabhya ambĕk nira tan rinakwa sira yan prabhu lituhayu sādara aṅucap,
śakty-a anindya mahāprabhāwa kumutug bala nira paḍa śūra suśrama,
tan pendaḥ kadi saŋ hyaŋ agni mijil amralayakĕna rumampaka ŋ jagat*

siṅha ambĕk saŋ awantinātha kadi saŋ yama guṇa nira lokapālaka,
nora adhaṙmma ṅaranya rakwa yan i bhūmi nira paḍa sukha agawe hayu,
söḥ wadwā nira piṇḍa kiṅkarabala amawa curiga gadāyudha apupul,
sākṣāt mrĕtyu curik nira akas aluṅid baṅun aṅayam-ayam parāṅmukha*

tan pendaḥ baruṇa anurun saŋ anupādhipati suyaśa bhūmipālaka,
himpĕṙ sāgara kāṅinan bala nira aṅrwabi nagara hibĕk tĕka i dalĕm,
tĕkwan lwiṙ nira riŋ raṅin dhwaja wĕlaŋ-wĕlaŋ aputiḥ arok lawan hirĕŋ,
rāhu mwaŋ śaśiwimba rūpa nika kāraṇa ni musuḥ ira atabĕḥ titir*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

siŋ solaḥ saŋ susenā pracalita kadi saŋ bāyu riŋ buddhi madrĕs,
wadwā-wadwā riŋ ambĕk lituhayu katĕṅĕṙ yan prawīra apriḥ iŋ praŋ,
himpĕṙ seḍuŋ karĕsrĕs bala nira kumisik lwiṙ gĕlap holiḥ asriŋ,
byakta syūha ŋ musuḥ de nira n asĕmu hudan sañjata awoṙ halisyus*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgada atyanta sugiḥ ira hibĕk mās maṇik rājayogya,
līla acum somya saŋ wꜽśrawana paḍa nira n ghorarūpa adawa agöŋ,
nora anaṇḍaŋ yatan mās bala nira satĕgal kāla niŋ hanyan aṅjraḥ,
sakweḥ niŋ śatru śīṙṇna akuniṅa wulat ikā de nira apan waḥ iŋ mās*

aśrī saŋ pāṇḍya śuddhākrĕti nira satirun paṇḍita anwam widagdha,
tan kāsy-āsiḥ tuhun tan harĕp iŋ ulaḥ agasyak yayan sopacāra,
saŋ hyāŋ īśāna sākṣāt paḍa nira n ahalĕp riŋ sabhā nora tan wruḥ,
atyanta iŋ yoga kawruḥ nira karaṇa nira n katwaŋ iŋ śatru śakti*

wwantĕn saṅka iry-ayodhyā lituhayu dahatĕn rājaputra adwitīya,
ndan rakwa anak mahārāja raghu saŋ aja saṅjñā nira iŋ rāt prakāśa,
saŋ saptādhikrĕta atyanta halĕp ira kabeḥ soṙ kagöṅan pratāpa,
himpĕṙ candra akucĕm tan wani mulat i narendrātmaja lwiṙ hyaŋ aṙkka*

saŋ hyaŋ brahma agawe rūpa nira kadi paran riŋ raras māṙ manisnya,
yadyan gandhaṙwwa widyādhara niyata nika asora riŋ rūpa kāliḥ,
aṅhiŋ hyaŋ kāma saŋ sambhawa mapaga raras rūm nira iŋ maṙttyaloka,
sāmpun pwa aṅāśraya i citta nira masuruhan rāga kuŋ don ira aṅher*

ndān ambĕk ni ṅhulun ṅhiŋ sira juga kadĕlö n kāptya rakryan suputrī,
anwam pūṙṇna iŋ paṅawruḥ lituhayu taruṇa apālapan kṣatriyāṅśa,
jaṅga aṅuṅsiṙ kapat rāmya nira winulatan dlāha yadyan patĕmwa,
Āpan tuṅgal sira iŋ rūm kadi wulan aṅilo wimba niŋ candrakānta*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

nāhan ujaṙnya paḍa asĕluṙ awara waraḥ kinatuṅgalakĕn,
söŋ i manaḥnya katon sĕmu semu niŋ akuŋ ri narendrasuta,
ṅhiŋ kakĕna priḥ ikā sira wiṣaya ni goṣṭhi nika n paṅucap,
rūpa nira sthiti ri twas ika sinamudāya lawan turida*

śri indumatī sukha māṙ hati nira rumĕṅö ry-ucapanya rĕsĕp,
yan tan awĕdya sira iŋ wwaŋ atuha hana buddhi nira amĕpĕra,
rāga nira i saŋ aja awĕtu taṅis inamĕṙ wĕdi kawruhana,
liŋ nira mogha lumuḥ yan aharip araras parihāra nira*

mojaṙ ikaŋ rinahasyan ira wacana liŋnya rĕṅön ta tuhan,
saŋ ratu tan hana tan lituhayu kadi dewata rakwa sira,
ndan paḍa soṙ sira de saŋ aja saphala putra narendra raghu,
hīṅan ira n sira yogya kaharĕpana digjaya rūpa nira*

śri indumatī kĕna rāga tuhun api hade kadi tan malara,
de nira mojaṙ apet silib amarani lokika buddhi nira,
haywa wawaŋ pinisiṅgiḥ ujaṙ ika tuhun hiḍĕpĕn sakarĕŋ,
Āpan ikaŋ dadi janma sakaharĕp ikā kaka mogha dudū*

nista nika an apadudwan ibu kaharĕp iŋ dadi janma kabeḥ,
yan kinatuṅgalakĕn ndya tika hala nikā tuhanĕn pituhun,
māsku mataŋnya kakūṅana saŋ aja tuwin wwaŋ anakta sira,
haywa kĕdö liŋ ira ndan asĕmu sĕmu haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ gumuyu*

ndaḥ paḍa bindaṙ ikaŋ marĕk i sira kapeṅin ajalwa muwaḥ,
mogha girahyasĕn ambĕk ika katanĕhan turida aṅlarani,
asyaŋ i rowaŋ ika aṅucap ucapa kinonya marĕk-marĕka,
liŋnya nihan sanu saŋ ratu pili pilihan dumĕn i ṅwaŋ ari*

wwaŋ-wwaŋ ahadwan agatgat anagu nagu mĕṅgĕp atĕṅw-ahĕniŋ,
bhāwa nika n kĕna rāga hanan asidĕha alupa tan paṅinaŋ,
wyaṙtha sĕrĕḥnya hana i taṅan inagĕm-agĕm tuhu tuhw-alaṅö,
bhrānta rumūpaka saŋ suṅana sĕrĕḥ asūṅa sĕpaḥ ri waja*

len taŋ agoṣṭhi ri gīta saŋ aja ginawenya hañaṙ katĕka,
dudw-aṅalĕm ri palambaŋ ira mamarani i manis iŋ paṅikĕt,
śri indumatī kawĕlad hati nira rumĕṅö ri rasanya lĕṅĕŋ,
lwiṙ jaruman saŋ aja amisiki hiḍĕp ira asriŋ akon mijila*

saŋ wwaŋ inuttama sāmpun adaluwaŋ adoḥ sira riŋ wiṣaya,
milw-atuha ambĕk ira ararĕm arĕja suśīla lana asiḍakĕp,
tan rĕṅu tan lumiriŋ duga-duga pakatonan i tiṅhal ira,
yan paṅucap sira tan paṅucap ucapa len saka riŋ kawikun*

strī sĕḍĕŋ iŋ wiṣaya anwam ahaṅan apasabraṅan ambĕk ika,
mwaŋ sira saŋ wiku wrĕddha marĕk aṅipi nāga milĕt ri sira,
yan wulat aṅdu matanya dinuluṙ i halisnya tikĕl minahā,
maṙmma manisnya paḍa aṅucapakĕn i kahaṙṣa nikā karĕṅö*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

wiku rājya kawi wruḥ aṅaji kaharĕpku siwiṅkwa sanu,
kakawinya palaṙ piguṇana ri parĕknya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,
ulaḥ iŋ paḍa kāsy-asiḥ aṅapi laṅö hiḍĕpĕṅkwa sukha,
kĕmulaṅkwa jajanya taṅan ika saput-saputaṅkwa susu*

agaḍuḥ kawi kāpti mami sanu wĕnaŋ pasabhā pawukir,
wijil iŋ pihutaŋ pawadal inani rowaŋ ika anukhani,
kalawan kalaṅönya wĕnaŋ anigakĕn manaḥ iŋ prihatin,
yadin aṅṅṅĕṅa adulura maṅusira i trĕbis iŋ paraṅan*

atitiḥ kaharĕp mami sanu wĕka niŋ pihutaŋ hutaṅan,
wruha ta iŋ kakawin kiduŋ ulaḥ-ulaḥ iŋ wahu wāhu kawi,
saparanya pamaṅkwakĕna lĕpihan amriḥ ameta laṅö,
sumĕpĕṙ sĕpĕra iŋ papihutaṅan i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ pasisi*

kaharĕpkw-alawas ṅhiŋ abasana wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅön,
niyata ararasĕn marĕk anigi nigi i pamabaṙnya tapiḥ,
paṅapusnya hatiṅku laris i paṅawaknya katon adadar,
prawalanya mara iŋ papasaṅan ika ta n kaharĕpku sanu*

puhawaŋ wahu wahw-amrĕti-mrĕti katönku siwiṅku sanu,
turidaṅku kaḍaṇḍa n alawas aharĕp wwatĕn iŋ banawa,
aputĕk hati niŋ kasarapuŋ alaṅö mulat iŋ pasisi,
kaputĕṙ hati ni ṅhulun alal aharĕp tumuta iŋ alayar*

anak iŋ prajurit mĕtu pajurit ikaŋ kaharĕpku sanu,
lĕwu rāmya niki n katĕkana lurugan ri huwuskw-atĕmu,
hawinĕṅkwa curiknya saha raṅin ikā payuṅaṅkwa tumūt,
tan arĕs yak umilwa sĕḍĕṅa nika keṇḍita riŋ palagan*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

ya ta tĕmahana tiṅluṙ denya n śꜽwa sira siwin,
ikaŋ apalaran anwam wruḥ ta iŋ śāstra wiku haji,
lilu tumakula lampūn dan yan paṇḍita nagara,
atuha-tuha bagañjiŋ byakta aṅhöbi yan inusir*

kunaŋ amuhara kiṅkiŋ yan bot swan sipi mararas,
wiku miraḥ aguṇa aśrī maṅgĕḥ wikwa narapati,
sira ta siwin aharyan santoṣa amalara dĕmak,
palumutana yan anwam yan wrĕddha apuput anadi*

taha sanu yan i rantĕnta aṅhiŋ tyāga juga siwin,
sipi raras iŋ ataṇḍaŋ deśa adoḥ mahas alaṅö,
lĕwu sukha niŋ akaṙwwan soṅsoŋ yan jamaŋ anipis,
pakararas ika paṅkun gantin mwaŋ palu daluwaŋ*

tuhu marika wuwusta ndan son mogha salaḥ ile,
tĕka turida kĕna priḥ de saŋ brāhmaṇa siniwi,
mulat iŋ awĕka mambaŋ prajñā prāya jitasabhā,
ṅhiŋ amuhara wiraṅroŋ heman dhūṙtta cala nika*

kunaŋ amuwuhi rāgī riŋ twas ni ṅhulun alawas,
wĕka-wĕka capaŋ apriḥ riŋ praŋ wāni panagara,
aṅawayuha saliŋ liŋnya n sāmpun ṅwaŋ apatutan,
ikaŋ ujaṙ ibu rakryan kady-asyaŋ maṅiṅin iṅin*

nahan ucapan ikaŋ strī tĕmbenya anĕmu turida,
tan awuni ri manaḥnya n bhrānta akuŋ managu-nagu,
hana ta titiṙ anambut wehan milw-aṅucap-ucap,
mawara waraḥ i rumrūm niŋ sāminya tan awiraŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rare mĕrĕ-mĕrĕḥ pajātyan agĕlo winara warahan iŋ pasaṅgaman,
mapaŋ kumĕtĕṙ aṅgamĕl susu taṅanya saha kĕtĕ-kĕtĕg sumamburat,
uliḥ niŋ amuruk-muruk tinaṅanan ri pataṅanan i sandhi niŋ prĕman,
huwus pwa ya tama aharĕp wayuha tan rĕṇa kadi manaḥ iŋ tama iŋ aji*

dudū sanu lawan huwus pracacaḥ asriŋ arabi siniwi priyambada,
huwus tama karāsikanya kadi waḥ madhu rasa nika riŋ giṇa amanis,
amakpak aṅucap tuhan tinikĕlan halis i sĕḍĕŋ ika aṅgamĕl tapiḥ,
baṅun pĕjaha riŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan ṅwaŋ i paṅamĕṙ ika aṅalap hati*

ikaŋ kawi ñamut laṅönya rinasan saha kakawin araśmi riŋ tilam,
ikaŋ jariji mogha kelu ginamĕlnya kinuku hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp tanaḥ,
lana anipati pet manis kawawa kelu kadi lĕkas ika anulis karas,
kiduŋnya panurū nurūnya sahaja aṅgamĕli susu nĕhĕṙ kinaṅsyakĕn*

prawīra siniwi priyambada tuhun kawatĕk ulaḥ ika n wani iŋ raṇa,
añumbu kadi de nika n paṅalawaŋ raṅin i sĕḍĕŋ ika n paṅolakĕn,
anaṅtaŋ amapag wulat nĕhĕṙ aminta linawanan anūt mamaṅkwakĕn,
mara iŋ susu taṅanya mogha hiniḍĕp nika ḍuka-ḍuka niŋ curik siṅī*

lawan-lawanan i ṅhulun wiku miraḥ lituhayu pinakesi niŋ kuṭi,
manisnya kadi poḥ apādapa tiki n mamaragi gula gaṇṭi dug siṅī,
liriŋnya pinarantyan i ṅhulun iŋ ambyan iŋ umaḥ i sĕḍĕŋ nika anasi,
dudū swara nika i karinya karĕṅö panamaya nika yan para i ṅhulun*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nāhan de nika goṣṭhi senak i manaḥnya panalimuṙ ika aharip mata,
tan tuṅgal rumĕṅö ry-ujaṙnya hana hewa hana sĕmu pacĕḥ mĕṅĕn-mĕṅĕn,
strī kryan-kryan paḍa mūla-mūla rabi niŋ kawi muwaḥ aṅucap samaṅkana,
tan doṣa asiŋ ujaṙnya mogha minanis manisan ika tinuṅtuṅan laṅö*

rakryan kenaka niŋ manuṣya sararā wĕrĕ wĕrĕha yayan papaṅgiha,
ambĕk nāgarika wruha aṅikĕta bhāṣa sakurasa sawīja riŋ laṅö,
yan pāywan kakawin maṅaṙwwana wilaḥ kakawin ika palambaŋ iŋ yaśa,
yekā kāma ratī ṅaranya n araras paḍa kawi sawawa anak iŋ maṅö*

luṅha aṅdoha mara iŋ pasiṙ kahalĕpanya n amarĕṅana māsa kāṙttika,
sakwan selwan ahimya himyana manumpaka ri walakaŋ iŋ karaŋ liman,
ramya atuntunana iŋ hĕnī ri surud iŋ rwab i tĕpi-tĕpi saŋsaya aḍake,
līla ameta huraŋ tanaḥ nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ asaṅu saṅu saṅwa niŋ maṅö*

ndak ton haṙṣa nika n parambakana riŋ bañu tuna-tuna mombak ombakan,
kāliḥ-kāliḥ ika aduluṙ paḍa girahyasĕn anĕmu laṅö lĕyĕp dahat,
strīnya amiṅkasakĕn tapiḥ jĕnĕk amet uwuṙ-uwuṙ agĕlaṙ mara iŋ tĕpi,
byakta alūma kaköma riŋ bañu hasin wĕtis ika panahā nikaŋ mulat*

rūpanya n mahasa iŋ pasiṙ kadi katona mahasa ri samudra niŋ tulis,
Āpan de ni lĕyĕp lĕyĕp ni patĕmunya kadi tasik awoṙ lawan laṅit,
yadyastun yan aṅumbaṅa iŋ jaladhi kawruhan i pamilĕt iŋ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ,
sākṣāt dewata dewatī mahas ahas lĕṅĕŋ aṭika ṭikan saka iŋ tawaŋ*

buddhinya n wahu wahw-acaṅkrama mara iŋ pasisi wahu mahas lawan priya,
maṅgā n tan muliha n panon paduluṙ iŋ layaṙ asĕmu matuntunan taṅan,
soliḥnya n pakaraŋ-karaŋ winawanan taṅan ulaḥ-ulaḥ iŋ hañaṙ hañar,
apwī niŋ hiliran ya sādhana nika akĕla kĕlana ri piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik*

piṅgiṙ niŋ paraṅan gihā watu sumoŋ pinakapasaji riŋ mara aṅṅṅĕŋ,
priṅga arĕs tinataṙ hĕnū nika sumĕṅka tumurun atupis rĕṅat-rĕṅat,
paṙṇnaḥ loṙ maṅuṅaŋ tasik mukha nikā dunuṅan i kĕñaṙ iŋ niśākara,
ṅkāna n paṅhinĕpa amaḍaŋ wulana yadyan aharipa sukha n paḍa amrĕma*

tĕkwan pwa iki n anak wĕsi nrĕpati kawwaṅan ika wĕka niŋ sinanmata,
yadyastun kilalan tĕkap saŋ ahulun pawĕkasakĕna riŋ mara iŋ pasir,
byakta n mantuka moliḥ oliḥ alaṅö haturakĕna ri jöŋ nareśwara,
cihnanya n kawi kaṙwwa kāsiḥ ika wāhu wihikan asabhā sabha amasir*

nāhan wastu ni denya mojaṙ api doḥ ndan abhimata nika i suputrikā,
śrī dewi indumatī huwus wruḥ iŋ apa n kasiliba riŋ ujaṙ samaṅkana,
kālap buddhi nira iniriŋ winawa riŋ lĕṅĕŋ amasiṙ ahimya himyana,
ndan moga api hade sahuṙ nira paṅawruhana panalimuṙ manaḥ rimaŋ*

siṅgiḥ ṅgānya wuwusta rāmya ŋ akurĕn sarara wĕrĕ wĕrĕḥ paḍa araras,
luṅha asaṅwa karas tanaḥnya mahasa iŋ pasiṙ aduluṙ ahimya himyana,
tan waŋ mātra kasiṅya mātra manaḥ i ṅhulun irikaŋ ulaḥ samaṅkana,
ndak ton kewran ikaŋ giṇa aniwi taṅeḥ mamaḍana raras iŋ wujaŋ-wujaŋ*

tĕkwan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅhulun ataṇḍaṅa pasisi huwus tama ṅhulun,
pora wwaŋ nika tan wruḥ iŋ puruṣabheda hiliran amukĕt hana amayaŋ,
mogha iraŋ ṅwaŋ isin maṅambila karaŋ karaṅan i pasurak niŋ ampuhan,
aṅhiŋ ṙyyaknya maṅaṅkul aṅkul ajajaṙ baṅun asĕgĕḥ anĕmbaḥ iŋ maṅö*

ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ wukiṙ tĕka rĕsĕp mwaŋ aṅalĕwihakĕn saka iŋ pasir,
de niŋ kweḥ nira paṇḍita atapa ri paṙśśwa nika kumuliliŋ tĕka i ruhur,
yadyastun ṅwaŋ atiṅgala iŋ nagara wikwa rara maṅusira i munīśwara,
rāmya ŋ pakṣa wukiṙ yayan ku n aṅuṅaŋ ry-abhimata saŋ apakṣa sāgara*

wöṅi iŋ māsa kapat ṅhulun milu ri jöŋ nrĕpati mahas-ahas mariŋ wukir,
saŋ hyaŋ lek i surup hyaŋ aṙkka mijil aṅḍaḍari kadi maṅumbaŋ iŋ pasir,
tūban mwaŋ gĕrĕḥ iŋ patĕṙ tan asarag dhwani nika lalita anurū nurū,
eñjiŋ meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu samaṅkana mawuṅu tinaṅhi niŋ cucur*

abhrā kaywan ikaŋ wukiṙ wijaḥ arūm kadi pinisalinan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,
len taŋ saṙwwalata awilĕt samaṙ arok baṅun ahurupa luṅgu luṅguhan,
sakweḥ niŋ kayu mās lawan kayu puriŋ paḍa-paḍa masuṅut wĕlas harĕp,
ṅkāna i piṅgiṙ ikaŋ juraŋ pĕtuŋ ikā paḍa kadi pinituṅtuṅan limut*

sore ry-ampĕḥ ikaŋ jawuḥ kari gĕrĕḥnya muni pinakarāmya niŋ wukir,
lāwan megha marantayan tura turaḥnya siniriṙ iŋ aṅin pĕgat-pĕgat,
miṅsoṙ miṇḍuhuṙ aṅlayaŋ kadi dinĕmwan añawĕli kukus carik-carik,
himpĕṙ siñjaŋ iŋ apsarī kasarakat ri laris ika saka i pamañcanan*

saŋkṣepanya katon kasoṙ i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasisi tĕkap i rāmya niŋ wukir,
tĕkwan wighna niŋ aṅṅṅĕŋ mahasa riŋ pasisi tarahan aṅhaḍaŋ haḍaŋ,
śuddha ŋ paṙwwata nityaśa asĕmu kadewatan i hana saŋ ugrapaṇḍita,
ndak gañjaṙ kita yan kita antuka tasik mamaḍana kapawitran iŋ wukir*

<śikhariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ : 17

taham rakryan di ŋ paṙwwata lĕwiha saṅka iŋ jalanidhi,
anūsa apaṇḍan raṅkaŋ apasiṙ asaṅhub saha kilat,
muwaḥ tan pāntyāntya ampuhan ika baṅun kāṙttika sadā,
manuknya aliwran yan wahu mari jawuḥ lwiṙ laru-laru*

kumĕmbaŋ tuñjuŋ kāṅinan uwuṙ uwuṙnya aṅjraḥ aputiḥ,
layaṙ niŋ baṇyāga anutakĕn aṅin aṅdoḥ kadi limut,
lĕṅĕŋ ṙyyaknya n sandhya amiraḥ asĕmu megha anisik iwak,
laṅit suṅsaŋ lwiṙnya n maśaśadharamāyā makalaṅan*

bhaṭārī śrī pöḥ niŋ jaladhi pinutĕṙ lāwan amrĕta,
muwaḥ catra aśwa atyanta riŋ aṅuparĕṅga i halĕp ira,
tuwin hyaŋ wiṣṇu swāmi nira jĕnĕk i jro jalanidhi,
mataŋnyan mūlya ŋ sāgara karaṇa niŋ paṙwwata sinor*

tuhan putrī tan kemĕṅan iŋ ucapan yogya sahura,
huwus wruḥ rakwa i tiṅkaḥ iŋ acala len kṣīrajaladhi,
apan yan mūḍhā buddhi nira pisaniṅw-a anĕmu sahur,
kunaŋ pwa apan prajñā sira sumahuṙ apyak saha guyu*

ndatan moli n hyaŋ śrī winijilakĕn iŋ kṣīrajaladhi,
parĕŋ lāwan catrāśwa kapat ira teki ikaŋ amrĕta,
apaṅgiḥ mwaŋ hyaŋ wiṣṇu hana riŋ anantāsana sadā,
ya hetunya n soṙ liṅta ŋ acala tĕkap niŋ jalanidhi*

kaka ndi n sora ŋ paṙwwata tĕkap i rūm niŋ jalanidhi,
apan lwiṙ wruḥ riŋ swaṙgga ŋ aṅahasi puñcak niŋ acala,
paran saṅkan saŋ hyaŋ rawi gati niŋ astodayagiri,
umādewī sākṣāt mara sira sinaṅguḥ girisutā*

sira atekā duṙggā ṅaran ira kasaṅkhya iŋ tribhuwana,
wĕkas niŋ strī siddhi syapa ta sira dewī kadi sira,
huwus limpad riŋ kāṣṭaguṇan atiduṙgga n tiru-tirun,
kunaŋ ta apan riŋ bimba ya sira n awās kottaman ira*

bhaṭāra hyaŋ rudra pwa siniwi nira atūt siliḥ asiḥ,
apaṅgiḥ ṅkāna iŋ meru sira paḍa siddhaprabhu wibhu,
mataŋnyan nora hyaŋ kadi sira mahāsiddhi dahatĕn,
anādi n riŋ liṅgodbhawacarita pamyaktana kaka*

sira atekā tūtĕnkwa lumĕwihakĕn riŋ mahidhara,
saka i sakweḥ niŋ sāgara mapa ta sī madwa karika,
sahuṙ haywa asowe kaka rasa rasa apan kita bisa,
tuhankw-ibw-amwīta alaha tuhu wuwusta ahayu dahat*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nāhan de nira goṣṭhi rāmya tadanantara rahina huwus ḍawuḥ pitu,
sakweḥ niŋ paricārika aṅiriṅa sāmpun anarima dadaṙ paḍa asalin,
lāwan saŋ wwaŋ inuttama ahayu sujanma paḍa sira marĕk sumaṅgraha,
śrī dewi indumatī sira aṅadĕg awaṙṇna ratu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ ṭika aṅaraŋ*

strī stry-a anekawiśeṣa pakṣa ḍatĕṅa iŋ paṅuṅaṅan aduluṙ hana iŋ lĕbuḥ,
ahyaŋ waṙṇna nika n hinĕmban araras pinayuṅan iniriŋ bhinūṣaṇan,
sakweḥ niŋ kapapag lumiṅsiṙ awĕdi iŋ wwaŋ ahalĕp akĕmul ya riŋ wĕṅi,
pañ̈ñjut sañjata len garantuŋ i harĕp prakaṭa baṅun akon sumiṅgaha*

eñjiŋ rāmya tiniṅhalan sahana niŋ paṅuṅaṅan atata akatap-katap,
de niŋ pañjut awaṙṇna wintaŋ anulaṙ wĕdi karahinana anusup nusup,
mrik gandhanya huwus kinasturi miṅiŋ rinacana tinulis linaṅwakĕn,
wwaŋnya apiṇḍa surāpsarī saha wimāna wahu tĕka saka iŋ surālaya*

wastra abhrā pinakapralamba hana riŋ walikuwaŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ,
kram niŋ cawli kukus baṅun truḥ anisiḥ pinakapaṅuparĕṅga niŋ hatĕp,
himpĕṙ nīrada citramegha nika riŋ haḍa pinakatawiŋ-tawiŋ marar,
luṅsiṙ baŋ pinakoluṙ-oluṙ i pucak-pucak ika kadi luṅgaḥ iŋ kilat*

saśrī waṙṇna nikaŋ payuŋ payuṅan akrĕp asĕmu-sĕmu paṅjraḥ iŋ jamur,
akweḥ waṙṇna nikā hanan dadu hanan prĕcik asira siran paḍa aṅadĕg,
de niŋ kweḥ nira saŋ wĕnaŋ paḍa katon kawĕnaŋ ira mijil samaṅkana,
len taŋ biṙyyan amet sĕkaṙ niŋ asana aniru-niru halĕp iŋ payuŋ kuniŋ*

saŋ hyaŋ sūṙyya mijil kamantyan abuṅaḥ pawulatan i sabhā nikaŋ kuwu,
wwaŋnya lwiṙ jalada akĕmul kilat asoŋ hima sahana hananya riŋ lĕbuḥ,
de niŋ kweḥnya lawan prabhā ni sasinaṇḍaŋ ika lumarap aṅhulap hulap,
śaṅkha mwaŋ tarayan mrĕdaṅga kumisik mamaji taliṅa niŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö*

wwaŋ-wwaŋ thāni paḍa aduluṙ wahu tĕka aṅibĕki nagara len hana iŋ hĕnū,
tĕkwan riŋ sakurĕn hana anak ika pat lima marĕk amilĕt-milĕt laku,
strīnya aṅĕmban anuntun āmĕtĕŋ apan maṅĕliḥ ika manamby-anuswani,
aprakprākan apan hilaŋ sasiki lūd kakutil awurahan siliḥ daliḥ*

len ta ikaŋ kaki kaky-amet putu nikā hilaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ ikā siliḥ sĕḍĕk,
liŋ niŋ strīnya maha akas ī kita harĕp mulata kita nininya riŋ waneḥ,
Āpan de ni uninta lāgi ta kita amupuḥ i sĕḍĕŋ ika aṅucap kaki,
iḥ dūra anaṅisa aku yan kita midoṣana pĕjahana sĕṅgahĕn bahud*

strī-strī wrĕddha huwus tĕka iŋ kabuyutan milu-milu mulat iŋ swayĕmbara,
aṅhĕmban raray-anwam akrak anaṅis winaliŋ ika putunya rakwa ya,
mojaṙ swāmi nikā nini syapiku hāpa ya kaki taha tan putunta ya,
hā-hāḥ tiṅgalakĕn hade nini tĕwas kita kabrĕkĕkĕ duhkha kabwatan*

nāhan liŋ nika hāsyakāraṇa sapolaḥ ika tucapa saŋ para prabhu,
ginyākĕn ḍatĕṅa irikaŋ pagĕlaran paḍa mijila kabeḥ sira iŋ lĕbuḥ,
wīṙyya-wīṙyyan amĕtwakĕn hati nira irikaŋ aṅinakana i wwaŋ iŋ sabhā,
muntab lwiṙ ni halĕp nira aṅarab-arab sama-sama kadi bahni kāṅinan*

maṅkat śrī magadheśwara atri gumuruḥ paḍahi nira karĕṅw-agĕnturan,
sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ kapūhan i halĕp nira paḍa mapipit-pipit mukha,
kady-a aṅaṙwwani sumpiŋ endaḥ araras pinatihakĕn ika n paḍa aṅuṅaŋ,
tuṅgal waṙṇna nika abuṅaḥ kadi wulan sasiki pinarawĕñca niŋ smara*

aśrī waṙṇna saŋ aṅganātha sawatĕk-watĕk ira mapupul paḍa ahalĕp,
himpĕṙ sāgara lakwa-lakwan ira rāmya tan asĕpi kapiŋ rwa niŋ laku,
tĕkwan rūpa nira asĕḍĕp tan ahañaŋ huwus amuyahi ri twas iŋ rimaŋ,
tan tuṅgal stry-aṅaraŋ tumon sira manaḥnya kalara-lara kaṙwwaban laṅö*

lwiṙ guntuṙ saŋ awantinātha tĕka gumrĕbĕg ahalĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratha,
himpĕṙ truḥ sumaput lĕbū nira mĕlĕk pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍa mrĕm apĕpĕt mĕpĕti mukha ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ sabuk,
agraḥ rūpa nikaŋ kaḍatwan i kĕtug ni paḍahi nira mapratidhwani*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

liṇḍū lwiṙ saŋ hanūpādhipati manaḥ ikaŋ strī mulat bhrāntacitta,
miṅgut-miṅgut halisnya arĕṅu rĕṅu kadi tan wwaŋnya kewalya mūṙcchā,
katrag santĕnya kegū hati nika kagiwaŋ sāri-sāri prapañca,
kady-a anumbak jajanya n pasidĕha tĕka riñcuŋ tĕṅaḥnya aṅgaluṅgaŋ*

wāni iŋ praŋ saŋ susenā laku nira lumurug kesyan ambĕk nira akras,
wadwā-wadwān dĕlit niŋ tahu rinĕbut i rūm niŋ mulat riŋ paniñjon,
siṅhākāra iŋ sabhā yogya wulatana kasaṅkhya n dhanurwedaśāstra,
sakweḥ niŋ stry-a amapag tiṅhal ira paḍa kĕna iŋ rāga tībra byamoha*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgada akweḥ asĕmu gunuŋ ĕmās katraṅan kāla sandhyā,
de niŋ siṅhĕl kaluŋ mwaŋ karaḥ atip apipit paṅharĕp niŋ lumampaḥ,
tan pendaḥ puṣpa sālas dadaṙ i bala nira arūm apan saṙwwawastra,
gĕṇḍiŋ tan kaṙkkaśa alwan bhramara kahiḍĕpanya aṅisĕp saṙwwasāri*

saŋ pāṇḍya apiṇḍa dewa alaku-laku tuwi saŋ paṅruhun paṇḍita akweḥ,
tātan pendaḥ saka iŋ buddhapada sahana saŋ boddhapakṣa ampak ampak,
śꜽwaṙṣy-a awaṙṇna saṅka iŋ śiwapada paḍa sāmpun pĕnuḥ riŋ paṅawruḥ,
sakweḥ saŋ brāhmaṇa apūṙwwa pawulatan ira lwiṙ saka iŋ brahmaloka*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

maṅkat śrī naranāthaputra kadi kāṙttika wahu tĕka de nira n laku,
luḥ niŋ strī kĕna rāga riŋ paṅuṅaṅan kadi riris inusap saka i mukha,
tiṅhalnya adu baṅun kilat lumarap aṅluru-luru ri huwus nikaŋ jawuḥ,
sambat-sambat ikā ginūḍha kadi mĕtwa marĕṅana kalaṅwan iŋ patĕr*

liŋnya i twasnya bhaṭāra manmatha manĕḥta kawĕlas arĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,
kiṅkiŋ rāga tĕka anaput prihati māṙ pinuhara nika tan wĕnaŋ kinas,
maṅke kāla nikaŋ swayambara tĕka amarupuhi sahasa aṅrĕmĕk hati,
aṅgyat lwiṙ hudan adrĕs iŋ katiga tan pakakaraṇa karĕṅwan iŋ gĕrĕḥ*

t asy-a asiḥ siha saŋ hyaŋ i ṅhulun alaḥ sĕpĕrakĕna nareśwarātmaja,
syūhĕn denta manaḥ nira iŋ lulut unĕŋ kĕtĕrakĕna nĕhĕṙ tĕkākĕna,
Āpan tan hana len saka i sira pakāśrayan awĕlasa riŋ griŋ i ṅhulun,
tambā rāga siroṣadha prihati jampi turida pinakāmrĕta iŋ rimaŋ*

yadyan laṅghana tan panūta manaḥ i ṅhulun i sĕḍĕŋ ira n pamaṅkwakĕn,
ndak ton kĕdwa nira anukūlakĕna tan kawaśa hinudanan wulat maliŋ,
Āpan siṅha sira iŋ rahasya niyata arĕp arĕpan i tan olya kaprĕma,
byakta aṅrampasa ken dunuŋ susu kayuḥ tĕṅaḥ anĕkani senaka i hati*

<abhikrĕti> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 25

nahan liŋ ika ri twas epu wihikan ri manaḥ ika yatan sakāra dahatĕn,
ya kāraṇa nika awuyuŋ ri taliṅanya tĕka rĕṅĕ rĕṅön i wrĕtta saŋ aja,
halisnya pinisitnya tan duga-duga n paṅujiwat i sĕḍĕŋ nira n umaliwat,
matanya dinaliḥnya duṙjana hĕnū nira mara ri hatinya tan pamali luḥ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

taṅeḥ yan ucapĕn laranya tali niŋ carita waluyana ucapĕn muwaḥ,
para prabhu huwus tĕka iŋ pagĕlaran mapupul asĕmu hetwa niŋ laya,
apan gumuruḥ apratidhwani surak ni bala nira ya ta amaṅun bhaya,
baṅun hana katona digjaya katona pĕjaha rĕbutĕn salaḥ siki*

atuṅgalan umaḥ bwat indranagara ajajaṙ asĕmu kaḍatwan iŋ tawaŋ,
para prabhu mahāprabhāwa sawaŋ aṙcca maṇik inululan hana iŋ sabhā,
paḍa asira siran pratāpa kadi tan hana lĕwiha saka i halĕp nira,
tĕka pwa saŋ aja akucĕm sira baṅun śaśadhara matĕmaḥ kunaŋ-kunaŋ*

syapa ika tan awĕdya riŋ kadi sira aguṇa wĕka niŋ amĕdyakĕn ratu,
awaṙṇna madhumāsa kāṙttika piniṇḍa piniturun adadya mānuṣa,
ikaŋ wwaŋ aharĕp wruha i sira humuŋ sahana-hana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ sabhā,
katon pwa sira denya rĕp wĕdi kumĕl humĕnĕŋ asĕmu sinyukan bañu*

rare saŋ aja śakti pustaka lĕṅĕn raghuwĕka wani kawy-anuṅgali,
ikaŋ guṇa hana i sira agaṇita riŋ kapana kawaśa taṙkka niŋ mulat,
prasiddha sira sūtra niŋ karawiwaṅśan amagĕhakĕn āgama iŋ prajā,
rusit niŋ aji ta pwa rūpa nira tan hana ratu wĕnaŋ aṅdĕlö dĕlö*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

sāmpun prāpta sira iŋ sabhā pinakamaṅgala ni halĕp ikaŋ swayambara,
śrī dewi indumatī sira inarahakĕn mijila wahu huwus bhinūṣaṇan,
muṅgw-iŋ ḍampa sira apĕga aṅĕnĕb-ĕnĕb kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira māṙ sumamburat,
saśry-a awaṙṇna tulis ḍinampan awĕnĕs wĕnĕs asĕmu rakĕt kapañjutan*

endaḥ ḍampa nira apĕnĕd kinajaṅan kusumaśara tinap linaṅwakĕn,
ronya indrāyudha puṣpacāpa pikulanya mamukha mukha nāga campaka,
mās tuṅgal nika puṣpaliṅga niŋ aṅaṙccana ri pada bhaṭāra manmatha,
nāgākāra surat suratnya tinĕtĕs ni luḥ iŋ akuŋ amaṅkwakĕn ṭikā*

Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira saŋ pinituhu ri tatā sama aṅiriŋ,
sāmpun muṅgw-i harĕp sira ahalĕp acum nĕhĕṙ aṅarahakĕn lumampaha,
kĕṇḍaŋ goŋ muni t aṅkat-aṅkat atĕrĕḥ dhwani nika karĕṅö saka i yawa,
sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍa aṅĕnĕb ĕnĕb raras i hati nika n tumiṅhala*

maṅkat śrīndumatī garantuŋ ira muny-asĕmu gula ghināṣa riŋ waja,
rūm niŋ paṅlima muṅgu riŋ śrigaḍiŋ iŋ masa kalima tinū hana iŋ kapö,
aṅlaṅwākĕn awaṙṇna kāṙttika pamatnya gumuruḥ araras rinĕṅwakĕn,
lwiṙ tūban kumusuḥ karĕṅwan i panĕmpuḥ ika kadi panĕmpuḥ iŋ jawuḥ*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

rakryan putrī mijil kābhinawa halĕp ira apūṙwwa saṅka iŋ kaḍatwan,
aṅlīla awās katon bhūṣaṇa nira kumĕñaṙ lwiṙ panoliḥ hyaŋ aṙkka,
aṅheṙ riŋ gopura aṅrĕgrĕg i pasalĕsĕk iŋ paṅharĕp söḥ marampak,
sākṣāt saŋ hyaŋ wulan wāhu mĕtu riŋ udayādri iniriŋ niŋ graha akweḥ*

moga ahyaŋ de nira amet hayu mamulaṅuni i buddhi niŋ wwaŋ tumiṅhal,
hyaŋ śrī liŋnya i sira aṅiṇḍarat aharĕp ameta aśraya iŋ maṙttyaloka,
len tekaŋ wwaŋ sumĕṅgaḥ ratiḥ i sira saka iŋ swaṙgga lāwan surastrī,
bhranta anĕṅgaḥ dwicandra aduluṙ i payuŋ ira atyanta śuddha rwa sādĕg*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

menmen rwaŋ siki wāhu rāgawaśa muṅgw-i harĕp ira marĕk manimbaṅi,
hyaŋ niŋ gīta tĕka anurun kahiḍĕpanya ḍatĕŋ iniriŋ-iŋ tabaŋ-tabaŋ,
siṅhĕlnya aṙjja lawan sawitnya katiraḥ wĕlas arĕp awilĕt lawan gaḍuŋ,
tan pendaḥ kadi nāgapāśa pamanaḥ niŋ atanu karaṇanya lĕŋlĕŋa*

nyū danta akuniŋ aṅhapit gula-gula lwiṙ ikaŋ amawa pawwahan gaḍiŋ,
tapwan wāla dahat rwa sādĕg abĕbĕd niyata kahirisan twas iŋ mulat,
tĕṅgĕknya aluŋ apiṇḍa kāṅinana polaḥ ika n asĕmu buṅkaḥ iŋ pupus,
aṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayawaspa paṅhulu manisnya n anilihi mamaṅku pawwahan*

tan hawwan gati saŋ rara ahawu-hawu wwaŋ ahayu tinuras raras nika,
lūd bhasmāṅkura laṇḍa rakwa sira saŋ tuha-tuha nika yan saka iŋ bibi,
solaḥ seṅĕṙ ika ahaṅan gĕsĕŋ i pāmbĕkan ika tĕkap iŋ smarānala,
yogyā kuṇḍaṅa niŋ manunwani pamiṅgiṙ amĕnĕma kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ*

mopiḥ wahw-amayaŋ-mayaŋ ri hati niŋ mulat anĕku-nĕku pralāpita,
tapwan rañca hatinya kewala walĕlwan amagĕhakĕn iŋ kakanyakān,
kāsĕṅkanya piliḥ pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ smara rumimaṅa buddhi niŋ kawi,
yogya n raṅkulĕn iŋ wani iŋ raṇa tĕṅaḥnya pasuṅakĕna sĕmba-sĕmbahan*

tapwan wrĕddha dahat sira iña nira lāwan uwa nira paḍa akurug miraḥ,
ekĕl roma nira asĕlat huwan ikaŋ hayu tumalawuṅan turuŋ lĕwas,
luñcip niŋ kuku pantĕs aṅgrĕmusa lagy-aṅuluŋ uluṅi rāga niŋ mulat,
edran tiṅhal ira iŋ sabhā baṅun anambĕra hinayamakĕn titik maṅö*

putrī niŋ kryan anak wĕsi nrĕpati rakwa kaka-kaka nira anwam iŋ wayaḥ,
pantĕs tan pamikārakĕn hayu rĕṅunya muwuhi raras iŋ mata amanis,
lwiṙ hyaŋ-hyaŋ tĕka tan hinundaŋ anurun sahana nika paḍa awulaŋ tatur,
kram niŋ sampiṙ i bāhu mās inapi molaḥ asĕmu hĕlaranya n aṅlayaŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ikaŋ mamawa kaṇḍi-kaṇḍi rara wahw-agĕluŋ ahayu poṣadhan lulut,
lumut-lumut ikaŋ payodhara wĕnaŋ paṅuwata sĕḍĕŋ iŋ jaja ahĕnĕk,
pupuṙ nika wĕnaŋ paṅoṣadha pilĕg niŋ iruŋ apan arūm saka iŋ kapur,
lukaṙ karika kenya mukhya pinakādi paṅuwata ri rāga niŋ rimaŋ*

wagĕd-wagĕd ikāŋ añāmarani waṙgga pasisi salĕmaḥ lawan wukir,
sawaṙgga kalawan wulan mukha nikā kalĕṅĕṅan ika mitra niŋ cucur,
tĕṅaḥnya wahu wanwa riŋ jriŋ aṅĕliḥ wahu waśa riŋ aśokapādapa,
sasīma kalawan mayūra gĕluṅanya wĕka niŋ asana akadaŋ patĕr*

kunaŋ saŋ apahidwan eṅas ahaṅan pawulatan i manaḥnya riŋ sabhā,
sĕkaṙ nika pinintakāsihakĕn iŋ kawi huwus aṅikĕt hañaṙ tĕka,
kisapwakĕna riŋ prawīra kahalĕp nika suṅana sĕpaḥ saka i waja,
kayogyan i laṭinya yan kadi duḥ iŋ wwaḥ ika sĕsĕpĕn iŋ priya atalĕḥ*

anak wĕsi narendra rakwa rasikā saŋ amawa curiga araras dahat,
aroma maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kahiḍĕpanya n apaṅawaka patrĕm uttama,
ikaŋ wwaŋ araṅin wineḥ curiga kadga sinĕpuhan apan wagĕd waśi,
wajanya mamiraḥ tĕka i gusi gusinya halis ika tĕka amraŋ iŋ mulat*

ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅagĕm curik pinakapaṅruhun aduluṙ arĕs twas iŋ mulat,
asiṅhĕl akaluŋ krĕtāṙtha riŋ ayun pinakapaṅisi niŋ wani iŋ raṇa,
surakṣaka kabhīnna bhīnna baṅun antaka mapupul ahöm aṅiṇḍarat,
winaswas asipattra sālas asĕwö krĕtala curiga tomara aluṅid*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

wwaŋ-wwaŋ kasturi sāri niŋ kusuma rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ inuttama ahayu,
meww-iww-a atap awaṙṇna kuntul aṅusī pasisi kakilatan hana iŋ tawaŋ,
yadyastun tulisĕn samaṅkana pira awig awiga nika yan hana iŋ yaśa,
ṅhiŋ ganya n drawanĕn manisnya niyatanya tumuluy-atĕmaḥ tasik madhu*

laslāsan wruḥ iŋ iṅgita aṅinakana iŋ mulat ahayu puji n pakawwaṅan,
yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ cala cala arĕṅu-rĕṅu sahaja apuput guyu,
nistanya n kadi pāwak iŋ madhu manisnya raras ika kadi ṅrĕs iŋ hati,
tan paṅgintiṙ i rūm nira asĕmu jamuṙ hapa-hapa marĕk iŋ jamuṙ wulan*

denya aṅlaṅkahakĕn sukunya kadi tan lĕpasa tĕkap i lon ikaŋ laku,
mĕñcuḥ-mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki pupūnya hana bĕnĕṙ adĕgnya pet ulaḥ,
kahyun-hyun laris iŋ wĕtis tan alaris laku nika minahā hinerakĕn,
aṅjiṅjiŋ sasisiḥ mĕluk tuṙ ika mātra wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ tulis*

strī-strī sabhya wicakṣaṇa anagara nora kakuraŋ ika pantĕs iŋ sabhā,
kady-a anaṇḍuṅakĕn rwi de nika lumampaḥ arĕṅu sahaja aṅhĕmu guyu,
eñjuḥ prāya nika n wulat riŋ aṅuṅaŋ tan ahulap atawĕŋ tawĕŋ taṅan,
tan pendaḥ salukat jajaṙ gĕluŋ ikā lukaṙ i jaja tinumbakan susu*

kady-aṅrakṣa hayunya rūpa nika de ni galak i pamatanya yan wulat,
hrū ni iruŋnya lanā katon amatitis pamarayaŋ i halisnya lot mayat,
waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ waja akrĕp asinaŋ gusi-gusi nika kesisan laṭi,
ahrit wit ni suśūnya tĕkwan aluṅid paḍa-paḍa kadi suṅga niŋ jaja*

<suwaṅśapattra> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏓ : 18

tucapa tikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan wagĕd aṅucap ucap,
liŋ ika suputrikā pinakaratna winuni ri dalĕm,
saŋ aja sujanma mās kinĕmit iŋ nagara wahu tĕka,
saphala sira n humambanakĕna i narapatiduhitā*

nrĕpatanayā katon wĕdi nira n mulat i para ratu,
yadin alupa ŋ śarīra sira mūṙcchita lumaya kawĕs,
hulĕsana tan bawaŋ jasunana i sĕḍĕŋ ira kapati,
niyata sira aṅliliṙ saŋ aja saṇḍiṅakĕna ri jaja*

narapatiputrikā n gĕluṅa niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis i ṭikā,
saŋ aja paṅisya mon sira wirāga sadaka pasaji,
athawa yadin padadyana sipat narapatitanayā,
nrĕpasuta de nira n gagaṅa mon pusuḥ usapa mata*

sĕkara niŋ aṅhiḍĕp smara kunaŋ narapatitanaya,
saphala n apallawa ambĕt i tĕṅaḥ narapatiduhitā,
nrĕpawaraputrikā n sĕkara de nira kumuda paḍa,
saŋ aja niśākarā nira maran patĕmu paḍa lĕṅĕŋ*

para ratu tan padon pisaniṅū sira kaharĕpana,
tuhu sira śakti wāni paḍa tan hana kakuraŋ ira,
ndan atiśaya prabhāwa saŋ aja adbhuta kagiri giri,
asana lawan wuṅū paḍa nira ndya ta hurĕn i rika*

nahan ucapanya yan dinuluran rĕṅu saha kujiwat,
waja nika tan wĕnaŋ winuni keṅis amuhara raras,
wĕkasan anagwa nagwakĕn i rowaŋ ika ri saŋ aja,
cinalukakĕn maha apicala haṙṣa riŋ ujaṙ ajuwĕt*

hana ta muwaḥ sira kryan apupul pupul ahayu raras,
walu-walu saŋ lumaḥ ry-anu patibrata lumaku wiku,
paṅawaśa niŋ nwam iŋ wayaḥ agatgat asalaha jamaŋ,
hana sĕmu niŋ manaḥ maru-marun mulat i nrĕpasuta*

hana wahu wahw-anūt karakĕtan siliḥ asiḥ akurĕn,
nrĕpaduhitā kahewa nika mĕṅgĕp aṅalĕm aṅupĕt,
tuhu-tuhu yan latā paḍa ni buddhi nika kadi nadī,
cumulu culuḥ priyanya pamawanya lulut i saŋ aja*

rara ri widaṙbbharājya makamukhya nrĕpatitanayā,
paḍa kĕna rāga-rāga nika tībra lumuŋ aṅalayan,
humañutakĕn lulut-lulut unĕŋnya mara ri saŋ aja,
bisa sira tan tĕñuḥ rinĕbut iŋ turida sanagara*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

osik buddhi nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,
sāmpun prāpta ri madhya niŋ pagĕlaran para ratu kĕna rāga de nira,
akweḥ bhāwa nira n wimūṙcchita hanan maṅuwahi makuṭa ndatan tulus,
dudw-a abhāwaka kady-aweḥ sĕpaḥ abhāwaka kadi tinĕwĕk miṅe midĕm*

len taŋ tībra lulut nira i nrĕpasutā humiḍĕp awak ira aṅisapwakĕn,
de niŋ rāgawaśa amarājaya tĕka amulaṅuni ya tinūtnya yan rimaŋ,
ṅhiŋ kāmīrasa lot ginoṣṭhi nira rāmya lawan ikaŋ amaṅku pawwahan,
moga aṅde tutuṙ iŋ gula drawa karĕṅwan i wacana nira anamaṙ juruḥ*

ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ rara ahayu lawan lituhayu sawawa an apaṅgiha,
ndan maṙmmanya n atĕmwa dūta lĕpihan pirĕsĕpakĕna riŋ pralāpita,
Āpan tan hana raśmi niŋ winaraŋ iŋ wwaŋ atuha tuna de nika alaṅö,
ṅhiŋ gandhaṙwwawiwāha rāmya katiga amawa sĕrĕḥ amisāta riŋ pasir*

luṅha ahĕmbana putra putran ika gantin arĕk arĕkana iŋ pararyanan,
liṅlīṅĕn kisapun kudaŋ  kudaṅĕn iŋ kakawin uliḥ iŋ aṅdadak-dadak,
yadyan māliha riŋ wukiṙ sipi laṅönya winulatan awikwa wikwana,
aṅhiŋ gīta panĕmba nĕmbaha nika n huwus inubhaya mantuka iŋ bibi*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

nāhan liŋ nira n aṅlipuṙ lipurakĕn kiṅkiŋ nira i twas nira,
kāsiḥ-kāsiḥ ira aṅlawan lawani goṣṭhy-a apan huwus wruḥ kawi,
wwaŋ śrĕṅgāra wicakṣaṇa aṅrahati sojaṙnya an asiḥ saŋ prabhu,
pet-pet haṙṣa sahuṙnya rāgakaraṇa wruḥ riŋ kasöṅan smara*

yan kanyā ri hiḍĕp patik haji hade kahyūnana apan raray,
tonĕn de nrĕpati ndya taŋ madhukarā hāna i kucup niŋ sĕkar,
lāwan yan lĕwasa ŋ rara apa pakĕnanya apan lĕwas riŋ raras,
paṅliṅganya sĕkaṙ lĕwas pisaniṅū kumbaŋ mara aṅambuṅa*

saŋkṣepanya sĕḍĕŋ rarā bwatana kiṅkiŋ hundaṅĕn riŋ ṭikā,
maṅgĕḥ de niŋ aṅolakĕn tĕṅaḥ ikā sāmpun pinaṅkw-a aṅliga,
kady-aṅgān i sĕkaṙ nikāŋ asana yan mĕmbaŋ katampwan riris,
ṅkāna ŋ ṣaṭpada miwya yan bhramara saṅjñānya n jĕnĕk tan midĕr*

nāhan denya n apet sahuṙ mĕtu rarasnya n pāwak iŋ rāsika,
tambā niŋ rimaŋ aṅlawaŋ lawaṅi kuŋ pet rāga denya aṅucap,
lwiṙ truḥ niŋ madhumāsa kāraṇa ni kiṅkiŋ śrī narendra asĕwö,
mambö ken lukaṙ iŋ tilam sahuṙ ira atuṅtuŋ rum iŋ saṅgama*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

kanyā liṅta hade kahaṙṣana paḍanya salaga kapana n kakūṅana,
kuŋ jaṅga aṅalayan tathāpi kapana n pamilĕta raras iŋ rara n lĕwas,
drĕṣṭāntanya sĕkaṙ lĕwas riŋ apa rakwa wulatana mĕne n kasumpiṅa,
kiṅkiŋ tībra yan iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara rarasnya paḍa-paḍa lawan jraḥ iŋ sĕkar*

ya ikā ta ika hade paṅawruhana campaka salaga nika n kinahyunan,
yadyan sumpiṅa niŋ maṅālihi hulĕs lĕwu raras ika yan pagantyana,
mambö rūmnya hana iŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan turaḥ ika rumĕsĕp tĕka i hati,
haryan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅwaŋ i sĕkaṙnya puru-puru rĕmĕk katiṇḍihan*

yan laywan pakasumpiṅĕn hana rarasnya tuhun asĕpi solaḥ iŋ lĕwas,
tĕkwan rakwa phalanya mogha pinalaywan asiŋ amupu luṅsuran sĕkar,
denya n mantĕna rūmnya yan pakirim iŋ wwaŋ ahayu panuwal nikā ṭikā,
ambönya n huwus aṅharas pipi ya ta arĕk arĕkana waṅinya kuṇḍaṅĕn*

mwaŋ yan strī hucapĕn rarasnya paḍa ta pwa kaharĕpana tan tayākĕna,
rūmrūm niŋ rara kanyakā kadi saroruha kumuḍu mijil saka iŋ bañu,
himpĕṙ paṅkaja karyakan wahu mĕkaṙ pamĕwĕḥ i raras iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara,
tan pendaḥ śatapattra wāhu lĕwas iŋ talaga hayu nikaŋ rara n lĕwas*

kanyā ta pwa wiśeṣa riŋ pawaraṅan raras ika marumaḥ lawan riris,
antuk niŋ maṅalap kasoṙ karaṇa niŋ tinarima marĕka aṅaras pipi,
riŋ paṅkwan winaraḥ riŋ akṣara manaḥ wahu tama wahu wanwa koluyan,
Āŋ aḥ wus kaka liŋnya mogha kawatĕk ri sĕḍĕŋ ika kinewala anukĕr*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ maṅaṙwwani hĕnū rumasa rasana rāmya niŋ kapat,
byakta alona lakunya sotan ika tan tahu mahas-ahas aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
tapwan wanwa dahat tuhun rĕṅu nika amarahakĕn i harĕpnya hĕmbanĕn,
suṇḍaŋ suṇḍaṅĕn iŋ tĕgal payuṅana asana hari harin iŋ pararyanan*

tan gyā gyākĕna de nikā lumaku mon karirisana ri madhya niŋ tĕgal,
yan paṅdöla paran kunaŋ wĕnaŋ akona pituhun ika yan lumampaha,
solaḥnya iriṅana apa tan wuruṅa luḥnya patulaka nikā yadin kĕdön,
ṅhiŋ gānya nya lumampaha n hana gĕrĕḥ maṅarahakĕna kāla niŋ rĕmĕŋ*

ndan yan rāmya nikaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara kapiŋ rwa niŋ arabi rĕsĕp twas iŋ mulat,
kas-kas pādapa kāṅinan kas i tĕṅaḥnya kinayuḥ aṅĕliḥ wawaŋ tumūt,
mwaŋ twasnya aṅasana aṅrĕṅö patĕṙ adan mĕkara hinudanan karāsikan,
kady-amrĕm kalawan puḍak ṅwaŋ aṅisapwakĕn arisi kanin ragĕt-ragĕt*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ lumampaḥ anukū sapara paran iŋ aṅraraḥ musuḥ,
śodha ata pwa hayunya nora kakuraŋnya mata waja nikā paḍa anulus,
mambö wīra raras-rarasnya tĕkap iŋ hañaŋ aṅiriŋ akālihan tapiḥ,
pantĕs-pantĕs anuṅgaṅa iŋ śakaṭa pamrĕgakĕna kahalĕpnya riŋ hĕnu*

aśrī raśmi nikaŋ rarā tuha kapiŋ tiga niŋ arabi mon kapiŋ pata,
prāya asiḥ wilaja n kinolakĕn anaṅgap i waja nika yan wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
dūra aṅrĕṅwana yan kisapwakĕna riŋ śayana pisaniṅūn apaṅgila,
eṅgal wanwa wisik pisan kadi sadoṣa ginupi tumuluy-kataṅgama*

yogya n rowaṅa niŋ licin wanawasa anusupa ri pasamūha niŋ sĕkar,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa niŋ mahas-mahas atīṙtha riŋ acala mahārakā gaḍuŋ,
līla anaṇḍaṅa walkala ajaṙ ajara analawaha jawuḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat,
śrī rājādayitā pi yogya ta ṅaranya n aduluṙ anusup lawan ratu*

nāhan de nira nātha mojaṙ apadudwan ulaḥ-ulaḥ ira n paḍa alulut,
buddhi śrī naranāthaputra milu rañca ri wulat ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,
mūṙccha apan wahu wahw-anon rakĕt aṅiṇḍarat anĕmu ṭikā tĕka alulut,
paŋ niŋ kūŋ asĕwö wilāpa kakawin tinama tama nira i dalĕm hati*

rakryan ṅke kahananku māsku mapa hetu niŋ asĕmu wiwal salaḥ wulat,
ahyun suṅsuṅĕn i ṅhulun karika māsku karaṇa niŋ arĕṅwa pet ulaḥ,
 Om   Om  haywa miṅe nihan ṅhulun amaṅkwakĕna ri kita milw-aḍampana,
taṅgap māsku sĕpaḥku sāmpun amiraḥ rumĕsĕpakĕna rāga ni ṅhulun*

dyaḥ saŋ sāgara katruhan luḥ apasiṙ panĕpi saŋ ahĕnī-hĕnī pupur,
muṅgw-i i jro hati kuṅta māsku kapana n rwaba sumapatana i kuŋ i ṅhulun,
ambĕk ni ṅhulun amriḥ aṅlayari tan wĕdi kajahata kombakan halis,
swaṙgga aku n karĕma iŋ tĕṅaḥta sukha kaprĕma kapaguta riŋ karaŋ susu*

rakryan saŋ madhu niŋ kaḍatwan uliḥ iŋ hyaŋ amituruni sāri niŋ sĕkar,
lwiṙ tawwan pakatonan iŋ kaka kaka aṅrubuŋ ahayu paḍa aṅisis wĕtis,
de niŋ hyunku tumon manista n agĕlaŋ gupura maṇi duwĕg pakolihĕn,
ndak lampū pĕtĕŋ iŋ mulat sakahananta ri dalĕm ibu rohĕn i ṅhulun*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

ndaḥ nāhan liŋ narendrātmaja ri hati nira apan sira bhrāntacitta,
rakryan putrī mara i śrī magadhapati pĕnuḥ wwaŋ manonton mara i jro,
awrĕg de saŋ sunandā kadi lanaŋ aṅusī sāhasa anĕmbuŋ iŋ hwī,
ramya awelā katon riŋ wĕkasan aṅililan śrī suputrī tinonton*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

mojaṙ śrī magadhādhipa i nrĕpasutā nihan ibu marĕka akisapwana,
socaṅkw-i ibu lawan matanta sakadaŋ paḍa-paḍa dadi niŋ gula drawa,
atyanta ibu hayunta tan patatalan tuhu-tuhu n awatāra niŋ ratiḥ,
heman māsku yatan papaṅgiha lawan ṅhulun apan awatāra niŋ smara*

wruḥ ku n tan hana sanmatanta hana duṣṭa marĕki ri kita amadohakĕn,
tonton denta matanta mĕṅgĕp amanis dumadak arĕṅu yan tumon ṅhulun,
paṅron wimba nikuŋ halista n abĕnĕṙ kuṭila milu ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ hiḍĕp,
tan saṅka iŋ hana doṣa kimburu manaḥta tĕka wiwal apeda ri ṅhulun*

rakryan janma ni janma ni ṅhulun adadyana ratu tumuta iŋ swayambara,
ndan rakryan ta muwaḥ swayambarakĕna amiliha ratu ri madhya niŋ sabhā,
denya n tan kinasanmatanta palalun sinalahasa ri tan siḥ iŋ widhi,
rāmya ṅwaŋ pinagantakĕn tulusa tan tulusa tuwi yaya apuput raras*

nāhan de magadheśwara aṅucap arūm amalaṙ i sahura nrĕpātmajā,
śrī dewi indumatī tan eṅĕḥ apa tan hana manaḥ ira keṅĕra i sira,
maṙmma śrī naranātha mantĕn aṅucap tĕhĕṙ amaḍĕm ikaŋ smara i hati,
wruḥ ri wyaṙtha ni kuŋ nira i nrĕpasutā n kadi wiphala niŋ ahyun iŋ tulis*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

ndaḥ mojaṙ saŋ sunandā ri narapatisutā liŋnya tiṅhal tuhanku,
nāhan ta śrī mahārāja magadhapati saŋ yogya petĕn siwinta,
yadyastun siddha rakryan sasisihana hulĕs dlāha lāwan narendra,
sakweḥ niŋ strī hana i jro nagara niyata tan sāha saṅka i padanta*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

sugyan tan wruha māsku yan śri magadheśwara sira maṅaran parantapa,
sāmpun śīṙṇna musuḥ nira awrĕg i kaḍatwan ika mati ri madhya niŋ raṇa,
aṅhiŋ pat lima śeṣa niŋ karahatan paḍa kawĕkas anūt mara i sira,
saŋkṣepanya yathāṙtta māsku sira yan prakaśita maṅaran parantapa*

yan riŋ wīṙyya lawan guṇa syapa sira aṅṅwihana sira yan paḍa prabhu,
waḥ riŋ mās maṇik uttama ndya ŋ adagaŋ lumĕwihana sira n dhaneśwara,
sāmpun pūṙṇna kadānaśūran ira kaprakaśita tĕka riŋ purāntara,
ṅhiŋ putrī kakuraŋ ni ghāra nira hetu niŋ aṅadu ri māskw-aṅĕdwakĕn*

wwantĕn deśa lĕṅĕŋ ri puṣpapura bhūmi nrĕpati pasamūhan iŋ kawi,
luḥ niŋ strī kĕna rāga rakwa talaganya pinarigi ri laywan iŋ gĕluŋ,
sambatnya n panaṅis ya ta aṅdadi madhubrata hana dadi cātaka iŋ tawaŋ,
mambö rūm ni mukhanya sāmpun atĕmaḥ kumuda mĕkaṙ i tambwaŋ iŋ wulan*

ṅkā ta induŋ parananta māmĕŋ amĕŋ an huwus atĕmu lawan nareśwara,
bhuktin siḥ nira denta rāmya niŋ atuntunan aduluṙ akālihan payuŋ,
ya ikā wīṙyya ṅaranya riŋ kadi kita ahayu pinuji yan amriḥ iŋ priya,
ramya aṅaṙwwana ḍampa riŋ para paran sipi wanĕḥ iŋ akālihan tilam*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– |– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

nāhan liŋ saŋ sunanda amanis araras arūm de nika akon atĕmwa,
sāmpun kājaṙ pratāpa nrĕpati lawan ikaŋ wīṙyya sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ,
ndātan mlecchā suputrī n inucapan aṅucap len saka i saŋ narendra,
moga asuṅsut mĕne n ahyuna kinĕdĕ kĕdö kewala adoḥ riŋ ambĕk*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

śrī dewi indumatī katon sĕmu ni buddhi nira n alalisa i nareśwara,
Āpan tan hana raśmi-raśmi ni wulat nira pinarĕkakĕn wawaŋ miṅe,
ya ikā hetu nira n kinon aṅaliha amwita rumuhun anĕmbaha i sira,
mambĕt madhya nira aṅgaluṅgaŋ i panĕmbaḥ ira kadi panĕmbaḥ iŋ tulis*

ry-aṅkat śrī nrĕpaputrikā śri magadheśwara kawĕlas arĕp kamānuṣan,
mary-a ateja sĕpaḥ nira asĕpa sigit sigitan ira tiba akusa iŋ lĕmaḥ,
tan śobha akilayū wulat nira sĕkaṙ nira maṅaway-awe hana iŋ kapö,
trĕṣṇā kūŋ ira tan katoliḥ inatīta nĕhĕṙ inilagan yayan tumūt*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

śrī dewi indumatī lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ prāpta i saŋ aṅgādhipa,
ndātan wany-asabha ahaliŋ haliṅan iŋ ceṭī paḍa akweḥ marĕk,
tan saḥ dyaḥ jayawaspa lot linihaṅan bāhunya kaṙwwa awiḍaŋ,
Āpan kāsiḥ ira alawas tuwin arūm tan soṙ dahat riŋ hayu*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

agyā ŋ buddhi saŋ aṅganātha ri ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā mara i sira,
mojaṙ tan panaha anĕkākĕn i lulut-lulut ira ri nareśwarātmajā,
ṅke rakryan mapa hetu niŋ kadi wiwal mulat ariris apakṣa maṅsula,
hāḥ wāliṅku tĕka akisapwana kita n tĕka dumadak adoḥ tĕka ŋ tamuy*

antĕnku n tuna kapwa siḥta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,
māskw-induŋ ndi wĕkas ni kuṅta palakuṅkwa hurupĕn i lara priḥ i ṅhulun,
rāganta mwaŋ unĕṅku denya n ahurup tali paṅuwata kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
wet niŋ tan hana sanmatanta palarĕṅkwa karika karaṇanta tan sahur*

dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa piniṇḍa ratnawanita aṅaraṅa karaṇa niŋ lanā lulut,
saŋ kiṅkiŋ ginawe rara ahayu sujanma karaṇa niŋ akuŋ tumon kita,
saŋ rāgānala maṅdadi wwaŋ amanas manasi hati kita n kinonĕṅan,
saŋ rĕs maṅdadi janma rājaduhita amuhara wĕdi niŋ ahyuna i kita*

nāhan de nira mojaṙ aṅrĕsi hati iniṅĕt iṅĕt apa tan kinahyunan,
heman wīṙyya nira mwaŋ uttama ni kaprabhun ira suyaśa adbhuta iŋ jagat,
riŋ rūpa asĕmu rūpa niŋ smara sawaṙgga lawan asana riŋ labuḥ kapat,
tan kewö wiphalaprayāsa hana tan pinakadi kadi kambaŋ iŋ caru*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

mantĕn śrī naranātha mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunanda aṅucap,
liŋnya dyaḥku harĕp kita wruha ri pāwak niŋ gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat,
nāhan māsku saŋ aṅganātha pahawās gĕntĕṙ madadyan ratu,
yogya atĕmwa lawan kitā kita tĕmaḥ niŋ cātaka amet jawuḥ*

ṅkāna i rājya saŋ aṅganātha wĕkas iŋ ramya i huwus niŋ laga,
ry-antuk saŋ prabhu maṅlurug saha bala lwiṙ waḥ saka iŋ paṙwwata,
gĕntĕṙ niŋ grit ikaŋ ratha anĕmahakĕn kuŋ ni wwaŋ iŋ kāṙttika,
luḥ niŋ strī kahañaŋ ri līna ni ratunya aṅde paḍĕt niŋ lĕbū*

ndan heman tuna rājalakṣmi satĕwĕknya n rājya niṙdewatī,
hetu śrī naranātha tan sthiti pijĕṙ luṅhā madewāśraya,
de niŋ hyūn ira n aṅhyaṅa ŋ nagara mogha n kewĕhan tan hana,
ṅhiŋ rakryan pakarājalakṣmi nira maṙmma de nira aṅundaṅa*

rakryan-yan hana sanmatanta ri sira anambāna kiṅkiŋ nira,
ndak pinta nya sĕkaṙ tajinta pamahugya mwaŋ sĕrĕḥ riŋ kajaŋ,
taṅgap denta mĕne sĕpaḥ nira katon heman yatan suṅsuṅĕn,
nya ŋ siṅhāsana kaṙwwananta pakisapwan māskw-i paṅkwan haji*

nāhan denya n aṅĕdwakĕn nrĕpasuta ahyun waspada i saŋ prabhu,
moga acūm ararĕm wulat nira sinuṅsuŋ riŋ wulat löṙ miṅe,
ndan dūra ahyuna kewala awĕdi kumöl ambĕk nira aṅdoḥ arĕs,
yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ mulat iŋ aṙcca aṅheṙ iŋ uṅgwan bhaya*

māliḥ śri indumatī riniṅriŋ inariḥ de saŋ sunanda amawa,
Āśābhūta saŋ aṅganātha ri layad dewī nĕhĕṙ tan waluy,
de niŋ bhrānta nira aṅikĕt rasa palambaŋ paṅlipuṙ luḥ pinöm,
ṅkāna i watwan ikaŋ salö panulisan maṙmmā rasanya amanis*

rakryan saŋ maliŋ-iŋ mata amatik i rūpaṅkw-a aṅĕḍap yan wulat,
kālap denta manaḥku mĕṅgĕp amanis rūpanta duṣṭa iŋ hati,
mukṣa twaskw-i sĕḍĕṅta mūṙ syapa ta len saṅka i kita aṅambila,
eman māsku tuhan-tuhan maliŋ atimpuḥ duṙyyaśakṣatriya*

rakryan haywa kita pramāda ri surup niŋ lek mĕne riŋ wĕṅi,
prāpta amora kakanta haywa kita tan yatnā ry-awakta iŋ jinĕm,
sāk niŋ ken awanaṅkwa mañjiŋ i parāhasyanta riŋ pamrĕman,
maṅgā matya mata aku pökana kukuṅku n paṅguhā riŋ pupū*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nahan rasa ni de nira ahyun amaliŋ maliṅana ri raras suputrikā,
agöŋ sukha nira n tibā manaḥ i saŋ katuduḥ arusita pwa riŋ manaḥ,
ri kāpusan ikaŋ smara apunagi yan waluyana sira de nrĕpātmajā,
lumakwa mapasaŋ pasaŋ wuyaha yan muliḥ iriŋ iriṅĕn mara i dalĕm*

atīta sira saŋ narendra maṅaraŋ tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,
sinuṇḍaŋ inamĕṙ kininkin aṅĕliḥ rasa tumayuṅa kabwatan raras,
tuwin manaḥ ira n prapañca kumĕtĕṙ hati nira mulat iŋ wwaŋ iŋ sabhā,
baṅun lumaku ri wwat ewĕḥ alĕyö maṅamĕṙ-amĕṙ i de nira n laku*

sahaṙṣa saŋ awantinātha ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ ahayu pinakahyaŋ iŋ sabhā,
hanan pasiḍakĕp hanan pasidĕha aṅuraḥ ariḥ ulaḥ iŋ girahyasĕn,
waḥ iŋ kapitu tan pahī wĕtu ni rāga nira ri naranāthaputrikā,
pĕnuḥ maṅarape tĕka iŋ kaka kaka anwam atuha sinarambahan lulut*

i maṅkana ni de nira n karakĕtan turida sinaput iŋ manobhawa,
tan enak aṅinaŋ tan enak aṅucap humĕnĕŋ apĕga ta n saya awĕnĕs,
sawet i pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,
ya kāraṇa nira aṅucap tan awiraŋ sumĕgĕ sĕgĕḥ i saŋ nrĕpātmajā*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rakryan bhāgya kita n ḍatĕŋ nihan aluṅguha yayi ri kisapwan i ṅhulun,
mās lāwan maṇik uttama aṙjja humaḍaŋ pakĕna nika panumbasa i kita,
yadyan kaprabhun i ṅhulun suṅakĕnaṅkwa ri kita yayi yan kita aharĕp,
yan praŋ yan kakawin panĕkwa ni kakanta ri kita yayi yan-n-apaṅgiha*

yan riŋ kāṙttikamāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕŋ-amĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅĕn i ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kakawinku riŋ yaśa,
yan māsa asujimāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕnĕm i rājya niŋ musuḥ,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa ni ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kawaninku riŋ raṇa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

nāhan de naranātha mojaṙ araras mambö laṅö niŋ jinĕm,
siṅgiḥ yan pracacaḥ karas waśa ri tuṅtuŋ niŋ tanaḥ riŋ kapö,
siŋ soṅkab ni tutuk nira awĕtu laṅö kāmīrasa apet manis,
pöḥ niŋ haṙṣa pinöm atūt guru laghunya aṙjja aṅĕnoḥ lambaṅa*

saŋ katwaŋ niŋ awaṙṇna campaka tumiṅhal sakṣaṇa i saŋ prabhu,
ceṣṭākāra nira inariḥ winulatan de saŋ sunanda ataña,
māskw-induŋ mapa buddhi rakryan i narendra n swāmya rakryan sira,
yogya apan kadi mūla tuṅgal apasaḥ maṅke n tĕmaḥ mānuṣa*

<upendrabajra> 
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 11

yadin kita atĕmwa lawan narendra,
ry-awantideśa atiśaya iŋ subhikṣa,
wwaŋ uttama wwaŋnya kawi iṅgitajña,
pacaṅkramānanta pasiṙ wukiṙnya*

gunuŋ mahākāla ṅaranya rāmya,
kapunpunan de saŋ awantinātha,
i pāṙśśwa pāṙśśwanya patīṙtha tīṙthan,
pĕnuḥ dwijaṙṣy-a ajaṙ ajaṙ tan imbā*

sabhā bhaṭāra iśwara nityakāla,
śiwāmbha sakweḥ ni bañunya śuddha,
kulĕm pwa saŋ hyaŋ tuwi krĕṣṇapakṣa,
yaya apaḍaŋ de nikaŋ aṙddhacandra*

paran tatan rāmya nikā parāna,
pamenana i kāla nikaŋ basanta,
ikaŋ lara agöŋ mala niŋ śarīra,
awās hilaŋ māry-aṅaweśa denya*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

tāman saŋ nātha tan popama halĕp ika sāmpun prakāśa adwitīya,
piṅgiṙ niŋ lwaḥ srĕp ātis ny-aṅin ika humaras gandha niŋ paṅkaja mrik,
sākṣāt swaṙggātmaka apan sahana-hana nikaŋ kĕmbaŋ aṅjraḥ paḍa arūm,
heman yan lena saṅka i kita śaraṇa ni kādewatanya n pinūjā*

nāhan de saŋ sunanda amirĕsĕpakĕn i saŋ yogya kaṙmmā sudewī,
ndān ambĕk śrī suputrī miṅay-atimĕs adoḥ tan hana ŋ rāga mātra,
sāmpun wruḥ saŋ sunandā karaṇa nika n akon muṅsira i saŋ pratīpa,
asrĕt lampaḥ nira alon laku-laku jalada anūtakĕn māruta alon*

ndan saŋ kāry-a aṅaraŋ sis kawĕlas arĕp ira ameri luḥ tan tinoliḥ,
baryan tiṅhal ri dewī sira rasa pĕjaha apan rĕmĕk twas nira syuḥ,
limbe-limbe sudewī kadi maṅaway-akon milwa ri śrī narendra,
wet niŋ bhrānta aṅikĕt bhāṣa ri saruṅan ikaŋ patrĕm aṅrĕs rasanya*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ṅhulun yaśana rāga māsku pakadhaṙmman ĕnahana raras niŋ aṅrĕṅiḥ,
hayunta makawāṇḍiranya ya paṅöbana para-paranaṅkwa yan rimaŋ,
prasĕnta ri dalĕm jinĕm titisananta luḥ i lukaṙ i kenta riŋ tilam,
susunta pakasādhananta kalawan pipi katiga tĕṅaḥ maran lĕpas*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

nāhan de śrī narendra anĕmahakĕn i lulut kuŋ nira awak wilāpa,
ya ikī tan saḥ ri paṅkwan winaca tiniliṅan koŋ rinĕṅwan winaswās,
adrĕs luḥ śrī narendra aṅrasani rasa nika apan katuhwan rasanya,
yogya aṅantya iŋ mahantĕn wacan iŋ alaradan kālapan ratnakanyā*

rakryan putrī huwus māliḥ asĕmu paṅaliḥ niŋ sĕkaṙ sālas aṅjraḥ,
kweḥ niŋ guṇḍik nira mwaŋ kaka-kaka rumara aṅasturi mrik waṅinya,
lagy-a ataṅkis humuŋ hambuluṅan i tali kenya anamaṙ ṣaṭpada strī,
haṙṣa ambĕk saŋ pratīpa amapag iŋ ujaṙ arūm tustus iŋ laṅwa-laṅwan*

<krĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏓ : 20

ibu t asy-asiḥ kita kadaŋ kadaṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ i ṅhulun rimaŋ,
kita yogya mitra kulabandhw-amarasana ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
pakawaṙgga ni ṅhulun i paṅkwan asisihana raśmi niŋ prĕman,
arĕnaḥ manahkw-aṅaku sānak iri kita patĕmwan iŋ jaja*

pakĕnaṅkwa yan marĕk i māskw-amibikana laṭinta riŋ waja,
lumut iŋ payodhara huwus kakiṅan usapanaṅkwa riŋ jaja,
iruŋ i ṅhulun panutulaṅkwa luḥ i pipi ri pamriḥ iŋ sipat,
lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ salinanaṅkwa karatala mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

ndaḥ ya iki n liŋ narendra arasa mijila saka iŋ bhāṣa lāwan palambaŋ,
sotan ta ŋ sāri niŋ rāga piturun i laṅö niŋ kawi bhrāntacitta,
tan paṅgintiṙ manis niŋ tĕbu sawukiṙ apan tan patuṅtuŋ manisnya,
maṙmma anyuḥ prāṇa rūmnya asĕmu paṅucapan iŋ wahw-amaṅkw-a aṅdudut ken*

rakryan putrī mulat riŋ nrĕpati kadi wulat niŋ ṭikā riŋ wilāpa,
mojaṙ ta dyaḥ sunandā wwaya ta sira siwin śakty-asaṅjñā pratīpa,
sākṣāt swaṙgga anurun rūpa ni nagara nira ry-a anupa khyāti riŋ rāt,
kumbaŋ kĕmbaŋ papaṅgiḥta kadi patĕmu niŋ kāṙttika mwaŋ basanta*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ aṙjjuna sahasrabāhu riŋ usāna sira siniwi śakti nītimān,
prakāśa sira saŋ daśānana musuḥ nira huwus ayaśa amatī musuḥ,
tathāpi kaparājaya iŋ raṇa huwus hinuripan alawas pinañjara,
hana pwa sira saŋ pratīpa sira rakwa wĕka nira suśīla digjaya*

paran pwa wĕkas uṅsirĕnta paḍa wastu kita wĕka niŋ uttamaprabhu,
para prabhu kapan paḍa asira lawan sira tĕwas amilĕt milĕt wulat,
ameta kita len muwaḥ tĕwas aṅel midĕṙ ibu kapana n pamaṅgiha,
mataŋnya sira sĕṅgahĕnta kaka yogya sira manuwala iŋ ujaṙ yayi*

<śikhariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ : 17

yadin siddhā rakryan sasisihana rūm niŋ siliḥ asiḥ,
awās rakryan glāna ahuyaŋ apupul i jro pakasutan,
hana lwaḥ ramya alwā prakaśita si rewā ṅaran ika,
kita adyūsa ṅkāna isuḥ isuhana lāwan saŋ ahulun*

raras niŋ kaṙwwa swāmi paran ika rakwa aṅṅwihana,
marā riŋ tāman tan hana marĕka līlā ṅwaŋ aṅĕnĕs,
yadin madyūsa iŋ lwaḥ talaga wulakan śūnya kasĕnĕt,
wĕnaŋ sāmbĕk niŋ swāmi tariman apan tan hana mulat*

kalīṅanya alaḥ māsku marĕka nihan dak parĕkakĕn,
paran maṙmmanta asuṅsut arĕṅu miṅe tan pamituhu,
paṅanti i paṅkwan saŋ prabhu hila-hila ŋ duhkha siwuhĕn,
apan māskw-a apet-pet hayu pahayu buddhinta ri sira*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

nāhan liŋ saŋ sunanda amirĕsĕpakĕn i tiṅkaḥ narāṙyya pratīpa,
pathya wruḥ sopapatti iṅgita nikaŋ ucap akrĕp kĕna priḥ narendra,
ya aṅde tan saṅśaya i twas nira ri ḍatĕṅa rakryan suputri i kisapwan,
kady-aṅhyaŋ motusan wallabha mamagĕhakĕn tan wuruŋ niŋ swakāṙyya*

rakryan putrī miṅe tan wawarĕṅĕḥ apa tan trĕpti rakwa i narendra,
saŋ nātha wruḥ sira n tan kinaharĕpan ikaŋ buddhi maṅkin prapañca,
Āśābhūta anulis ketaka rasa kakawin pöḥ nikaŋ rāga tībra,
tambā niŋ keraṅan tan winadal i liḍaḥ iŋ kāma nāhan rasanya*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

ibu tan paphala pwa ŋ amalaṙ i hayunta sĕḍĕṅta rare,
syapa māsku kadi ṅhulun aṅurati rāga lawan turida,
katunan lĕpihan kita kinirimakĕnku karaskw-i kita,
tĕka riŋ kararan pwa kita mapa tiki n sahaja api lupa*

sĕḍĕŋ iŋ pabĕlaḥ turida kinĕkĕsanku kita iŋ lĕpihan,
makasādhana kuṅkw-aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt i rūmta lanā n pinalar,
aṅadĕg pwa kita iŋ puḍak araras inastwakĕn iŋ bhramara,
winaliṅku kita aŋ liṅa puji-puji yan ratu niŋ kusuma*

saŋ apiṇḍa wukiṙ ṅhulun ajaṙ ajara i kita muṅgwa sadā,
tarukāṅkw-i hayunta pamiṣayana rāga sĕḍĕṅkw-alulut,
licina iŋ śayana akw-anusupa ri hulĕsta sugandha miṅiŋ,
sipi māsku sukhaṅku katuruna ri soṙ i tĕṅaḥta rari*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

nāhan de śrī narendra akakawina maṅani twas nira i jro drawa aṅras,
ndātan tiṅhal muwaḥ riŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā kewala iraŋ tumuṅkul,
māry-a aśābhūta sāmpun pinĕgat ira lulut kuŋ nira i śrī suputrī,
hetunya n tan wijil luḥ nira pamaḍĕm ira iŋ rāgabahni i dalĕm twas*

sāmpun māliḥ sudewī kasusu laku nira aṅĕñcuḥ ĕñcuḥ kaṅelan,
ndan tiṅhal saŋ susena aṅiriṅakĕn aṅamĕṙ tan wĕnaŋ sāḥ amaṇḍĕŋ,
kady-a adandan kisapwan yan alihan asila ahyūn amaṅkwa i sudewī,
haṙṣa agyā gyān anuṅsuŋ riŋ ujaṙ akakawin lwiṙ katona iŋ palambaŋ*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rakryan saŋ pinunagyakĕnku śaraṇāśraya tumuluṅa kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
aṅlū māsku kisapwan i ṅhulun aluṅguha kita yayi haywa saṅśaya,
t asy-a asiḥ kita māsiha i kawi guṇaṅku palaṙ amalĕsa iŋ karāsikan,
lambā kaprabhun i ṅhulun kita rumaṅkĕpana saphala yogya tuṅgalĕn*

maṅke n prāpta ni māsku tambay-iŋ anon wwaŋ ahayu kadi dewakanyakā,
yan riŋ śūnya katĕmwananta saha bhūṣaṇa maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
byakta anĕṅgaha dewatī kalĕmahan ṅhulun iri kita dūra saṅśayā,
Āpan de ni hayunta yogya kita māsku panadinakĕna n pinaṅkwakĕn*

paṅkwankw-i ibu paranti niŋ wwaŋ anukĕṙ-nukĕṙ aṅĕsaḥ-ĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
śīṙṇna syuḥ lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun pinakarantunan i kuku niŋ epu tan panūt,
tan pamwas jaja ni ṅhulun wahu waras linawad i panĕpak niŋ aṅrĕṅiḥ,
lagy-emö pipi ni ṅhulun sabha sabhā ni waja niŋ anulak wineḥ sĕpaḥ*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

sojaṙ saŋ nātha kady-a aṅalapana kasusuk niŋ kĕna iŋ rāgapāśa,
kady-a anambāna kiṅkiŋ niŋ amalaku suwal kewĕhan kāladeśa,
sākṣāt sambat niŋ onĕŋ kinirimakĕn apet pet manis de ni kuŋnya,
mambö rūm niŋ katurwan winuṅu ni jarumanya anĕkākĕn wilāpa*

tatkāla śrī suputrī sapawulatan aṅanti i harĕp saŋ susenā,
tan kantun saŋ sunandā marĕk ataña tĕhĕṙ sopacāra atalaṅkup,
rakryan sāmpun kita wruḥ ri narapati mapa ambĕkta māsku n patĕmwa,
Āpan saŋ nātha sākṣāt madana midĕṙ amet hyaŋ ratī riŋ kaḍatwan*

yadyastun māsku siddha aṅhaturakĕna hayunta iŋ kisapwan narendra,
ṅkāna iŋ gĕṅgā kita amena mahas ahasa riŋ nūsa śūnya i tĕṅaḥnya,
mwaŋ yan rakryan mara iŋ wrĕndawana taman ira anopama iŋ laṅwa laṅwan,
akweḥ bhuktinta ramya amarĕkana yamunā lālana akuwwa-kuwwa*

rakryan putrī tan eṅĕḥ sira kinĕdĕ kĕdö yan paniwya i narendra,
siṅgiḥ rakwa n rarā suṇṭi masĕmu lĕṅa suṇṭy-a akalis de nira ambĕk,
ndan buddhi śrī susenā kadi pulut atĕguḥ tan lumeṙ de nira ahyun,
saŋkṣepanya ndi tan siddha kapalikĕtana śrī suputri i narendra*

luṅhā lampaḥ sudewī narapati kawĕkas keraṅan tan tinoliḥ,
kady-agriŋ nora rakwa aṅinaki laṅu laṅun yan mulat riŋ sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,
rakryan putrī juga anuṅgayap i hati nira atyanta riŋ priṅga wiṣṭi,
maṅkin bhrānta aṅikĕt bhāṣa panalimuṙ ira i tībra niŋ rāga tikṣṇa*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

dyaḥ maḥ luṅsuran i ṅhulun pasuṅa ni ṅhulun iri kita māsku taṅgapĕn,
siñjaŋ siñjaṅa rakryan iŋ paṅaraṅan ri huwus iŋ anulis pralāpita,
göŋ ny-a asiḥku ri māsku yogya suwalĕn ṅhulun amalaku luṅsuran tapiḥ,
donya ibū pinakātmarakṣa n amĕrĕnkw-abasahana tĕhĕṙ pamera luḥ*

rakryan saŋ hinarĕp harĕpku śaraṇāśraya mulata ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
tan sa inuṅsiṙ adoḥ manaḥta salawasku tĕka ri kita mogha tan liniŋ,
ṅhiŋ gānyā hana kāsihanta ḍatu ḍatwa kahulunana tan saha i kita,
ya ikī pañjiṅanaṅkwa nitya saparan ṅhulun aṅucap ucap lawan kita*

nāhan bhāṣa nira n tiniṅgalakĕn iŋ paṅaraṅan i layat suputrikā,
mantĕn duhkha nira asamun turida rāga ni manaḥ ira tan tinūtakĕn,
śrī hemāṅgada kabwatan kuŋ i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā mara i sira,
wwāgan mogha gumanty-amukti lara rāga niyata sira tan kinahyunan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

śrī dewi indumatī ḍatĕŋ sira ri saŋ sāmpun kaciṙyyan smara,
ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp harĕp nira lawan tan hyūn ira i saŋ prabhu,
ndān eman wĕkasan kataṙkkan i kalis ny-ambĕk nira n tan rimaŋ,
aṅhiŋ piŋ rwa mulat kapiŋ rwa sahaja atuṅtuŋ tikĕl niŋ halis*

sāmpun waspada doḥ i rāga nira tan tuṅgal panononana,
suṅsut-suṅsut ira n kinon marĕka len tiṅhal nira aṅrĕṅwani,
Ākāra iṅgita niŋ manaḥ saha wijil niŋ śabda nora akadi,
ahyun kawruhana n tan ahyun ika kaprajñān ira apet wiwal*

tan wruḥ śrī naranātha yan tan aharĕp rakryan suputri i sira,
aṅgĕṅgöŋ kamadan trĕṇāṅkura hiḍĕp saŋ nātha riŋ wwaŋ kabeḥ,
hamham paṙccaya de ni rūpa nira tĕkwan śakti wāni iŋ raṇa,
kĕdw-a akuŋ makasoŋ lara unĕŋ ira yan pojaṙ waśa akon marā*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ sākṣāt smarakanyakā saŋ anarīra ri hati saŋ amiṇḍa riŋ hiḍĕp,
buddhiṅkw-a alal aṅantyakĕn siha ni māskw-ahuyaŋ ajaruman pralāpita,
maṅke pwā tĕka tan wawaŋ marĕk awaṙṇna kĕna guṇa miṅe kita ariris,
rakryan haywa kakanta māsku sinaranta kalalaḥ ibu rāga ni ṅhulun*

saṇḍaŋ bhakta samotusankw-apuyĕŋ an layat alisuḥ amet rara ahayu,
ndātan poliḥ aṅel aṅulwan aṅawetan aṅidĕri kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ,
maṅke pwa n hana māskw-arūm pakawayaŋ wayaṅĕn amĕrĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,
tan pātmā rasa kaprĕman saśayana anĕkĕnakĕna śarīra ni ṅhulun*

nāhan de naranātha mojaṙ awuyuŋ sira wĕkasan adoḥ suputrikā,
śrī putrī katibān ujaṙ haji tan eṅĕḥ apuji sira yan tuhan-tuhan,
Ājñālaṅghana yogya daṇḍan apa tan hana sahuṙ ira pakṣa māliha,
simbantĕn haji moliha amidhi balik sira kawidhi dinaṇḍa niŋ smara*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

sakweḥ saŋ marĕk uttamottama wiwal munduṙ paḍa amid miṅe,
aṅheman ri narendra yan sira tan antuk śrī suputrī mulat,
mwaŋ strī-strī paricārikā paḍa humuŋ maṅyogyani i saŋ prabhu,
ḍyam ta iki i wĕkasan tuhun hana mulat yan saŋ sunanda aṅucap*

rakryan tiṅhalana atpada nrĕpati sākṣāt ṣaṭpada amet sĕkar,
maṅheṙ-heṙ i dalĕm taman makapaṅanty-antyan kucup niŋ mĕnur,
maṅke n mūṙ aṅaliḥ cumuṇḍuk i widaṙbbha apakṣa tan mantuka,
Āpan maṙmma nira n ḍatĕŋ kita karĕṅw-an paṅjraḥ iŋ campaka*

śrī hemāṅgada laṅwa-laṅwan asana ndātan mĕkaṙ kābunan,
saŋsāra kṣaya saŋsaya aluru lume de niŋ smarākhya apanas,
heman māsku kucup ni buddhi nira yan tan sanmatan kāsihan,
ṅhiŋ gānya n mĕkara n kita aṅlawada māskw-a apan gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat*

wwantĕn rājya nira i kaliṅga kita yogya hyaŋ hyaṅanya ahalĕp,
tĕkwan paṙśśwa nikaŋ mahendragiri hetunya n kadi indrālaya,
gĕntĕṙ ny-ampuhan iŋ mahodadhi karĕṅw-a agĕnturan tan pĕgat,
aṅhiŋ donya mamuṅwa saŋ prabhu lawan māsku n katurwān apöm*

rakryan tan kasasaṙ hayunta kawawa i saŋ nātha hemāṅgada,
Āpan buddhi nira abĕnĕṙ tan arusit wruḥ ry-ambĕk iŋ dug rimaŋ,
hĕnwanta n marĕka i kisapwan ira kewalya ṅhulun tan saha,
ya ikī don i manĕḥta mājara ri māṙgganta n sukha asaṅgama*

aṅhiŋ yogya siwinta tan patatalan trus tuñjuŋ iŋ kaprabhun,
prajñā wany-anulus bisa aṅaji dhanurweda adhika wruḥ nira,
yan riŋ kīṙtty-aniwāṙyya śuddha hana soṙ niŋ candrawimba akucĕm,
tustus niŋ ratu śakti digjaya sĕkaṙ tajy-aṅkuran kṣatriya*

nāhan de niŋ amet manis niŋ aṅucap mambö juruḥ kābunan,
antuk niŋ maṅalap manis ni kakawin saŋ wrĕḍdha wrĕddhi iŋ laṅö,
ndātan paṅgarit aṙddha tan rĕsĕp i buddhi śrī narendrātmajā,
luṅhā wruḥ tumuluy-sira n kinĕḍapan de saŋ sunanda aṅaliḥ*

śrī hemāṅgada kāri keraṅan akiṅkiŋ tan wĕnaŋ sāhasa,
maṅga amora makilya kilyana tumūta i śrī narendrātmajā,
saŋ hyaŋ manmatha duṣṭa tan rwa tĕlu pat rowaŋ nira aśa alara,
ya ikī hetu nira aṅikĕt rasa wilāpa aṅras rasanya i hati*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

maṅko pwa antĕnku denta ambĕk atiśaya dahat kewala aṅgöŋ kaputryan,
buddhinta apyak mada iŋ haṙṣa tan akuŋ iŋ akuŋ saŋsaya apy-a awalepa,
denta aweḥ rāga tan popama kadi ginawe lĕŋlĕŋa aku n tumiṅhal,
māyā muṅgw-iŋ crĕmin lwiṙtta riŋ apa wĕnaṅaṅkwa aṅisapwa i tuwuḥta*

saŋ lwīṙ aṙcca aṅaraŋ byakta pan ulaha ni māskw-i ṅhulun yan pamaṅkwa,
saŋ lwiṙ dewi i tulis tan wuruṅa kasarika aku n mara i pamrĕmanta,
saŋ lwiṙ wwe niŋ samudra aṅaraṅakĕn i manaḥku n surud siḥta māsku,
saŋ tuṅtuŋ ni rwi niŋ ketaka kari kacarik twaskw-i luṅhānta maṅko*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

nāhan manis ni paṅikĕt nira rāgacihna,
śrĕṅgāra rāsika pinöm atĕmaḥ wilāpa,
muṅgw-i i dalĕm hati ginūḍha raras-rarasnya,
pinrāṙthanākĕn ira mĕtwa mĕne n papaṅgiḥ*

saŋ lwiṙ hyaŋ iŋ jalada kāṅinan iŋ basanta,
ndātan panis nisi huyaŋ ni manaḥ niŋ onĕŋ,
luṅhā lawan riris i buddhi nira i narendra,
saŋ nātha kāri tĕlĕs i drĕs i luḥ nira aṅdyus*

byātīta saŋ prabhu narendrasutā wiwakṣan,
dolāyamāna ri turuŋ ni manaḥ nira isi,
luṅha amiliḥ-miliḥ i jalwa nira i narendra,
himpĕṙ sĕkaṙ midĕṙ amet bhramara i kuwuŋnya*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ sira ri sanmukha saŋ narendra,
śrī pāṇḍya haṙṣa kadi tan rat ira n tumiṅhal,
runtuḥ lĕbuṙ manaḥ ira asĕmu rāgabahni,
lwiṙ mās hana iŋ muṣa wawaŋ drawa de niŋ apwī*

saŋ pāṇḍya siṅhapuruṣākrĕti rāgaśatru,
śrī putrika aciri wĕdi n para riŋ paḍöman,
söḥ buddhi sattwa naranātha paḍa awrĕg awri,
keṇḍit manaḥ nira lawan kuŋ ira i dalĕm twas*

sāmpun pĕtĕŋ twas ira söḥ turida aṅaweśa,
aṅhiŋ hineṙ siliḥ asiḥ naranāthaputrī,
Āpan katon mukha nira asĕmu śītaraśmi,
ya ikī nimitta nira mojaṙ amanwa-manwa*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ṅke siṅhāsana māskw-aluṅguha paran karaṇa niŋ aṅadĕg baṅun wiwal,
rākanta alawas aṅrĕṅö ri hayu rakryan ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun ḍatĕŋ,
tĕkwan śrī naranātha bhoja maṅutus ḍatĕṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,
nāhan taŋ karas esi bhāṣa pahulaṅkwa ri kita yayi hantusākĕna*

wruḥ ku n tan paṅĕnoha kuṅku ri kita apan ahayu sakadaŋ lawan ratiḥ,
tuṅgal rakwa rarasta riŋ mukha lawan rĕsĕp i raras i māsku riŋ pupū,
rāgaṅkw-i ibu hana iŋ tĕṅaḥta kapipis lara turida kinölwa riŋ susu,
lampūn kaprĕma riŋ pasaṅgaman i paṅhapit i wĕtis i māsku ri ṅhulun*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

sojaṙ narādhipati tan palawan manisnya,
maṅgiṣṭa śiṣṭa mari śiṣṭa sinorakĕnya,
lwiṙ tan madhu ŋ madhu tinaṇḍiṅakĕn yayān sor,
lambā manis-manis ikaŋ gula tan panaṅkĕp*

śrī putrikā sira mulat ri harĕp narendra,
ndātan kapūhan apa tan hana paṅgaritnya,
moga akalis manaḥ ira asĕmu tan panaṅgĕl,
kady-adwa tiṅhal ira kewala tan papiṅrwa*

do-doḥ i buddhi nira niścaya saŋ sunandā,
śrī pāṇḍya tiṅhal ira kady-aṅutus maṅĕdwa,
ndan saŋ kinon ira bisa aṅupacāra śabda,
mojaṙ tuhun pali-palin ya tĕkapnya mojar*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nāhan śrī naranātha pāṇḍya sira yogya paṅayatan i māsku riŋ hayu,
heman rūmta yatan pagĕgwan i manis-manis ira n aṅisapw-aṅolakĕn,
aṅhiŋ sambhawa rakwaṅöbana huyaṅta saphala parĕkĕnta riŋ tilam,
siŋ sojaṙ haji yan rahasya rasan iŋ śayana kĕmitananta cupwana*

yadyastun kita māsku n a amĕŋ amĕṅa iŋ tuha rawa kalawan nareśwara,
byakta anaṅśaya cakrawāka dadi mānuṣa maṭika ṭikan mariŋ ḍarat,
mwaŋ yan kaṙwwa narendra māsku mahasa iŋ pasisi mĕgila riŋ wwaŋ iŋ pasir,
byakta anĕṅgaha dèwa niŋ mithuna rāśi mĕtu harĕp ahimya himyana*

atyanta iŋ kalaṅön lĕyĕp winulatan patĕmu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,
ndan dūra amaḍana i laṅö ni patĕmunta matĕmu kalawan nareśwara,
yadyāpin paḍa riŋ laṅö pisaniṅū kadi rarasa ni māskw-asaṅgama,
ṅhiŋ gānya amaḍana i rarasta raras iŋ rati madana n akālihan hulĕs*

<mālinī> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 15

nahan ucapan ika apet pet manis tan pamandi,
kadi rĕsĕpa rasanya i buddhi rakryan suputrī,
kunaŋ apa tan ika aṅde haṙṣa riŋ haṙṣa niŋ len,
wiphala kadi manis niŋ twak yan iŋ madyasakta*

narapatitanaya aṅliḥ tan sahuṙ lwiṙ tulis mās,
rĕṅu nira paṅadeśan yan tan aṅga amituhwa,
kalalu laku nira aṅdoḥ mūṙ lawan saŋ sunandā,
nrĕpati kawĕkas ākuŋ śīghra māwak wilāpa*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rakryan saŋ kĕna rāga tībra kaka rakryan aṅuwatana haywa saṅśaya,
hrū saŋ hyaŋ madana i hatinta dahutĕṅkwa bĕbĕdĕn i taṅanku hĕmbana,
ṅhiŋ jampyanta karāsikanku n amĕkul garĕgĕtĕn amijĕt-mijĕt susu,
romanta ajumĕn i ṅhulun sadakanaṅkwa n anĕsĕpi laṭinta riŋ tilam*

kocap māsku wicakṣaṇa uṇḍahagi yogya panagara bisa amaṅun lulut,
ṅke ta dyaḥ mata ni ṅhulun sipatananta pĕnĕdĕn usapanta riŋ pusuḥ,
yan kālanta pinaṅkwakĕn wwaya jajaṅku rari siku-sikunta yan cala,
kuṅta mwaŋ turidaṅku pādwakĕna māsku patitisana luḥ maran rapĕt*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nahan tĕmahan iŋ prapañca ni manaḥ nrĕpati wahu lipuṙ linaṅwakĕn,
hana ambĕk ira mantuka amruda tuhun mawaraha rumuhun ri saŋ prabhu,
katon ujara niŋ mulat ri sira tan pamahayu kadi buddhi niŋ rare,
