ya hetu nira tan wawaŋ muliḥ aṅantyakĕn i huwusa niŋ swayambara*

byatīta ri sĕḍĕŋ nira n mari rimaŋ tucapa sahana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ sabhā,
manaḥnya paḍa pakṣapāta ri narendrasuta tan aharĕp ri saŋ prabhu,
paḍa asraŋ aṅucap ry-uliḥ nrĕpasutā wruḥ i harĕpa nira iri saŋ haja,
alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikana aṅgĕtĕm asahuran atry-aṅadwakĕn*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rāga śrī naranāthaputra masĕwö kadi kayu ragas iŋ labuḥ kapat,
osik buddhi nira i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasutā winaliŋ ira tĕka akisapwana,
agya aweha sĕpaḥ saka i waja siliḥ suwala guyu panaṙkka niŋ mulat,
bwat śrĕṅgāra dahat panāntwa nira maṙmma rasa nika rĕsĕp rinĕṅwakĕn*

ṅke rakryan pakisapwan onĕŋ alawas ṅhulun ibu saŋ apiṇḍa nīrada,
saŋ saṅhub ni lulutku saŋ patĕṙ i kuṅku kilat i pĕtĕŋ i twas i ṅhulun,
saŋ rĕm niŋ turida aṅalaḥ siḥ apuput huyaŋ amĕkasakĕn putĕk hati,
saŋ truḥ-truḥ ni laṅöṅku mukṣa hiniḍĕp kinisapu sahaja atĕmaḥ riris*

donkw-aṅlitlita roma rakryan anapak napaka hayu ni māsku riŋ tilam,
Āpan tan hana len pramāṇa ri rarasta n aṅaraŋ aṅisapwakĕn puḍak,
māskw-induŋ huniṅan ṅhulun ri manis iŋ mata sarasija kābunan madhu,
suṅsuŋ rāga tĕṅaḥ puriḥta kalawan pipi taḍaha ni luḥta pintanĕn*

paṅkwankw-i ibu wĕtĕḥ turuŋ pinakapaṅrĕṅihan iŋ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
tapwan kāni lĕṅĕnku de ni kuku niŋ hinari hari miṅe kinolakĕn,
mwaŋ tapwan katĕpak jajaṅku kalawan pipi tĕkap iŋ arĕs kinewala,
ṅhiŋ rakryan karaṇanya n emwa ragĕta mwaŋ anuluṅa manĕmbu nĕmbura*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

ṅke saŋ apiṇḍa nirātmaka tinĕmahakĕn maṇi rājasutā,
tan hana ṅūni dĕlāha kadi kita sujanma suśīla wagĕd,
saŋ dadi janma saka iŋ taya-taya kadi rakryan arūm anulus,
māsku śaśāṅkawimāna karika kita maṅdadi maṙmma dahat*

aṅgriṅi simbali rakryan amarasana mogha tĕka aṅlarani,
dyaḥku nihan tuluṅĕn ṅhulun uwatana kāraṇa niŋ warasa,
griŋ kĕna rāga laraṅkw-aṅinak inaki mĕṅgĕp atīs apanas,
māsku mataŋ yan akaṙ pipi guliga tĕṅaḥ palakun ri kita*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nāhan de saŋ aja aṅucap mĕtu raras ni kataruṇan ira aṅhiḍĕp smara,
mambö turwan i paṅkwan aṅharas i paṅlawad iŋ ahayu riŋ pasaṅgaman,
kady-aṅrĕṅwa rĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsaḥ iŋ kinisapu rasa niŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,
śrī dewi indumatī pwa muṣṭi niŋ akuŋ kapana sira n aṅiṣṭya mintara*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

ujaṙ saŋ aja waṙṇna waṙṣa tumiba anĕkarakĕn asana aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,
aśoka ḍinĕḍĕṙ sawaŋ nrĕpasutā wahu kasiram alūŋ apādapa,
wawaŋ sĕkaṙ ira anĕḍĕŋ bhramara tan hana wani mara kewala atilar,
apan saŋ aja rakwa tan wuruŋ aṅol aṅarĕkana mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*

narendratanaya awĕnĕs mulat i rūpa saŋ aja wawaŋ agriŋ aṅlayuŋ,
kasambĕt i manis-manis ni luṅid iŋ mata sarasija keṅgutan halis,
huwus wruḥ i manis nira n kasarik iŋ lituhayu subhaga iŋ swayĕmbara,
ya kāraṇa nira aharĕp marĕka paṅkun uwat uwatana iŋ sĕpaḥ sarik*

sawet ni pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,
tinaṙkka nira rājaputra dadi niŋ smara saŋ aja mara iŋ swayĕmbara,
muwaḥ saŋ aja saŋsaya anaha nahā mulat i hayu narendraputrikā,
ratiḥ karika sinwayĕmbarakĕn iŋ madananagara liŋ nira i hati*

sipat nrĕpasutā lutuṙ kadi humeṙ i paṅusapa nareśwarātmaja,
gĕluŋ nira baṅun harĕp suruyana i jariji nrĕpatiputra yan lukar,
aṅrĕs kadi harĕp kadĕmwanana de saŋ aja mata nira aṅdadak lumuḥ,
paniṅsĕt i tapiḥ nira asĕmu harĕp lukarana ni taṅan nrĕpātmaja*

waja nrĕpatiputra kātara rarasnya tĕka ta mamusuḥ yan iŋ laṭi,
alal kĕtĕ kĕtĕg nira iŋ jaja lumiṇḍihana jaja narendraputrikā,
asaṅgraha nakha aluṅid taṅan ira amiraḥ aharĕp adun lawan susu,
tĕka iruŋ ira tan pakāla kumĕsut sĕmu-sĕmu niŋ asĕṅhit iŋ pipi*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan saḥ i narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
lāwan dyaḥ jayawaspa kāsiḥ ika tan saḥ i pada naranāthaputrikā,
ndan rakwa inalapan sĕḍĕŋnya n ahañaŋ tinut ika mapasaḥ madum tuhan,
tĕmbenya n sapatiṅhalan paḍa lumuḥ kawĕlas arĕp aluṅluṅan taṅis*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa mājaṙ i narendratanaya nĕhĕṙ aṅhĕmū taṅis,
rakryan honya manĕḥta tiṅhalana pun marika makaṅaran madhūdakā,
pun muṅgw-i i hiriṅan marĕk linihaṅan wagĕd araras amaṅku pawwahan,
aṅhiŋ pun juga tan wĕnaŋ mulat awaṙṇna lara mata n aṅölakĕn taṅis*

yadyastun nrĕpaputrikā mara mĕne humaturakĕna rūm nira i kita,
rakryan tan wĕnaŋ ediha i sira yadin sira tumĕṅĕta pun madhūdakā,
dūra n dhāraka riŋ lara smara manĕḥta pinasahakĕn iŋ tuhan-tuhan,
ṅhiŋ maty-a aṅaraṅa i daganta bapa tan panĕmu kahulunan sadā marĕk*

mwaŋ yan śri indumatī tan aptya ri tuhanku muliha sira tan panoliha,
suṅsut śrī naranātha rakwa ri manĕḥta bapa maṅulanĕḥ turuŋ lipur,
byakta aṅgĕgwana sĕmpalĕn manĕḥta bāpa kita tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn,
māti iŋ māti kināladeśa kadi kambaŋ iŋ asana sinĕmpal iŋ kapat*

nāhan liŋnya nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul anaṅis tucapa ta panaṅis madhūdakā,
hāḥ rakryan kadi riŋ paṅipyan ahurip takari manĕ manĕḥta tiṅhali,
nāhan pun madhusūdana amwaṅi narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
kĕmbĕŋ-kĕmbĕŋ i luḥ nipun marahakĕn siḥ ipun arabi tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ*

maṅke ry-antuk ipun tumūt ri naranāthatanaya baṅun aṅhuwus-huwus,
tan lot ṅgānya pun aṅhiḍĕp turida rāga kadi wuruṅa matya monĕṅa,
ya ikā hetu nipun tĕka ahañutan aṅlalu pĕjahana de nareśwara,
aṅhiŋ luḥ ni manĕḥta kahyuna nipun rurubakĕna lawan ṅrĕs iŋ taṅis*

Ājñā śrī naranātha ṅūni ḍumawuḥ ri para panĕpi riŋ pasiṙ wukir,
an pun patyana tūt tlasĕn haḍaṅĕn iŋ hawan i hawan ipun mara iŋ musuḥ,
maṅke n tan hana patya-patyana sadoṣa nipun i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,
pun ṅgānya ika dumeḥ pun ahyuna mulat mulata juga sawet ny-unĕŋ nipun*

hāḥ rakryan siha rakryan iŋ manĕ manĕḥ ṅhulun ibu pituhun ṅhulun tuhan,
nāhan śrī naranāthaputra pakisapwan ibu ri sira haywa ta awihaŋ,
Āpan yan tuna kūŋ i māsku ri sira apa ta hamĕṅana ni ṅhulun mĕne,
tan wandhyā mati kaṙwwa pun madhu manĕḥta tuhan i huwus iŋ swayambara*

maṙmmā de jayawaspa mojaṙ ataṅis tĕka hirĕŋ i narendrakanyakā,
pantĕs-pantĕs apolahan marĕk atakwan i manaḥ ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,
siŋ solaḥnya wagĕd hanan pamisusal-misusal api cala aṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,
kĕdw-a akon marĕka akisapwana nĕhĕṙ mulat arĕṅu waśa aṅdĕlö mata*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

sāmpun dyaḥ jayawaspa mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunanda aṅucap,
rakryan tiṅhalananta māsku saŋ aja atyanta iŋ halĕp riŋ sabhā,
putra śrī raghu potraka i haji dilīpa aṅhiŋ kadaṅta aparĕk,
śuddhakṣatriya sūṙyyawaṅśa taruṇa aṅhiŋ śakti maṅke n raray*

waswāsĕnta halĕp nira aṅdaśaguṇa i rūm niŋ tulis mās tatur,
waṙṇnākāra nira amarājaya ri waṙṇnākāra niŋ campaka,
muṅgw-i i pāda nira alawan miraḥ i kĕmbaŋ niŋ tawā kedĕkan,
aṅhiŋ ketaka lot pinaṅkwakĕn ira n lwiṙnya n wĕtista alaris*

tan sāha iŋ śarapuṣpa kenaka nira apan lwiṙ smara aṅiṇḍarat,
mwaŋ maṅgĕgwana puṣpacāpa ri kiwa n paṅde raras niŋ mulat,
pantĕs muṅgwa ri citta niŋ rara sujanma n sūkṣma tan pāwaka,
yogya amaṅkwa ri māskw-apan paḍa lawan dewī ratiḥ riŋ hayu*

nāhan raśmi nikāŋ ujaṙ tĕka rĕsĕp ri twas narendrātmajā,
sāmpun waspada kuŋ nira i saŋ aja maṙmma dyaḥ sunandā sukha,
ndan moga aṅjrum apet prahelika laṅö siṅgiḥ juga n strī kawi,
denya aṅjrum rasa guywa-guywan araras ndātan tĕke jro hati*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

rakryan tan sasiwinta māsku sira de ni karakĕtan ira aṅurĕn laṅö,
riŋ tāman sira menduŋ enduṅan aśoka mĕkaṙ inarĕkan pinaṅkwakĕn,
aṅkĕn māsa kapat mahas-mahas adoḥ sahaja majamahan karas tanaḥ,
praŋ-praŋ ciṇḍaga ketakī pracacaḥ akṣara salawas ira asiḥ iŋ ṭikā*

rakryan maṅsula māsku saŋ ratu kabeḥ muwaḥ ibu parananta waswasĕn,
piŋ pat piŋ lima waspadākĕna raras nira waluyana haywa saṅśaya,
yadyastun sira nora kāptya ni manaḥta muwaḥ uwahana ŋ swayambara,
ṅkā ta dyaḥ t aduluṙ pahuṙ hurakĕnanta sira lamakananta mantuka*

nāhan denya n amet prahelika laṅö rasa kakawin anambyakĕn manis,
ndan simbantĕn adoha buddhi nira maṅkin arumaḥ apulaŋ lawan smara,
tan wruḥ ry-ambĕk ira i narendrasuta yan sira winarahakĕn mara iŋ laṅö,
tan pendaḥ lara koluran turida rāga nira ri saŋ aja awuwuḥ laṅö*

ndān ambĕk saŋ aja anahā sira ri buddhya narapatisutā n tan ahyuna,
Āpan tan huniṅa i halĕp niŋ asĕkaṙ taji wĕdi mulata iŋ ajoŋ kuniŋ,
tan hep hepĕn aniwya riŋ kadi sira api puji sinahuran patik haji,
riŋ siṅhāsana saŋ katiṅgal aṅaraŋ paḍa lĕṅĕŋ aṅikĕt pralāpita*

aṅlampū saŋ aja anahĕn turida māry-amalaṙ i harĕpā suputrikā,
Āpan tan ratu liŋ nira iry-awak ira prabhu tuwi sira tan kinahyunan,
enak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥ nira harĕp harĕpĕn amĕnaṅa iŋ swayambara,
molaḥ bāhu nira i tĕṅĕn marahakĕn ri pamĕnaṅa nira iŋ swayambara*

ṅkā n jātismara putrika atutuṙ i rūpa saŋ aja ri sĕḍĕŋ nira apsara,
riŋ swaṙgga n pakurĕn lawan sira tuhun kapalaŋ alaŋ i tan siḥ iŋ widhi,
maṅke pwa n paḍa janma mānuṣa sira atutuṙ i siliḥ asiḥ nira alawas,
wruḥ meraŋ kadi tan priya apriya ri kāla nira n atĕmu riŋ surālaya*

kāla śri indumatī kapāśa tĕkap iŋ lara turida ḍinaṇḍan iŋ smara,
rāga aṅaṇḍĕhi sāhasa amarĕpĕki twas ira rasa kapatya riŋ sabhā,
yekā hetu nira n harĕp marĕka riŋ nrĕpatanaya palaṙ sira asiha,
Āpan yogya pakāśrayan saphala paṅgajaha maḍĕmana ŋ smarānala*

ratna anopama candrasūṙyyaja kaluŋ-kaluŋ ira naranāthaputrikā,
ya ika n pawwat ira i narendrasuta rāgapahula sumĕnö mara i mukha,
embuḥ teja nikā sĕḍĕŋnya kinaluŋ kaluṅakĕn ira riŋ nrĕpātmaja,
lwiṙ dewī ratiḥ aṅhyasi smara sira n paṅamĕṙ aṅĕnakĕn kaluŋ-kaluŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

nrĕpātmaja mulat ry-awak nira sukha ambĕk ira n amĕnaŋ iŋ swayambara,
paḍa aṅrahati cakṣuṙ ādi nira moliḥ i turida narendraputrikā,
tĕka i mukha nira apriḥ oliḥ inusap hariṅĕt ira tumus tĕka i jaja,
ginañjaṙ ira riŋ sĕrĕḥ waja nira asĕmu sĕmu guyu sabhya riŋ sabhā*

para prabhu sira alara alaḥ arĕbut ri turida naranāthaputrikā,
paḍa anĕsĕl awak nira alaraŋ anaṇḍaŋ inucap ira duṙyyaśaprabhu,
gĕluŋ nira rusak mure n inalapan makuṭa nira katon paḍa akucĕm,
tiḍĕm waja nira asamun mari lumöŋ hinilan ira sĕrĕḥ mĕṅĕs-mĕṅĕs*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

hĕnĕṅakĕna narendra śrī putrī sira caritan,
muliḥ aṅalihi ḍampa awās de niŋ mulat i sira,
paḍa sukha paḍa haṙṣa anĕmwākĕn kaharĕp ira,
patĕmu nira winaswās dewī dèwa piniturun*

kaka-kaka nira mantĕn denya apet wulat amanis,
akusikan apĕga apriḥ yan lampaḥ paḍa balisaḥ,
siliḥ usap i mukha apan rūkṣa glāna hariṅĕtĕn,
wuwuḥ i hayu nika aṅhiŋ tiṅhalnya arĕṅu n ahuyaŋ*

paḍahi paḍa gumĕntĕṙ muny-asraŋ sraṅan i harĕp,
grĕbĕg i laku nikaŋ wwaŋ sāmānya aṅiriŋ adulur,
ri harĕp i wuri lumrā sakweḥ niŋ para pajurit,
saha curiga karĕsrĕs maṅrakṣa i nrĕpatanaya*

ri tĕka nira maluṅguḥ riŋ paryaṅka maṇimaya,
kaka-kaka para guṇḍik muṅgw-i i soṙ paḍa humarĕp,
kadi talaga patīṙthan sakweḥ niŋ marĕk apupul,
nrĕpasuta nrĕpaputrī tan pendaḥ kumuda mĕkar*

tucapa ta para taṇḍa n tan sthity-a akuṭa kaṭikan,
pijĕṙ aṅarahakĕn wwaŋ siŋ yogya aṅatĕṙ atĕra,
hana sira wiku wrĕddhācārī motus atawura,
amilihi śubhasaṅjñā mwaŋ saŋ wruḥ-wruḥ atawura*

sĕḍĕŋ atawuṙ ahosan ginyākĕn sira huwusa,
curiŋ amarĕṅi ghaṇṭa arūm lālitya tan asarag,
paḍahi niŋ atawuṙ śabdanya araśmi puja pujān,
mahuwusan i huwus niŋ pañcabrahma kinĕnakĕn*

tĕlas ika ginuwantĕn śuddha ŋ mūla patawuran,
śarawa kalaśa lāwan śrāntimrĕt paḍa sumaji,
ghaṭa kanaka wawan tīṙtha atiṅkaḥ marĕk atatā,
paḍa hana pinalaṅkan salwiṙ niŋ saji humaḍaŋ*

huwus asaji pari rwaŋ saṅgha aṙppat saha pipisan,
pasikĕpan ika tan saḥ soṅgwan mwaŋ hapit ajajar,
saŋ aja sira maluṅguḥ ṅkāna mwaŋ nrĕpaduhitā,
sĕmu ni manaḥ ira iraŋ yan tuṅkul baṅun aṅurit*

widhi nrĕpati paṅajyan dewī maṅdyusa ri sira,
nrĕpatanaya lawan śrī dewī śuddha manaḥ ira,
ndan i huwus ira dinyus dyus pahyas nira kumĕñar,
kadi salaga kalahrwan mĕmbaŋ wāhu kajawuhan*

nrĕpawaraduhita adan siñjaŋ wāhu sinalinan,
tapiḥ ira katutuṅkul maṅde tuṅkula saŋ aja,
dumadak amuhara aśrī siŋ dodot nrĕpatanaya,
siliḥ asiha nira aṅhiŋ don iŋ wastra siliḥ asiḥ*

atha ri huwus ira ahyas prāpta mpuṅkw-aṅarahakĕn,
sira tumuluy-adandan sakweḥ niŋ marĕk aṅiriŋ,
i lari nira cumuṇḍuk riŋ dewagrĕha madulur,
dwijawara sira masyaŋ tan sāha i hiriṅan ira*

huwus ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ tapwan wanwa siliḥ asiḥ,
siniwikaraṇa de saŋ paṇḍya brāhmaṇa matuha,
saŋ amawa kuśapāśa aṅgyākĕn mādĕga ri sira,
kadi mĕbĕda sira n tan sāha atĕmwa siliḥ asiḥ*

ri sĕḍĕŋ ira tinuntun de saŋ brāhmaṇa ri harĕp,
kumuliliṅi bhaṭāra agni mwaŋ kāsiḥ ira tumūt,
dwijawara paḍa saśrī masraŋ weda nira humuŋ,
abhinawa kadi kumbaŋ moliḥ kĕmbaŋ iŋ asana*

hyaŋ anala sukha haṙṣa n ton saŋ rwa aṅidĕri sira,
dilaḥ ira paṅadeśan tan suṇḍe malad aṅadĕg,
nrĕpawaraduhita agyaŋ moga anoliḥ i saŋ aja,
sĕmu ni wulat ira ajaṙ yan piŋ sapta sira midĕr*

muwaḥ ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ kāliḥ-kāliḥ ira marĕk,
kĕtĕṙ i taṅan ira n wahw-a apāṇigraha rumaras,
paḍa parĕŋ anibākĕn pūṙṇnāhūti saha samit,
śiwa sakala bhaṭāra agni n sākṣī niŋ awiwaha*

<waṅśastha> 
⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏓ : 12

huwus mamūjā ri bhaṭāra pāwaka,
parĕŋ sira anĕmbaḥ inastwakĕn jaya,
lawan sawīja n siniwi n jaya iŋ raṇa,
muwaḥ pratiṣṭha inabhiwāda śāśwata*

śinaṅkhapāṇyan sira de mahādwija,
muwaḥ mahāpaṇḍita śꜽwa sogata,
maśaṅkhapāṇi i sira len mahāguru,
huwus wineḥ uttamadāna de haji*

mijil suputrī kalawan nrĕpātmaja,
paḍa apatĕmwan wulat esi manmatha,
harĕp gumuywa nrĕpaputrika awiraŋ,
tumuṅku tuṅkul matukup-tukup tutuk*

marĕk wruḥ ī tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ pasaṅgrahan,
hatĕp nikaŋ ḍampa wineḥ sumiṅhita,
narendraputra aṅgĕnĕṅi i suputrikā,
parĕŋ manuṅgaŋ wĕkasan paḍa araras*

sĕkaṙ taji śrī naranāthaputrikā,
tiliŋ kagiṅgaŋ kalawan tutup gĕluŋ,
narendraputra amahajĕŋ saka i wuri,
anĕmwakĕn leśya sukha aṅharas pipi*

alakwa lakwan paripūṙṇna riŋ halĕp,
tabaŋ-tabaŋ rāmya karĕṅw-awaṅsulan,
kiduŋ kinaṅsyan murawanya tan humuŋ,
lalitya tan kaṙkkaśa saŋsaya araras*

mrĕdaṅga sāmpun sumĕneha paṅruhun,
hana atĕkap len sinameni riŋ kiduŋ,
ṇḍĕk ĕṇḍĕkan prāya ni de nikā muni,
lĕṅĕŋ karĕṅw-a asĕmu paṅgyat iŋ jawuḥ*

payuŋ putiḥ rwaṙwwa manimbaṅi i sira,
parĕŋ lumampaḥ tan adoḥ paḍa aṅadĕg,
pujut lawan jĕṅgi rara amawa ahirĕŋ,
baṅun graha rwa-rwa paḍa aṅgayaṙ wulan*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

ri huwus ira tĕka iŋ paprāsan bwat suranagara,
sahana-hana nikaŋ wwaŋ bhakty-a aṅañjali ri sira,
pasaji ri sira hampyal danta aśrī sira n apupul,
kadi surapati saṅka iŋ swaṙgga mwaŋ suramahiṣī*

tucapa halĕp ikaŋ paprāsan dug sira winaraŋ,
kadi humarasa wimba hyaŋ candrāṙkka winulatan,
tĕka riŋ alun-alun söḥ luṅsiṙ baŋ hinatĕpakĕn,
paḍa kadi gunuŋ āpuy-muntab de niŋ aṅin adrĕs*

rasa bubula tĕṅaḥ niŋ rājya apan paḍa gumĕrĕḥ,
para ratu saha gĕṇḍiŋ goŋ rojeḥ tabĕ-tabĕhan,
apituwi para taṇḍa asraṅsāṅan midĕṙ aritan,
saha paḍahi gumĕntĕṙ lagy-atry-a asurak aṅawat*

para widu sĕḍĕŋ aywan saŋ taṅkil hyaŋ acarita,
paḍa gumuyu kapūhan sakweḥ niŋ widu binisa,
hana kawatĕk ujaṙnya n guyw-a awaṙṇna macarita,
uḍuḥ uḍuḥ-uḍuḥ āḥ-āḥ hā-hā-hāḥ bisa dahatĕn*

sahana niŋ abañol denya aṅguywākĕna puraci,
aṅigĕl-igĕl agĕŋ göṅan koṇṭol paḍa mĕtĕtĕŋ,
wĕlu sakĕbĕḥ agasyak ndan moga awĕdi wĕkasan,
kaguyu-guyu kagöman yan prāpta ŋ wĕlu sabaṭaŋ*

pirus amirusi menmen denya amet pacĕḥ acĕmĕḥ,
rabi nika bisa pantĕs denya abhāwaka maṅĕyĕḥ,
laki nika mulat aṅdrĕŋ kahyun hyūn aṅuṅas-uṅas,
kadi wĕḍus anut añjyan yan tĕṅhā tĕka muriṅis*

ikaŋ amacaṅaḥ oliḥ guyw-apriḥ paḍa sinurak,
tĕkap ika nini niny-elik maswāmi wĕrĕ-wĕrĕḥ,
paḍa bisa ŋ awayaŋ wwaŋ denya aṅguywakĕn atarik,
pacĕḥ ika kaki kaky-akrak ginyat muliḥ akusa*

sahana nika pinaṅguŋ tūt padw-a abhinawa katon,
paḍa gumuruḥ awantus sakweḥ niŋ guyu gumĕtĕr,
bari-bari kapacĕḥ niŋ wwaŋ thāni n gumuyu kĕkĕl,
patĕmu ni pasurak niŋ wwaŋ kady-ampuhan apagut*

atali-tali kakulwan loṙnya arĕṅgiṅan ajajar,
rasa ḍawuha tĕkapnya n lumpat-lumpat api tibā,
milu-milu para raṇḍa anonton dan paḍa gigirĕn,
paḍa sinurak i lumpatnya n kālaḥ paḍa kawalik*

amĕnuhi nagara ŋ wwaŋ thāny-akweḥ madulu dulur,
winijilakĕn ika asiŋ saṇḍaŋ saṇḍaṅan ika mās,
wijaḥ amĕli ḍaḍaŋ saṅgiŋ calwan saha kurupuk,
anak ika sukha de niŋ tumpi mwaŋ gaja gajahan*

hana sira wiku saṅka iŋ haryāha alĕpiṙ acĕpuḥ,
kasutapan ira maṅde kweḥ niŋ śiṣya paḍa marĕk,
tuhun ulaḥ ira pĕñcul siŋ-siŋ bhāwa nira kiṭuŋ,
siŋ ucapan ira baṅsit ya ikī śabda nira rĕṅön*

ra tapa laki kapūhan wahw-a anon nagarasabhā,
abhinawa mulat iŋ bhoga atyanta amuhara sukha,
kalĕwi lĕwiḥ ikaŋ kory-alwa agöŋ gupura nikā,
nrĕpati tĕka salumbuŋ riṅgi ṅgānya tiniwikan*

nahan ucapan ira wwantĕn ta ikā titiṙ ataña,
paḍa karika ŋ ujaṙ kĕto mwaŋ kori hayu nipun,
kalawan ujaṙ anĕṅgaḥ kāri mwaŋ kari liŋ ikā,
sira sumahuṙ agampil mruḥ-mruḥ maṅhawag aṅucap*

kṣamakĕna bapa denta atakwan yogya tan ahala,
tumañakĕn ikanaŋ kori mwaŋ kori paribhaṣa,
paḍa bapa wĕnaŋ aṅgon yan tuṅgal taliṅa gajaḥ,
kalawan ujaṙ adigra mwaŋ tan padriga rahayu*

nahan ujaṙ ira baṅsit-baṅsit tan ya cala nira,
sahana-hana nikaŋ wwaŋ thāny-atwaŋ mulati sira,
tapa-tapa nira pĕñcul wwaŋ-wwaŋ sākṣara maṅucap,
milu-milu ta ya baṅsit ndan twaŋnya i sira liŋ ikā*

hĕnĕṅakĕna saŋ aṅdon tontonan sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg,
waluyana caritan śrī putrī mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya,
ndan i huwus ira pinrasprās mantuk mara ri dalĕm,
gĕrĕḥ ikaŋ arĕbut prasprāsan maṅgyat adadakan*

kunaŋ ikaŋ arĕbut penī-penī hana ri ruhur,
uliḥ ika paḍa mūlya apan wastra ahayu saphala,
binĕbĕdakĕn ika akweḥ len muṅgw-iŋ cĕṅĕl i gulū,
hilaŋ i cĕṅĕl ika i soṙ mwaŋ dodot nika karĕbut*

nda tucapa para nātha an sāmpun kewwan ira kabeḥ,
paḍa mamaluyakĕn mās lāwan wastra pamisalin,
saha manis iŋ ujaṙ ndan liśya n pawwata pahula,
muliḥ i huwus ira amwit duhkha asĕṅhit i saŋ aja*

muwaḥ ucapakĕna śrī putrī mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya,
saŋ amaraŋ i sira strī-strī wrĕddhā pitu ŋ abuyut,
tuwi kadaŋ ira tan len riŋ sajña ahayu manulus,
atuha-tuha tinuṅgal sakweḥ niŋ marĕk i sira*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

bwat kāmeśwara ratna nīla winaṅun grĕha linaraṅan iŋ huwus prabhu,
lwiṙ padma asana siṅha rūpa ni sakanya kumĕñaṙ abirū paḍa akiris,
kasraŋ de ni sĕnö nikaŋ kanaka paṅhatĕp apituwi söḥ madhubrata,
sākṣāt rātri winĕtwan iŋ wulan awā linĕṅĕṅakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur*

ṅkā dewī winaraŋ lawan saŋ aja māṙ hati nira rumaras paḍa awĕnĕs,
ry-antuk saŋ mamaraŋ-maraŋ ri sira kāri sira kadi madhubrata asana,
maṅke pwa n tumĕmu ŋ prayojana ni rāga nira malawas aṅhiḍĕp smara,
kady-a aṅipy-aṅisapwakĕn wulan awa ambĕk ira n aṅisapu nrĕpātmajā*

śrī dewi indumatī miṅe tan anumoda ri palaku ŋ asiḥ nrĕpātmaja,
heman luḥ nira maṅṅtuḥ lĕtuhi soca nira kadi saroja kābunan,
moghanya pwa mayat-mayat halis ira arĕṅu-rĕṅu kaharas wawaŋ tikĕl,
tan pātmā kinisapwakĕn twas ira tan pajajamuga rĕmĕk saka i taṅan*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ lod lĕyĕp niŋ wukiṙ inayu papaṅgiḥ nira arok piniṇḍa,
kālaṅkyaŋ mwaŋ rĕrĕb waṙṇna nira kadi liraŋ kāmukan saṅhub awrā,
himpĕṙ saŋ hyaŋ śaśī kĕmbaṙ apupul akĕmul truḥ-truḥ iŋ kāla sandhyā,
dewī dewa aṙddhanārīśwara patĕmu nira lwiṙ ṭika akaṙwwa kaṙwwan*

saŋ kady-a anaṅga māry-a atanu mijil atĕmaḥ rājaputra adwitīya,
maṙmma apet siḥ tan imba amĕkul aṅamĕṙ-amĕṙ cumbu cumbw-a aṅalap sor,
sotan ta ŋ wwaŋ riris kāṅinan apĕnĕd arūm paṅhilaŋ rāgabahni,
pömpöman rāsika lwiṙ nira paliḍaḥ iŋ elik miṅe riŋ kisapwan*

mambö sub niŋ smara aṅde huyaŋ i hati nira awaṙṣiḥ apriḥ rasanya,
sumyuk taŋ rāgawaṙṣa aṅapitu makĕcĕhan lagy-awantö raras twas,
atruḥ-truḥ haṙṣacitta amarupuhi turida awaḥ wahan sanmata agöŋ,
trĕṣṇa aṅumbaŋ lawan siḥ manis iŋ ujaṙ arūm saŋsaya adrĕs hilīnya*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

saŋ hyaŋ-hyaŋ ni laṅöku māwak aśarīra mĕtu ri paṅaweśa niŋ smara,
lwiṙ dewī sakala anurun bĕsuṙ i rāmya niŋ amĕŋ-amĕŋ iŋ surālaya,
lakṣmī niŋ nagarī turuŋ matĕmahan karika kita wiśāta lālana,
saŋ sākṣāt pratima aṅaraŋ hulun anugrahana tariman aṅharas pipi*

ṅūni i kāla nikaŋ swayambara mijil kita kadi wijil iŋ niśākara,
sakweḥ saŋ pininaŋ prabhāwa nira söḥ murub aṅabaṙ abaṙ tĕka iŋ laṅit,
rākanta anwam alĕk tathāpi kita haṙṣa tan aharĕp i wīṙyya saŋ prabhu,
göŋ niŋ priḥku lawan siḥ iŋ hyaŋ aṅiriŋ ri ḍawuḥ i turidanta ri ṅhulun*

maṅke muṅgaḥ apöm waliṅku ta kataṅgamaṅakĕna pamaṅku ni ṅhulun,
seṅĕṙku n dinĕlö ndatan tinarima aṅusapi hariṅĕt i wwit iŋ susu,
denta ahyun kadi guywa-guywan iŋ apa n rĕsĕpa pisaniṅū tĕka i hati,
siŋ solaḥku sinikwakĕnta tinĕpak hana tinama rare pinīḍana*

nāhan de nrĕpaputra haṙṣa maṅĕnākĕn ucapan amanis priyambada,
aṅluṅlūṅi laṅö hanan pakakawin kakawin aṅarĕki nrĕpātmajā,
moga atön aṅusap jaja aṅĕluk-ĕluk lĕṅĕn araras amaṭya maṭyani,
pet-pet rāga mamanwa-manwa mamĕpĕṙ-mĕpĕṙ ataña ri mūlya niŋ tapiḥ*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

śri indumatī kakĕnan wiṣa niŋ ujaṙ arūm sumusuk ri hati,
ndan kadi tan huniṅā pawulatan ira mogha maha api hade,
rwā ŋ katahā n uduhĕn brituha wilaja hetu nira api tulak,
rāga nira aṅulanĕḥ tuhun awĕdi kawĕs riŋ ulaḥ kawawa*

maṙmma nira awri lana akiput awĕdi kasiṅkaba siñjaŋ ira,
tan huniṅan tinañan lara ni wĕtu ni luḥ nira niṣkaraṇa,
nora waneḥ paran iŋ manaḥ apĕga kumöl winisik wisikan,
ṅhiŋ panamantara ri sru saŋ aja winiweka nira i twas ira*

sāma paran wĕnaṅa anulaka ri pamĕkulnya tan eraŋ amĕl,
dāna paran ta kunaŋ wĕnaŋ anuculana i paṅagĕmnya tapiḥ,
bheda paran wĕnaṅanya kumawaśakĕna bwat i rāga nira,
daṇḍa juga inaka liŋ nira nĕhĕṙ anĕpak jaja sāhasika*

kāla nira n panĕpak taṅan ira kadi pādapa molaḥ alon,
mambĕt ikaŋ luṅayan kadi lurus iŋ aśoka tinūb niŋ aṅin,
tiṅhal ira arĕṅu mogha kadi sarasija i tĕka niŋ bhramara,
suṅsut ira i nrĕpaputra hana kadi gula drawa de niŋ ĕbun*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

Ꜽ koŋ bhrānta kasop i luḥ niŋ aṅaraŋ kasarik i laṭi niŋ wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
lĕŋlĕŋ denta mulat piliḥ winawa niŋ turida sinaput iŋ hyaŋ iŋ ṭikā,
rūm niŋ śabda mameka sambĕt i gĕluŋ kari kita pati jumput-jumputi,
denta aṅol midĕṙ iŋ tĕṅaḥ kapana yan warasa kadi panumpal iŋ smara*

siṅgiḥ bhrānta kakanta māsku mapa don iŋ aṅasag inawenta lĕŋlĕŋa,
twaskw-apriḥ binĕbĕdta riŋ tali gĕluŋ cinucuk i luṅid iŋ mata aluru,
moga aṅde wulaṅun manista rinasan tuhu-tuhu n agĕlaŋ-gĕlaŋ kuniŋ,
ṅhiŋ yan rakryan aṅastwa riŋ luḥ uwatanya marasana ri rāga ni ṅhulun*

pintĕn māsku wuyuṅta tan hana waneḥ pinalaṙ asiha sanmata iŋ akuŋ,
cĕp ta induŋ taha tan taṅis kaharĕp i ṅhulun aṅisapu jöṅta sewaka,
luhta adrĕs humilī pasuṅta karikā taham ibu tan ikā prayojana,
aṅhiŋ prāṙthana mogha siddha katĕkāna siliḥ usapa luḥ lawan kita*

intaṙ haywa marĕk paran karika donta paran iku kināṙyya niŋ marĕk,
tan siḥ rāga nimitta niŋ taṅis adoḥ tiki kakĕnana kapriyambadan,
lāwan tan sukha hetu niŋ luḥ aṅasapta ri mata tuwi tan gawe-gawe,
luḥ-luḥ duhkha luḥ i ṅhulun taṅi taṅis prihati karaṇa niŋ lana anaṅis*

nāhan de nrĕpaputrika anulak i sāhasa saŋ aja saranta riŋ prĕman,
tan paṅde wĕdi riŋ kĕdö marĕk aṅol nĕhĕṙ aṅarĕki de nira aṅucap,
maṅkin haṙṣa rinĕṅwan aṅlalu kasuṅsutana saŋ aja saŋsaya awawuḥ,
śrī putrī sira kāpĕsan ri panulak nira jaja wĕkasan sira anaṅis*

<nawahaṙṣa> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓ : 19

adawa n panukĕṙ saŋ ahayu kadi tuhwa nĕhĕṙ miṅaya,
anaṅis kadi tan patĕmahana lulut pwa ri suṅsut ira,
aṅĕsaḥ kadi tan siliḥ asiha mĕne ri huwus niŋ ulaḥ,
anulak ri sĕpaḥ nrĕpasuta kadi tan pamalakwa hĕlĕm*

atukup taliṅa awĕdi katĕkana rūm niŋ ujaṙ kinire,
susu tan winĕḍaṙ wĕḍaṙ awĕdi kakukwa ragĕt-ragĕta,
akĕmul-kĕmul epu ri pĕpĕsa ni madhya nira n pinĕkul,
asaput mukha kady-awĕdi hilaṅa rūm nira kārĕkana*

nrĕpaputra mamaṭyakĕn i manis ira n gula rāga rinok,
ratus iŋ madhupaṙkka sira guliga niŋ lara haṙṣa pinöm,
rinĕbut pinakesi ni mata niŋ akuŋ ri dalĕm nagara,
papa de nira tan paṅaraṅakĕna tan panibākĕna luḥ*

lĕṅĕŋ iŋ madhumāsakusuma pinakaswaśarīra nira,
paḍaŋ iŋ wulan aṅrahinakĕn alaṅö pinakāmbĕk ira,
lumĕkas pwa sira aṅhari-hari kadi kāṙttika raśmi nira,
mĕtu kady-asirat sirata maṇik ujaṙ nira maṙmma dahat*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

māskw-induŋ mapa rāmya niŋ wulatana iŋ mata mamanisa tan pawora luḥ,
tan paṅrĕṅwa rĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsaḥ iŋ kinisapu manukĕṙ tĕka i hati,
mwaŋ tan paṅgilana n paṅol sahurana n paṅucap ubhayana aṅharas pipi,
byakta n mūra lawan śawaṅkw-ibu yadin kita mulata manuṅsuṅa iŋ guyu*

ndin wanya aku tĕka aṅisapwakĕna māsku pinaṅĕmulakĕn tĕpak jaja,
epu ṅwaŋ mapa tekiŋ enaka baśa aṅarĕkana pinamömakĕn waja,
rĕskw-induŋ tumĕkākĕna ambĕk i hayunta pinaṅagĕmakĕn nakha aluṅid,
ṅĕs ṅösĕn mulata iŋ mata amati mati i ri paṅayat i halista mamraṅa*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

nāhan wĕtu ni turida rāga rakryan aja māwak ucapan amanis,
an sāhasa sira kahanan wĕlas ri panaṅis nrĕpawaraduhitā,
 Om  yan humĕnĕṅa sakarĕŋ maṅantyakĕna rāga nira saŋ anukĕr,
saŋ hyaŋ smara ri manaḥ ira aṅalaḥ pisaniṅūn wĕnaṅa pihĕrana*

saŋ śrī niŋ ahayu sakaḍatwan osaḥ aṅĕliḥ kawarĕgan anukĕr,
wahw-a alupa taṅan ira riŋ tapiḥ tuṙ ira kaṙwwa lumay-akilusū,
mwaŋ puṇḍutan ira tumibā lukaṙ tali talinya paḍa tan iniwö,
aṅlampw-anaṅis aṅĕsĕsan paṅewala narendrasuta tinarima*

ambĕk saŋ aja sukha girahyasĕn marĕk añaṅkiraṅi tan inapa,
riŋ swapna hiḍĕp ira ri tan kawādhan i paṅol nira n inĕnĕṅakĕn,
oṅsil taṅan ira tumama irikaŋ kadi manuk wahu kumapu kapu,
mūṙcchā twas ira kawa kawa an anon kadi tanaḥ sumĕlap i taliṅa*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

utpāta nrĕpaputra riŋ śayana mogha tĕka ri papupul nira iŋ jinĕm,
liṇḍū gumrit ikaŋ palaṅka kumĕtug pakĕtĕb iŋ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
olaḥ lwiṙ bubula ŋ tilam pakĕdal iŋ wĕtis amijilakĕn larap-larap,
wintaŋ sūṙyya śaśaṅka nāga kagiwaŋ-giwaŋ i kĕlab ikaŋ laṅit-laṅit*

guntuṙ luḥ mahawan ri lambuŋ iŋ iruŋ tumĕḍun amalapaṙ mara i kapö,
kasrĕg katrag ikaŋ payodhara lana apipit alara kawantus iŋ jaja,
lambe śīṙṇna babak laṭinya hana mātra miraḥ i tapak iŋ waja anĕsĕp,
miṅgut śrĕṅga nikaŋ halis huwus apaṙwwa sana sini tikĕl mayat-mayat*

<wīralalita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

śri indumatī huwus kawawa māṙ gupe kawĕnĕsan,
mĕṅgaḥ awuṅw-anoliha paran tikāŋ inusapan,
siñjaŋ ira amiraḥ karudhiran tinuṅkulan ira,
kapyuhan aṅliga asidĕha hewa riŋ nrĕpasuta*

maṙmma narendraputra mawĕlas lana aṅhari hariḥ,
liśya nira aṅgamĕl susu maha aṅusap luḥ i jaja,
ken winirū wirū lamakan iŋ paṅol hiḍĕp ira,
cumbu wicakṣaṇa amisiki leśya niŋ maṅarĕki*

śri indumatī maṅö kadi tulis wineḥ aṅaraṅa,
waṙṇna nira akucĕm kasirĕman damaṙ mari lumöŋ,
kram-kram i pāmbĕkan saŋ aja wahw-aghāṣa tumitiḥ,
hetu nira n wijil kadi tapĕl turuŋ tinapihan*

<udgatawisama>
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 20
– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 11
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏓ : 13

dumunuŋ sira iña nira kāliḥ uwa nira kapaṅgiḥ iŋ natar,
muṅgw-i patiga niŋ aśoka liman,
akĕmit lawan kaka kaka amajaŋ wulan*

tumuluy-kataṅgamaŋ anuṅsuŋ iña nira wawaŋ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mojaṙ uwa nira marĕk manuluŋ,
ibu kölakĕn ṅhiŋ ika de nika aṅlare*

wihikan ṅhulun ri lara niŋ gati kawawa tinambay-iŋ priya,
soṙ ibu lara-lara niŋ kawĕlad,
kasahasrabhāga lara niŋ mata apĕpĕḥ*

anulis ṭikā dinudutan puḍak ibu lara niŋ minaṅkana,
lwiṙ hrĕbuk aṅalilipi ṅrĕs ikā,
aṅinaŋ sĕrĕḥ lĕgĕ paḍanya riŋ pĕḍĕs*

i kapiŋ rwa niŋ gati wĕnaŋ rinĕṅihakĕn ikaŋ lara ahaṅan,
yan huwus alawas apöm akule,
alilaŋ laranya kadi mukṣa riŋ tapiḥ*

tuhan i ṅhulun muliha rakryan alaḥ ibu waluy-para iŋ jinĕm,
tolihĕn alal ira saŋ kawĕkas,
mulat iŋ lawaŋ mapaga rūmta riŋ guyu*

araras wuwus ny-uwa nira aṅlipu lipuṙ i manaḥ nrĕpātmajā,
mogha winawa nira riŋ kalaṅön,
lara niŋ hañaṙ kawawa riŋ pasaṅgaman*

sira saŋ kinon maluya tan paṅucap arĕṅu hewa suṅkawa,
kāṅĕn aṅĕn ulaḥ-ulaḥ saŋ aja,
kamatolihĕn tuhun arĕs kapiṅrwana*

wĕkasan hinĕmbanakĕn iŋ kaka-kaka mara riŋ pasaṅgaman,
gaṙjjita saŋ aja sawet niŋ alal,
mĕtu kapriyambadan i de nira aṅucap*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

yak maty-a aku dĕlönta māsku palalun makahawana hayunta gĕgwana,
Ūṙṇnā nūpura bhūṣaṇanta katĕkāna tĕmahana ni janma ni ṅhulun,
mwaŋ rup chattra kaluŋ-kaluŋ saha sĕkaṙ taji mijila lawan tutup gĕluŋ,
aṅgon denta ri kāla niŋ piniḍuḍuk mapa rasa-rasa niŋ sinanmata*

tan hephepĕn abhūṣaṇa apan anukĕṙ nukĕri laku pataṅkis iŋ kale,
prāya aṅrup tĕka kaṙṇnaśūla niyata amuhara tuna ni de niŋ aṅrĕṅö,
kaṇṭha aṅrĕs tĕkap iŋ kaluŋ-kaluŋ ikaŋ payuŋ aṅadĕg adĕg hana iŋ adoḥ,
Ūṙṇnā wyaṙtha lawan sĕkaṙ taji tutup gĕluŋ anĕwasakĕn bwat iŋ mulat*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

nahan ujaṙ ira mambö rāga anūta ri saŋ aja,
lukaṙ i tapiḥ ira asowe keṅkab hinĕnĕṅakĕn,
wahu sumahuṙ anū de maṅke yan tinaña tañan,
mari luḥ ira kumĕmbĕŋ wahw-a aweḥ maṅarĕkana*

nrĕpatanaya kasĕṅkwan rāga amaṙppĕki sumaput,
amahawas isi niŋ ken sāmpun waspada kaharas,
aṅamĕṙ-amĕṙ amakpak wruḥ ry-ambĕk niŋ aṅĕsaha,
lwiṙ anadaki kĕna iŋ hrū maṙmma aṅrehi tan asarag*

ri huwus ira kapiṅrwan saŋ śrī niŋ tulis aṅaraŋ,
lara nira mahĕli prīty-a aluṅluŋ hyun aṅalaya,
manaḥ ira wahu tūtūt kālap de nrĕpatanaya,
turida nira kahĕnti mwaŋ siḥ niŋ hati kapulut*

paṅusĕŋ ira ri lambe-lambe tan tĕka ri hati,
panĕpak ira huwus mūṙ mukṣa aṅdohi taṅan ira,
mari marĕṅu tumiṅhal tuṅtuŋ niŋ halis alaris,
manis i guyu nira aṅdyun wruḥ giṅgaŋ wahu kasiṅī*

patĕmu nira winaswās kady-anwam yumayi yayi,
saŋ ahayu sira molaḥ maṅlaḥ-laḥ kumĕda kĕdal,
saŋ aja sira sumuṅkĕm tan paṅle kumuru kurub,
paḍa kumĕsĕk iŋ ambĕk tan kewrān awuda wudā*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

riŋ krāban kalasā mijil sira sumaṅgraha wali nira pūṙṇna tan kuraŋ,
sāmpun kewwan ira anaḍaḥ sira pĕnuḥ sama marĕk i sira wwaŋ uttama,
ramya atiṅkaḥ atūt paluṅguḥ ira saŋ huwus agati wineḥ akaṙwwana,
Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira mukhya pinituhu paḍa wruḥ iŋ krama*

ṅkāna i soṙ apupul paḍa aruhuṙ iŋ ambĕk aruhu ruhuran paḍa aṅaliḥ,
ewĕḥ tan kawĕnaŋ tiniṅkaḥ aputĕk saŋ amahayu makon atiṅkaha,
de ni kweḥnya wiwal paḍa awyahata buddhi nika puji-puji n pakawwaṅan,
siŋ soṙ uṅgwan ika anĕsĕl ri saŋ aniṅkaḥ inucap ika tan wruḥ iŋ krama*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

wet-wet niŋ brāhmaṇa atyanta wĕkas iŋ aruhuṙ kadwijāṅśan ginöŋnya,
wet niŋ śꜽwaṙṣy-aluṅgw-i i nĕhĕṙ apuji kabhasmāṅkuran mūlya denya,
wet niŋ boddha adwitīya n rumĕja rĕja kabuddhāṅkuran kāraṇanya,
tan tuṅgal māṙgga niŋ kādyan asĕmu hawan iŋ muṅgaḥ iŋ paṙwwatāgra*

wwaŋ wruḥ riŋ lokikācāra sĕḍĕŋ iŋ anaḍaḥ tan kawoṙ-woṙ manaḥnya,
denya abuddhy-a amanis mĕṅgĕp upaśama tinon mewĕḥ olaḥ tiniṅkaḥ,
aṅdoḥ tan saṅgraha iŋ uṅgwan aruhuṙ alĕmĕḥ worĕn iŋ tan kaśuddhi,
maṅgā muṅgwa iŋ asoṙ ndan yan apupul atatā sabraya arok sahāṙyyan*

guṇḍik rwaṙwwa apupul tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ adoḥ de ni göŋ iŋ pamitran,
kady-a akaṙwwan swarūpanya paḍa-paḍa siliḥ mūla tuṅgal pināliḥ,
solaḥ seṅĕṙnya moga aṅinaki ri panunasnya iŋ tuhan sāri-sāri,
denya aniṅkaḥ ry-awaknya aṅruhuri rinuhuran rāmya sawyāpasawya*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

paḍa anaḍaḥ akālihan sama kinon marĕka sukha linawwa lawwakĕn,
sawaŋ hudan atöb tiba iŋ bañu kĕcap niŋ apupul amaṅan rinĕṅwakĕn,
marĕk sahana niŋ magoṣṭhi humĕnĕŋ rumasa rasani pathya niŋ rasa,
tuhun kasĕrĕtĕn juga aṅucap aminta paluṅan atĕkĕm jaja asĕgu*

lariḥ lumari tan pararyan alaris ri katahapan ika n hana atulak,
sura asira siran rasanya surasa arĕbu rĕbu sumĕḍaḥ kinahyunan,
maṇik pinakajaṅga tan papĕgatan kucuṙ ika kadi pañcuran juruḥ,
kilaŋ brĕm inalap ginanti kadi tīṙtha madhu mamulakan saka iŋ gĕḍaḥ*

paḍa alap alapan tahap sama marĕk wija wijaḥ awĕrö girahyasĕn,
apintiga hanan papiṅpat aṅigĕl katĕkan urak aganti tan bĕsur,
ikaŋ wwaŋ atĕrĕḥ manaḥnya kĕna riŋ sayub ahaṅan agasyak iŋ sabhā,
putus maṙ atĕṅö para mpu bini mogha salaḥ ĕluk ulaḥ nira aḍake*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

strī niŋ śꜽwa tan eraŋ-eraŋ aṅigĕl kaguyu-guyu wĕrö-wĕrö dawā,
tan haṙṣa iŋ swara niŋ mrĕdaṅga salukat ṅuni-ṅuni yan i gīta niŋ waneḥ,
hetunya n paṅiduŋ wijil niŋ ajiyaḥ sahuli huliḥ ika aṅrĕṅö-rĕṅö,
sahtote prathamā kiduŋnya n aṅawat midĕm aṅujiwat ambahan tayoḥ*

ḍaŋ hadyan tumurun gumanty-aṅigĕl oṅsil aṅawak akikat rumampayak,
ṅhiŋ kahyunya kiduŋ buwun ya kiniduŋnya n aṅalik alik endaḥ iŋ sabhā,
ramya arūm sinĕlanya gĕṇḍiŋ i tutuk kaguyu guyu ginañjaṙ iŋ lariḥ,
giḥ-giḥ puŋ ri kipaḥ ḍuraŋ diniwayūḥ amamati juga de nika ambahan*

endaḥ bhāwa nikaŋ waneḥ saha kiduŋ midĕṙ aṅilagakĕn wwaŋ iŋ sabhā,
ndan strī niŋ widu rakwa mogha kawatĕk sawaŋ acarita de nika aṅigĕl,
dhik haḥ kaśmala nāhan ambahan ika aṅgyat anudiṅi mata aṅjĕjĕk lĕmaḥ,
Ꜽg lĕs liŋnya nĕhĕṙ muliḥ matĕlasan maṅumik umik aṅañjali iŋ tawaŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

samantaji tibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu muliḥ nrĕpasuta kalawan suputrikā,
parĕŋ maṅadĕg iŋ nataṙ sira kabeḥ tumut aṅiriṅakĕn mara i dalĕm,
paḍa amwit atatā wineḥ maṅinaṅa ararĕm upaśama sādara aṅucap,
dwijāṅśa maduluṙ duluṙ maṅabhiwāda para wiku marĕk maṅañjali*

gumanti para wālaka amuhun anĕmbaḥ inubhaya sināntwa riŋ guyu,
ikaŋ baṇija lot amaṅkari panambaḥ ika kawagĕdanya tan hilaŋ,
paḍa aṅucap akon ahosana mara iŋ jinĕm agawaya paṅhawin laras,
mulat saŋ aja ri priyā nira nĕhĕṙ gumuyu guyu midĕm suputrikā*

aliṅgiḥ atitiḥ pupū siliḥ usap mukha sira ri huwus nira adamu,
prahāsana narendraputra manĕcĕk nĕcĕki rahi ri kĕmbaŋ iŋ hawu,
baṅun harĕp aminta paṅkwakĕna söŋ ni paṅawaśa ni siḥ suputrikā,
paṅawruhana ken lukaṙ kadi maha aṅiṅin-iṅin i manaḥ nrĕpātmaja*

<śikhariṇī> 
⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓ : 17

sukha asaṇḍiŋ saṇḍiŋ samaṅinakana iŋ citta ginawe,
sĕlaŋ māꜽn pojaṙ saŋ aja mawaraḥ ry-antuka nira,
manaḥ dewī kagyat-gyat asĕkĕl ikaŋ twas kapĕnĕtan,
kumĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕŋ luḥ nira mijil aṅeṙttambaŋ asayut*

sĕnĕŋ yan yogya i jöṅta wawarĕṅĕhĕn luḥku k anaṅis,
wiraṅrwaŋ de niŋ tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ i śrī narapati,
manĕḥ rakryan ndi n yogya kawĕkasa tan tūta ri kita,
mataŋnya n paṅheṙ ṅke kahuluna kĕnaṅkwa i kita sadā*

paran kahyūnanta i haji pisaniṅūn tan katĕkana,
tuhun buddhyanta aṅhera pakatuhanĕn māsiha siwin,
yadin muṅgwa iŋ siṅhāsana pakaratun yan kita harĕp,
katon tan trĕṣṇā śrī nrĕpati palakun kaprabhun ira*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

yogya wuwusta tuhun ṅhulun aharĕp aṅuṅsira wīṙyya guṇa,
ndātan adoha saka iŋ ibu parĕkĕn apan sira māsiḥ anak,
göŋ i kabhaktin iŋ aprabhu maṅipulu ri twas akon muliha,
ṅhiŋ kita māsku rumaṅkĕpana kahulunankw-i narāṙyya raghu*

yan muliha prihawak ṅhulun ibu kita kāṙyya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,
tiṅhali kāsihan iŋ huwus akurĕn asiḥ mara tambaṅana,
yan waluya aku muwaḥ ri kita pira piraŋ tahunĕn ḍatĕṅa,
ṅhiŋ panaṅisku lawan kita linalu ri dūra nikaŋ palagan*

mwaŋ yan anuṅgaṅa riŋ ratha lĕpasa madoha saka iŋ nagara,
brāhmaṇa sogata śꜽwa rĕṣi sira ta maṅgala niŋ lumaku,
söḥ bala śūra kuraŋ hawan aṅiriŋ arampak aṅambaḥ alas,
śūnya hiḍĕpku yatan hana kita maṅisapwana minta sĕpaḥ*

<girisa> 
⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 16

priya kahiḍĕp ujaṙtta arūm kady-a amrĕta kasirat,
kunĕŋ amuhara kepwan ry-ambĕk ni ṅhulun alawas,
ya tan asiha kita anaṅsāra apujya tinutakĕn,
syapa ta taṅisanaṅkwa ṅhiŋ matya anaṅisi tawaŋ*

ya ta karaṇa niŋ aswī yan rakryan jĕnĕka siwin,
iwĕḥ iŋ aniwi maṅheṙ siḥ niŋ hyaŋ ya ta tinahā,
atilara kita luṅha atiṅgal wanwa n alalisa,
ṅhiŋ anaṅisana ri śrī bhoja mwaŋ nrĕpamahiṣī*

taham ibu taha rakryan maṙmma asiḥ ṅhulun atuhan,
saphala pinakadewī tan wwaŋ len kadaŋ aparĕk,
sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ sakwan selwan adulura,
kita pinakahuripku n sekaprāṇa siliḥ asiḥ*

manis i wacana rakryan sāmpun kagraha ri hati,
pinakapaṅanumānan ry-ambĕkta n tulus asiha,
sapara parana rakryan bhaktya akw-a aṅiriṅi kita,
yadin anadina lampūn matya aśa anuku riŋ awak*

ṅhulun ibu wihikan yan buddhyanta awĕlas asiha,
ika karaṇa niŋ aswī māsku n rowaṅa muliha,
nrĕpati raghu katon gyā-gyā ny-ambĕk nira mulata,
niyata papagĕn iŋ strī sāyodhyā n kita ḍatĕṅa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

sāmpun māyu wuwus nrĕpātmaja lawan dewī nira n maṅkata,
ṅkāna i wwit niŋ aśoka rambay-anaḍaḥ prāpta ŋ madaṅga aṅhaḍĕp,
luṅhā ŋ kāla huwus hyaŋ aṙkka sumurup sandhyā masĕṅsĕŋ miraḥ,
mambö kasturi niŋ paturwan araras kady-a aṅutus mañjiṅa*

ambĕk niŋ paḍa haṙṣa sāmpun amatĕḥ riŋ rāga soluṙ lulut,
trĕṣṇa iŋ saṅgama tan kawaṙṣihan apöm māywan raras riŋ prĕman,
yan līlā mijil iŋ nataṙ pinanasan de niŋ smara aṅras hati,
oṅsil tuṅtuŋ ikaŋ halis jaruman aṅgyākĕn marā riŋ tilam*

sāmpun muṅgaḥ aṅanti riŋ pasamayan saŋ hyaŋ-hyaŋ iŋ pamrĕman,
maṙmma asiḥ paḍa de nira aṅĕnahi rāga wruḥ ri tuṅgal nira,
aṙwwa rwan manaḍaḥ manis niŋ upadeśa atyanta riŋ rāsika,
nora ŋ saṅśaya riŋ rahasya winĕḍaṙ kāgĕm rasanya i hati*

saŋ raśmi inayu niŋ smara aṅucap ucap riŋ pamrĕman tan bĕsur,
sekaprāṇa sapakṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ māsiḥ sadhaṙmma adulur,
prajña iŋ buddhi siliḥ wikalpa ri rusit niŋ śabda kady-a acĕṅil,
paṅliṅganya n anak sinādhya nira masw-aswa amibhāwa iŋ tilam*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

i sāmpun iŋ ulaḥ kapintiga nikaŋ ghaṭita kawalĕsan sira aturū,
ikaŋ hulĕs adoḥ saka i sira lanā kawadal alulunan mara iŋ dagan,
hanan pawuṅu sakṣaṇa alĕḥ akaraŋ hulu taṅan aharip suputrikā,
tapiḥ nira huwus lukaṙ kasarakat kahurup i basahan nrĕpātmaja*

huwus kalalu de nira amrĕm asuwe paḍa tan umik aṅel asaṅgama,
ikaŋ manuk anaṅhi riŋ ḍawuḥ ĕnĕm sukha muni maṅuyūyu riŋ taman,
cucuṙ taḍahasiḥ swaranya kawĕlas harĕp anaṅis i paṅlwaŋ iŋ wulan,
ikaŋ mrak akakab muni iŋ gupura lagy-amuṅu ri sira riŋ ḍawuḥ pitu*

paḍa asraŋ aṅaji iŋ kulĕm sahana niŋ manuk anarawata aguṇa iriya,
parañjaṅan aṅanti riŋ gagana pathya tumiru tiru śabda niŋ pĕkiŋ,
i soṙnya hana caṅkiluŋ muni laki stry-asĕmu mamarahi ry-anak nikā,
syapa ika ta kunaŋ paṅajyan ika maṅhuwusakĕn ika yan bisa aṅaji*

awuṅw-ajajaṙ iŋ surambyan arahup nrĕpatanaya lawan suputrikā,
anĕṅgaḥ atis aṅharas harasakĕn susu saŋ ahayu maṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,
kataṅgamaŋ aṅolakĕn saŋ aja maṙmma maṅĕmuli nĕhĕṙ mamaṅkwakĕn,
pupū nira kasiṅgahan hulĕs i polaḥ ira kasuluhan niśākara*

samaṅkana ni göŋ i rāga nira kāliḥ aṅisapu lawan mamaṅkwakĕn,
tathāpi sinamantaran manis i de nira ṅucap araras prahāsana,
saŋ adyaḥ api hewa-hewa tuhun ambĕk ira tumiliŋ-iŋ karāsikan,
nrĕpātmaja mañumbu ñumbu mamibik tapiḥ aharĕp i buṅkaḥ iŋ tĕṅaḥ*

ri luṅsuṙ i tapiḥ nira arukĕt ikaŋ luṅayan asĕmu luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
ikaŋ gĕlaŋ ataṅkis iŋ wĕtis apiṇḍa madhukara mara ahyun iŋ puḍak,
payodhara lana apipit kadi wĕdinya kaharasa ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ kuku,
ikaŋ mukha sawaŋ wulan marĕk i wimba nira sĕḍĕŋ ira n sapamrĕman*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

maṅkin wrĕddhi wijil ni rāsika nira n paṙwwaṙwwan iŋ pamrĕman,
nidra acumbana ta pwa nitya ginawe maṅde sukha i twas nira,
söṙ mambö waṅi niŋ sĕkaṙ kadi mahā mañjiŋ mamuṅw-i i sira,
tan wruḥ yan rahina apaḍaŋ paḍa mijil de niŋ hrĕbuk niŋ puḍak*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

samantaji mijil hyaŋ aṙkka kadi raktakumuda sumĕkaṙ saka iŋ bañu,
wulan mari lumöŋ kagöṅan ahulap sumirĕp awĕdi tan wĕnaŋ mulat,
tĕka iŋ grahagaṇa anusup nusup arĕs karahinana humöt paḍa akucĕm,
ikaŋ wĕṅi huwus paḍĕm kadi hilaŋ pinĕjahan ira riŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu*

ikaŋ bhuwana kālapan wĕṅi baṅun jaladhi karaŋ asat ḍasaṙ nika,
katon awas ikaŋ gunuŋ kadi timiṅgila makatihalaŋ paḍa aṅjĕlag,
urut saka satal kumĕṇḍĕŋ ajajaṙ paḍa-paḍa kadi nāga maṅlayaŋ,
muni ŋ jalada maṅrĕguŋ sagajamīna kasatan aṅuliŋ harĕp bañu*

<puṣpacāpa> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓ : 20

ri wwit niŋ kayu pārijāta hana tīṙtha alantaran wwad kucuṙnya,
tūsanya analaga ajajaṙ watu karaŋnya agroŋ rinoŋ pañcuranya,
tampyak-tampyakan iŋ wĕrĕḥ pamarigi lwiṙnya n patap de nikaŋ ṙyyak,
wwꜽnya abhrā kadi saṙwwawaṙṇna ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ puṣpamāyā hana i jro*

ṅkā dewī marahup-rahup sira yathālīla aṅuḍoḍa añawuk wwꜽ,
tan saḥ śrī naranāthaputra maṅĕmit lwiṙ kumbaŋ aṅrakṣa kĕmbaŋ,
wruḥ riŋ cāmana pītrĕtaṙppaṇa satiṅkaḥ-tiṅkaḥ iŋ tīṙthayātra,
mādĕg pūṙwwamukha ajajaṙ parĕŋ amūja aṅañjali i saŋ hyaŋ aṙkka*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

mantuk śīghra mara i dalĕm humatuṙ i śrī bhoja riŋ pamrĕman,
akweḥ strī haji sambhrama i tĕka nira aganty-a aṅucap gaṙjjita,
maṙmma śrī parameśwarī mulat anuṅsuŋ cumbu cumbw-a aṅucap,
Ī-Ī śrī maṇik i ṅhulun sira ḍatĕŋ kāliḥ nihan liŋ nira*

śrī dewi indumatī parĕŋ sira manĕmbaḥ mwaŋ narāṙyyātmaja,
riŋ lampit hana siṅhacaṙmma humaḍaŋ kāna n pratiṣṭha ararĕm,
saŋ nātha wruḥ i don ira n para wawaŋ śoka drawa twas nira,
amwit sādara sopacāra saŋ aja anĕmbaḥ ri jöŋ saŋ prabhu*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ> 
– – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓ : 22

sĕmbaḥ niŋ aśaraṇa ri jöŋ narendra huniṅan parĕk i narapati,
amwīta muliha satata aṅriwĕg riwĕgi tan bĕsuṙ amaribini,
tan sĕṅgahĕn akalis i pāda saŋ prabhu pasaŋ kuhira pinahayu,
paṅgil wĕnaṅa dadaha riŋ raṇa aṅharĕpa śatrukula yan iŋ ayun*

 Om  wruḥ ṅhulun ika mara hetu niŋ kahĕnĕṅan kapĕgan aṅucapa,
māsiḥ ṅhulun iri kita mogha tan wĕnaŋ asiḥ karaṇa niŋ asĕkĕl,
maṅke n mulat iri kita tan palekan aṅĕḍap muliḥ analahasa,
wahw-a apupul alal alawas tĕka pwa kita sakṣaṇa wawaŋ apasaḥ*

pintaṅkw-i kita bapa sihanta tan kapalaṅa amipila riŋ agati,
saṅkan raray-uwuḥ-uwuḥ ūpamānĕn iŋ ulaḥ kasiḥ arĕp alawas,
maṅke n marĕk iri kita sanmatan kawiguṇanya tan ucap-ucapĕn,
aṅhiŋ pakadaṅan i bapaṅku tolihĕn i māsku laki pakatalin*

nwam ny-ambĕk ika mĕṅĕ mĕṅö kalotakĕna denta kajugulan ikā,
tan wruḥnya riŋ aṅinakana i mulat pipili denta pituturi piṅit,
saŋkṣepa nika kita waśa pramāṇa guṇadoṣa nika wawarĕṅöḥ,
yadyastun iwĕŋ iwĕṅa riŋ hulun bapa manaḥnya palu-palu waraḥ*

atwaŋ saŋ aja sumahuṙ apraṇamya rumuhun saha manis iŋ ujar,
Ājñā nrĕpati rasa nira awĕkas wĕkas akon siliḥ asiha sadā,
sāmpun karĕgĕp i hati de patik haji minuṣṭi maṅinaki hati,
ṅhiŋ gānya n apasaha ri tan siḥ iŋ widhi harĕp mulata riŋ alara*

atyanta hĕla-hĕla niŋ aṅrĕṅö wacana rakryan aṅinaki hati,
niṙwighna kita bapa tĕka iŋ sinādhya wĕnaŋ uṅsirĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,
śānti dwijawara ri bapaṅku kesyana tumiṙwwa narapati raghu,
swasty-astu saha tanaya dāra māsku saŋ anĕmwa jayaphala sadā*

mwaŋ yan pawuwuha kita ghāra pat lima sujanma wĕka-wĕka ratu,
tan doṣa tumĕkakĕna sāmbĕk iŋ wĕnaŋ amukti wiṣaya saphala,
ndan haywa sira ta bapa kāri denta pakamaṅgala niŋ anakĕbi,
yogya n kalĕwihakĕna tan paḍan phala nika aṅurati kahulunan*

tĕmbe ŋ śubhadiwasa bapaṅku maṅkata kakanta maṅatĕrakĕna,
jyotīṣa paḍa tinañan i ṅhulun wiṅi ri kāla nira paḍa marĕk,
awyāhata pawaraḥ ira apadohan atukaṙ paḍa kamasĕṅĕrĕn,
saŋ lekan aṅucap apagĕḥ tuwin binisa kāraṇa niŋ amituhu*

ya ikī muwaḥ ucapakĕna i  bapaṅku sahaja alupa kamituturĕn,
dūmĕn sahana hana ni drĕwya-drĕwya haji dewata tĕka tĕkanĕn,
lāwan sahana hana nikaŋ rare kawula rakryan aṅalapa muwaḥ,
yadyan jĕnĕka kita bapaṅku pālihĕn ikaŋ nagara kaliliran*

nāhan paṅucap ucap ira lwiṙ amrĕta hañaṙ mĕtu siniratakĕn,
maṅdadyakĕn i sukha narendraputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā,
kesyan rasa ni manis i de nira aṅucap arūm asĕmu gula siṅī,
bheda mwaŋ ujaṙ amanis iŋ pralāpita namun rĕcĕpa rasa nikā*

kañcit paḍa tĕka maduluṙ sira iŋ pagaḍuhan marĕk i narapati,
sakweḥ ni kĕmitan ika mās maṇik pirak ikā ya tinañakĕn ira,
ya ika n pamaca padadaran tĕlas pwa ya samaṅkana winijalakĕn,
kasraḥ satĕṅaḥ i naranāthaputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā*

nantĕn samĕgĕt aniga mukhya sāra ginulaŋ halu makĕmitana,
mwaŋ drĕwya pahula naranātha sojaṙ i narendra paḍa sinuṅakĕn,
lāwan muwaḥ anĕkakĕna iry-ayodhyanagarī tumuta ri saŋ aja,
Āpan wĕnaŋ akun iŋ ulaḥ prayatna wĕka sādhu wĕka niŋ aniga*

dum dūman ira pira kunaŋ wilaŋnya kadi tan kawĕnaṅa wilaṅĕn,
yadyan banawa saha bahitra dūra wĕnaṅa amwata niyata sarat,
muṅgw-iŋ ratha pira-pira taŋ ratha iŋ nagara hĕnti paḍa hinibĕkan,
wastrādi pinada pinadāti pādadara tan wuruŋ apan adadar*

ndātan caritan ulaḥ ira anaḍaḥ ri huwus iŋ wwalu wahu ḍumawuḥ,
tan saḥ uwa nira kalawan sira iña nira mukhya niŋ aṅiriṅakĕn,
sāmpun praṇata sira paḍa aṅadĕg muliḥ i pamrĕman ira ri dalĕm,
sakweḥ ni hulun ira kinon madandana paḍa agarawalan ataña*

dewī sira maṅutus aniṅka niṅkaḥ i sadrĕwya nira pinahayu,
nora ahala-hala kalasā tinon kinajaṅan winalunan ahalĕp,
akweḥ papiku pikul ira apupul kawula dāsa kaliliran ira,
boṇḍan sajuru lawan ikaŋ pujut sajuru jĕṅgi sajuru humaḍaŋ*

wyāpāra sahana hana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ nagara tan hana maṅinak inak,
kady-a asawuṅan asipĕt olaḥ-olaḥ adamaṙ damaṙ amalaku duḥ,
ceṭī rumara rara paḍa aṅasū wija-wijaḥ dudu taŋ amususi,
siṅgoḥ ya humuŋ asahuran baṅun śakaṭa gumrit amuhara laṅö*

guṇḍik kaka-kaka mawiweka pahyas ikaŋ endaha tan awanĕha,
lagy-a aminĕkĕti hayu tuṅgal ĕmbulana tan hana niŋ amihaṅa,
ṅhiŋ raṇḍi dadaṙ ika kabeḥ kahaywakĕna don ika pinagĕhakĕn,
denya amahayu sipat ināptyakĕn pinakadaṙśśana tiniru tiru*

sāmpun ghaṭita pitu tibā putiḥ timuṙ ika awawa rahina mijil,
Ābhā ni pawuṅu naranāthaputra karĕṅö piliḥ anuculi ken,
dewī kadi kahĕnĕkan asriŋ ambĕkan ira asahuran aṅĕsĕsan,
Ākāra ni hĕnĕŋ ira meḥ tigaŋ paṅinaṅa awuṅu mijil adamu*

dewī sira pinahayu hinyasan pinahawās kadi maluya rarā,
dūran wĕnaṅa paṅanumānana i huwus ira apriya luṅayan ira,
lāwan mata waja nira tan wĕnaŋ pinakaliṅga ni pasawi nira,
ṅhiŋ mājaṙ i huwus ira medĕman susu nira i kiwa kani kakuku*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

sāmpun sira ahyas asalin hima puṣpawaṙṣa,
dodot narendrasuta rakwa kilat rinĕṅga,
Āsĕṅka niŋ mulat i rūpa narendraputrī,
putrī saka iŋ surapada anĕmu rājaputra*

prāsāda ratnamaya muṅgw-i dalĕm kaḍatwan,
ḍaŋ hyaŋ purohita sira iniriŋ iŋ pamūjā,
ghaṇṭa alaṅö dhwani nikā saha pūja pūjān,
śaṅkha lwiṙ asyaŋ aṅuhuḥ ri narendraputra*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ nrĕpatiputra lawan suputrī,
gandha akṣatādi humaḍaŋ kalawan niwedya,
mañjiŋ sira i dalĕm aṅaṙppaṇakĕn pamūjā,
amwīt i wimba haji dewata bhakty-anĕmbaḥ*

dewī sira amĕkul i jöŋ nira saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,
aṙṇnaḥ manaḥ nira sada aṅaku rāma rena,
glāna anaṅis kasiḥ arĕp twas ira wyamoha,
sambat nira amuhara luḥ pamĕlas harĕpnya*

Ꜽ rāma rena kita saŋ lumaḥ iŋ kaḍatwan,
ṅūni n maṇusya kita kaṙwwa bapa ibu liṅku,
maṅke dadi hyaŋ inalĕmbana sāṙddhadeha,
hā-hāḥ yayā bapa haji ibu haji iki liṅku*

ndā t aṅrĕṅö bapa haji ibu haji i taṅisku,
pamwitku tiṅhali sumambaḥ i pādukanta,
Āḍā wĕkasku mulati i kita ta iki maṅke,
rakṣan ṅhulun bapa haji ibu haji i paranku*

nāhan taṅis-taṅis ira alara wāhu mantĕn,
milw-a anaṅis nrĕpatiputra nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul,
lāwan hyaŋ aṙcca pakatonan ira ipu winwit,
de niŋ śiwāmbha ri mukha asĕmu luḥ drawa adrĕs*

sāmpun mijil nrĕpatiputra lawan suputrī,
prāpta i narendra mahiṣī tumuluy-sira aṅliŋ,
kĕmbĕŋ ni luḥ nira panuṅsuŋ ira i suputrī,
de niŋ sĕkĕl sapaṅucap nira tan sphuṭa asrĕt*

māskw-i ibu haywa kita tan praṇatā subhakti,
i swāmi rakryan apan uttamarājaputra,
Āsiŋ sakahyun ira tūtakĕnanta māsku,
ya ikā patibrata ṅaranya pakabratanta*

mwaŋ haywa māsku paṅayāya karājaputryan,
lāwan hayunta wiphala n pakapaṅhaḍanta,
tan kweḥ ni māsta makapaṅgajahanta māsku,
kakṣatriyanta maniwi ibu pakātmarakṣa*

lāwan muwaḥ saŋ aja haywa bapaṅkw-atiṅgal,
i śrī narendraduhitā paḍa wastu māsku,
riŋ rūpa sampĕlaḥ awaṙṇna sĕkaṙ pināliḥ,
prāṇanta tuṅgalakĕnanta maran tan imbā*

tan ketaka ŋ puḍak adoha ri ṣaṭpadanya,
tan ṣaṭpada ŋ bhramara sāha saka i puḍaknya,
tan putrikā sarika yan taya rājaputra,
tan rājaputra kita yan taya rājaputrī*

nā liŋ narendramahiṣī n panaṅis sumuṅkĕm,
i śrī narendraduhitā pinĕkul siniṅsĕt,
akweḥ mulat kapitaṅis ri narendraputrī,
Āpan wĕkas nira katon ri widaṙbbharājya*

embuḥ taṅis ri pataṅis taṅisan suputrī,
de niŋ swawandhu nira söḥ atuluŋ bwat iŋ luḥ,
prāpta amalandani pirak maṇi wastu mūlya,
len taŋ sĕrĕḥ kinajaṅan saha modakādi*

<dodhakawrĕtta> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏓ : 11

śrī nrĕpaputra lawan nrĕpaputrī,
amwit anĕmbaḥ i jöŋ mahadewī,
mary-ataṅis taṅisan paḍa līlā,
śeṣa ni luḥ nira mātra kumĕmbĕŋ*

maṙmma dahat paṅucap mahadewī,
 Om  bapa saŋ makapunpunana ŋ rāt,
sora samāpta para prabhu denta,
śrī raghu māsku tirunta jaya iŋ praŋ*

śri indumati ibu huripku kita antĕn,
mogha katĕmwa sukhanta dadi strī,
rowaṅa rakryan aja asisihan siḥ,
tuṅgalĕn apriya riŋ nrĕpaputra*

sāmpun ira n paṅucap mahadewī,
śri indumatī kalawan nrĕpaputra,
mādĕg inumbalan iŋ paricārī,
maṅkat awaṙṇna śaśāṅka kameghan*

kīṙṇna tikaŋ pamikul  pikul akweḥ,
denya lumampaḥ arampak apaṇṭa,
nora jaruḥ wihikan ri duluṙnya,
yogya katiṅhalana apan atiṅkaḥ*

maṅkana taŋ ratha nora kagiṇḍal,
meww-iwu lampaḥ ika adĕdĕṙ adrĕs,
drĕwya narendrasutā winawanya,
mās maṇi len rajatādi suwastra*

salwiṙ ikaŋ paḍahi iŋ nagara asraŋ,
rāmya tĕkapnya hanan sinameni,
len masarag makapaṅhaḍa göŋnya,
lwiṙ kĕtug iŋ lĕwu denya gumĕntĕr*

śri indumatī siwuhĕn sira luṅhā,
de ni lulut nira riŋ nrĕpadewī,
lūḥ ira tan pĕgat adrĕs awantu,
śrī nrĕpaputra kaṅelan ameri*

muṅgw-irikaŋ kapiṅan sira kāliḥ,
rāmya katonan ira apan awelā,
lwiṙ kawĕlad twas ikaŋ wwaŋ aniñjo,
bhakti mamakpak aṅañjali māsiḥ*

maṙmma nira n mari sukṣĕka rañca,
rūm saŋ aja aṅhari hary-aṅalap sor,
mwaŋ jayawaspa wicakṣaṇa tan saḥ,
māry-aputĕk sira rakwa tumon ya*

strī ri dalĕm nagara arĕja pantĕs,
mātus atus paḍa maṙmma rarasnya,
kocap anampikakĕn sĕkaṙ aṅjraḥ,
milw-aṅiriŋ ri nareśwaraputrī*

kādbhuta lampaḥ iraŋ nrĕpaputrī,
de ni halĕp para guṇḍik atiṅkaḥ,
wastra nikā paḍa raṇḍi sapaṇṭa,
lwiṙ kusuma anĕḍĕŋ iŋ pratimāsa*

śrī naranātha tumūt saha mantrī,
söḥ aṅiriŋ paḍa śūra wani iŋ praŋ,
meww-iwu lakṣa sahasra kumĕṇḍĕŋ,
lwiṙ paṅawak nikaŋ antaka sākṣāt*

śrī naranāthasutā sira śoka,
sis kamatolihĕn iŋ nrĕpadewī,
wāhu lipuṙ tumuluy-sira monaŋ,
luḥ nira lāgi kumĕmbĕŋ asowe*

sāmpun ira n lĕpas iŋ kuṭa wetan,
toliḥ ikaŋ nagara asĕpi tistis,
kaywan ikā manira aṅaway-asriŋ,
kady-aṅutus maluya i sira kāliḥ*

rāmya nikaŋ kahawan sawaḥ alwā,
maṅdadi bhasma daminya tinunwan,
ṣaṭpada muṅgw-i sĕkaṙ ni wuruŋnya,
lwiṙ kawi māsiḥ aghāra daridra*

ndan sadawā ni hĕnu nira rāmya,
sontĕn ikaŋ jawuḥ adrĕs asowe,
śīghra pucuk ni tĕkinya tumūwuḥ,
waṙṇna nikā kadi campaka siṅsal*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

kīṙṇna katon wijil iŋ laru-laru kumukus kadi tan lĕwasa,
haṙṣa sira iña nira mwaŋ uwa nira riwönya katon aṅĕliḥ,
mwaŋ para guṇḍik amupw-awurahan arĕbut paḍa buddhi rare,
śri indumatī marĕk iŋ nrĕpasuta sukha haṙṣa sira amawani*

hyaŋ rawi tumraŋ ikaŋ walaŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ makamūla ŋ atis,
cumbw-i rabinya marĕk nĕhĕṙ aṅĕpĕṙ uninya karĕṅw-araras,
strīnya kumöl inaras haras anarima solaḥ ulaḥ niŋ akuŋ,
saŋ rwa mulat marĕn ahyun aṅalapa tumon i wilāsa nikā*

mogha jĕnĕk sira de ni paṅaraman ikaŋ bañu wāhu ḍatĕŋ,
katkat aliwran amet walaŋ asira siran kalawan dadali,
aṅṅṅĕṅi twas ira ika ta karaṇa nira asrĕt alon lumaku,
lālana lagy-anĕpĕṙ nĕpĕri sĕkaṙ arūm kadi mitra kadaŋ*

lampaḥ ira atut ayun tinutakĕn iŋ aṅin saha megha rĕmĕŋ,
lwiṙ makadoṣa laṅö nira sahasa manĕmpal aśoka liman,
hinrĕt i kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕḍĕŋ analyani buddhi nira,
riŋ wĕkasan dinudut ni karas ira nimitta nira n lumaku*

lwaḥ laraṅan kahalintaṅan asat apirak pirakan gumĕlar,
waḥ kayu mās ri tĕpinya salak apupul awwaḥ atöb anĕḍĕŋ,
nista nika n sugiḥ iŋ kalĕṅĕṅan atĕṅö tuwi tan papaḍa,
wwatnya katiṅgal adoḥ anĕmu maru hĕnū pamĕnĕṙ mĕnĕran*

piṅgiṙ ikaŋ pagagan harata hara-hara n pamuraŋ muraṅan,
luñcip ikaŋ rwi kulampis i pagĕṙ ika waṙṇna tanaḥ kinikir,
wwaḥ ni saganya baṅun mata hañaṙ asipat pinuyuṙ puyuran,
daṅdaṅan aṅgarit iŋ wĕtis aniru kuriñjĕm umuṅgw-i pipi*

sīma kawaṅśan alas juraŋ anasarakĕn sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,
saṅkawilanya mañaṇḍĕt i rusit i hĕnūnya lawan wadara,
mĕṅgĕp arūm araras gaḍuŋ ika katĕkan tuha milw-amilĕt,
buddhi nikā wilut aṅduhuṅakĕn apituwy-aḍaḍap wwaŋ agöŋ*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

taṅeḥ yan ucapĕn kalaṅwan i hĕnū nira kadi nawanāṭya niŋ kawi,
wimūṙccha para guṇḍik aṅrĕṅi rĕṅiḥ para kaka-kaka śoka kaṅlihan,
katuhwan iŋ apa n tan apriha sukunya wahu lumaku lakw-adoḥ dahat,
sira iña nira len uwā nira paḍa akĕsĕl awak ira muṅgu riŋ ratha*

i tan wĕnaŋ ikā lumampaḥ awĕḍak suku binĕbĕd ika iŋ kajaṙ kajar,
baṅun surawadhū paḍa adarupa kady-anapaka gagana n tiniṅhalan,
tuhun sukha manaḥnya riŋ wĕkasan eṅgal asĕmu guyu māri suṅkawa,
ikaŋ magiliṅan kajātaka paḍa amawa giliṅan inājña mamwata*

tigaŋ wĕṅi sira aṅinĕp nrĕpati mamwit i saŋ aja lawan nrĕpātmajā,
i pāntaran ikaŋ wukiṙ hiṅan ira aṅatĕrakĕn i nareśwarātmajā,
maluy-sira lawan gaja aśwa ratha tan hana hiḍĕp ira wanya wādhakā,
narendratanaya anaṅis nrĕpatiputra salahasa tumon kamānuṣan*

muwaḥ nrĕpatiputra maṅkat aṅusī pakulĕmana nira wwaŋ iŋ pasir,
karaŋ karaṅan endaḥ-endaḥ alaṅö hinaturakĕn ikā lawan sayub,
paḍa anrik aṅinum twak iŋ pasisi saŋ watĕk aja karuhun nrĕpātmaja,
bhaṭāra baruṇa aṅaliḥ nagara rūpa nira wahu mijil saka iŋ tasik*

riŋ eñjiŋ i wijil hyaŋ aṙkka sira maṅkat aduluṙ ahawan gunuŋ-gunuŋ,
huwus tĕka sira irikaŋ pĕkĕn agöŋ sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg ikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ pĕkĕn,
ikaŋ baṇija saṅśaya anaha nahā ri patukara nareśwarātmaja,
lawan sahana saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ rumĕbuta ri narendraputrikā*

mpu rāma humatuṙ mara i saŋ aja sādara tĕkap ika mojaṙ aprĕgi,
tuhanku bapa sugya tan wruha bapaṅku ri hana nira saŋ watĕk ratu,
ry-uliḥ nira saka iŋ swayĕmbara paḍa apupul amarĕki deśa duṙggama,
kunaŋ bapa panaṙkka-naṙkka ni manĕḥta kadi rumĕbuta i suputrikā*

putus mara lĕbā nikaŋ tĕgal ayun palapat alas-alas gunuŋ-gunuŋ,
tathāpi paḍa söḥ kinuwwan arupĕk wĕkasan asalĕsĕk tĕka iŋ juraŋ,
dudū sawĕṅi saŋsaya awuwuḥ ikaŋ gaja ratha saha sañjata asinaŋ,
mataŋnya bapa yatna-yatna tuhan i ṅhulun apupula haywa wismrĕti*

nahan wuwus ikā nrĕpātmaja wawaŋ sumahuṙ asĕmu siṅha kātara,
mpu rāma tak anāgata akw-iriya yadyan awuwuha muwaḥ samaṅkana,
muwaḥ yadin ameta dꜽtya saha dānawa pakaśaraṇanya riŋ raṇa,
hade raghusuta aku tak sy-aja ṅaranya yak atakuta riŋ samaṅkana*

samantaji ḍatĕŋ hulun nrĕpatiputra sahana nikaŋ aṅruhun-ruhun,
kanin rujit awaknya maṅhaturakĕn śiraḥ apan arujit nĕhĕṙ murud,
ya ta ajaṙ i narendraputra saha cihna rĕsĕp i hati de nika aṅucap,
alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikanaŋ wani-wani karuhun nrĕpātmaja*

i sāmpun ira muṅgaḥ iŋ ratha tumūt nrĕpawaraduhitā hana i wuri,
pasaṅgha ni surak watĕk raghusuta amaji taliṅa nikaŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,
linūd i kĕtug iŋ gubaṙ saha garantuŋ uni nika karĕṅw-aṅalw-alö,
ikaŋ wwaŋ apĕkĕn-pĕkĕn gumuruḥ awrĕg inawaran i dūta niŋ musuḥ*

<meghawitānā> 
⏑⏑– |⏑⏑– |⏑⏑– | ⏓ : 10

tucapa ŋ kahawan paḍa yatna,
wihikan ri manaḥ para nātha,
sahasa aṅrĕbuta i nrĕpaputrī,
saŋ aja prihĕn iŋ raṇamadhya*

juru sāmya ḍatĕŋ paṅatagnya,
i samāṅjuru len para duhwan,
paḍa sambhrama maṙmma paḍa agya,
anabĕḥ kukulan makapĕṇṭok*

pamaja anwam anaṇḍaŋ agasyak,
wahu wahw-akurĕn paḍa māsiḥ,
kamĕnanya lumakwa masaṇḍiŋ,
hana buddhi nika amwit akāṙyya*

juru tuṅgul añumbw-i rabinya,
ibu puñcawali n pĕjaha ṅwaŋ,
pĕraṅĕn ri jajaṅku kita antĕn,
mila liŋ ni rabinya tan aṅgā*

widu milw-aharĕp tumuta apraŋ,
wĕdi wĕdy-aṅabuk prawalanya,
i hilaŋ ni galaḥnya salaḥ ṅgwan,
tinañākĕn ika i pagaḍaynya*

saŋ ibu nya paran di galaḥku,
hana riŋ paḍaṅan ya hikā ya,
aŋ usĕn laku t āsaḥ iri ŋ lwaḥ,
mata maḥ laku he pira dohe*

ndi wahosku paran di wahosku,
mbruta pet ndi pametana siŋ sī,
syapa ta wruha takwanakĕn sī,
aḥ aḥ-aḥ sy-apĕṅiŋ kadi wāni*

alupa aku paran pwa katiṅgal,
ri sĕḍĕṅta siliḥ galaḥ oliḥ,
kawĕkas ni wĕtis ni lawanta,
si ḍuli ika paṅenak uwanya*

atutuṙ wĕkasan sy-aku maṅke,
pañukilku hapū maḥ asaḥ ñen,
mapa yan guruwindakĕnanta,
paṅupaḥ tĕlu mās aḍug induŋ*

ndi juluk julukuṅku dalampat,
hana riŋ lwaḥ anakta si maṅdyus,
a dĕlit ny-anak iŋ wani riŋ praŋ,
baribin pa ya tan tuhu hāḥ ñwak*

ndwa sĕrĕḥ ndi ta polihanaṅkwa,
ndi pupuk ni hucu n kinaṅĕṅkwa,
maḥ alap haḍug ību taluḥnya,
ndwa kamal ḍiḍikan hibu rakryan*

laku t aṅkat amaḥ bĕkĕlanta,
ndwa ta sī mapa liṅta malīya,
ndwa ta sī mapa hāḥ hapi tan wruḥ,
ndwa ta sī si putiḥ pisane wus*

ya tikā paṅucap si jarĕmpu,
aṅadĕg ya maṅundurakĕn wwaŋ,
gumadā wĕsi ta iki galaḥnya,
pinikulnya nĕhĕṙ mĕtu Ꜽg lĕs*

para sāmya paḍa aprĕgi maṅkat,
muni goŋnya lawan paḍahinya,
saha sañjata söḥ ri tĕgalnya,
papupulnya salakṣa sinākĕn*

tĕka śīghra ri jöŋ nrĕpaputra,
sira muṅgw-irikaŋ ratha ratna,
i katon ira denya madandan,
humatuṙ saha tuṅgul anĕmbaḥ*

sĕmu haṙṣa sira i para sāmya,
kadi wanwa tĕkap nira n aṅliŋ,
ubhaya i panunasnya macatwa,
paḍa maṅdaśamāsa catunya*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

śīghra adandan kinon de saŋ aja marĕka lumrā katon sañjatanya,
Āpan prāpta ŋ musuḥ sāhasa waragaŋ ikā krūra tan paṅgalaŋ twas,
sakweḥ niŋ śūra-śūra ŋ watĕk aja kumutug söŋ ikaŋ krodhabahni,
gut gūtĕn tan panaṅgĕl trĕṇa hiḍĕp ira riŋ sañjata akrĕp lumaṅkuŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ strī makādi nrĕpawaraduhitā muṅgu riŋ deśa duṙgga,
mwaŋ salwiṙ niŋ ratha amwat pahula haji lawan drĕwya rakryan suputrī,
līla anon tan tinon śrī nrĕpawaraduhitā de nikaŋ kaywa kaywan,
tĕkwan salwā nikaŋ papraṅana kalihatan koṅkulan tan pawighna*

mojaṙ saŋ mambaŋ iŋ śrī raghusuta bapa haywa ata tan yatna-yatna,
haywa iccha apan musuhta aṅdaśaguṇa ri wilaṅta iŋ mahāpadmasankhya,
loṙ kulwan wetan akweḥ tumut i paṅuliliŋ niŋ gunuŋ söḥ lumaṅkuŋ,
wadwānta aṅhiŋ wijilnya n paṅayat ayat i göŋ niŋ prabhāwanta riŋ praŋ*

ndā nāhan śrī mahārāja magadhapati kady-a anĕṅaḥ riŋ samudra,
Āpan sāmantarāja akĕmit i sira lawan rājaputra prawīra,
ratna ayw-aywan lawan mās ratha nira kumĕñaṙ katraṅan de hyaŋ aṙkka,
śwetākāra ahalĕp chattra nira kadi halĕp niŋ wulan tan kameghan*

paṙṇnaḥ kulwan saŋ aṅgādhipati kadi kilat niŋ truḥ iŋ kāla sandhyā,
de niŋ saṙwwāstra muṅgw-i i hiriṅan ira pĕtĕŋ lwiṙ hudan tan pamegha,
lāwan mātaṅga meww-i iwu kadi gunuŋ apuy-de ni rĕṅganya kumram,
aṅlīla anuṅgaŋ iŋ ratnaratha sira hana i wwit nikaŋ pārijāta*

nāhan taŋ bāṇa sālas kadi sinaliwaḥ iŋ campaka aṅjraḥ sĕkaṙnya,
akweḥ wīra aṅrĕrĕb ṅkāna saha gaja turaṅga awaki iww-i iwu lakṣa,
honya i wwit niŋ susantĕn ratha kanaka rinĕṅgan maṇī hīrabajra,
uṅgwan śry-a awantinātha adbhuta bapa kadi digdāha niŋ kāla sandhyā*

ndaḥ nāhan śrī pratīpa aṅadĕg amawa laras riŋ ratha aṅdandani hrū,
akweḥ wadwā nira atumpuk awuwuḥ i harĕp maṅrĕgĕp sañjatanya,
lwiṙ priŋ sālas galaḥ niŋ prajurit ira wahosnya anamaṙ megha mĕṇḍuŋ,
maṅde rĕs niŋ tumiṅhal raṅin i bala nira n lwiṙ gĕlap tan pawaṙṣa*

lamban loṙ saŋ susenā saha bala kadi siṅha asiga asiṅhanāda,
salwiṙ niŋ sañjata alas nira pinakaguhā rūpa niŋ hastirĕṅga,
wyāghra aṅjurw-a apupul tiṅkaḥ i bala nira muṅgw-i i harĕp sāra śūra,
buddhinya asiŋ musuḥ kewala dĕmakĕn ikā pawwatanya i narendra*

nā saŋ hemāṅgada aḍĕm sawatĕk ira kabeḥ riŋ kĕpuḥ rambay-akrĕp,
tan pendaḥ rākṣasa mwaŋ bala nira kadi dꜽtya aṅuhuḥ sāri-sāri,
solaḥnya n kādbhuta asañjata baḍama lawan laṇḍĕsanya n pamöki,
agya amūka iŋ musuḥ sāsinĕsĕb ika turuŋ matya laṅgan ya raḥnya*

paṙṇnaḥ wetan walū mwaŋ karamayan aṅurambat mara iŋ siṅkṣapa agöŋ,
saŋ pāṇḍya aṅhöb karĕsrĕs kagiri giri baṅun rāja bhūta atirodra,
wadwā peka asĕmu preta hana kadi piśāca alapā raḥ paḍa aṅhruk,
agyā gyān apraṅa agya aṅrujaka hati nikaŋ śūra sāmpun pinökan*

nā liŋ saŋ mambaŋ ojaṙ saŋ aja mijil ikaŋ buddhi kakṣatriyāṅśan,
siṅgiḥ kweḥ niŋ musuḥ liṅta kadi jaladhi bahny-atrigañca aṅgaluntaŋ,
ndātan waŋ mātra wĕdy-a aku dan irika kabeḥ mon patambĕḥ samāna,
siṅha aṅanti i guhā byūha nika surupi wūk hĕntyakĕn hīnaśakti*

nāhan liŋ saŋ narāṙyyātmaja kadi sinaṅa twas nira asĕṅhit apriḥ,
tan saḥ saŋ mambaŋ āpan marĕk añamarani mwaŋ kawi ḍaṇḍanīti,
siṅgiḥ yan putra niŋ śakti saŋ aja katĕṅĕṙ krūrasiṅha awamāna,
agya amūka iŋ musuḥ duṣṭa kamadan ika śīṙṇnan marapwan panĕmbaḥ*

sākṣāt hyaŋ niŋ dhanurweda saŋ aja sakala n pāwak iŋ dhaṙmmayuddha,
raktākāra akiris wastra nira kilat i sub niŋ praŋ asriŋ larapnya,
saṅka iŋ swaṙgga anurun cāmara nira kumĕlab roma niŋ saṙwwakadga,
saṅhub niŋ sañjata aḍĕm pinakapayuŋ ira antuk niŋ aṅdaṇḍa śatru*

hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ tuṅgaṅan sārathi nira wĕka niŋ siddhi sāmbĕknya siddha,
ratna inādyūta de hyaŋ rawi ratha nira tan manda-manda prabhānya,
śuddhākāra aputiḥ roma ni kuda nira pöḥ niŋ prabhā niŋ śaśāṅka,
rwaŋ lakṣa ŋ sūṙyyabaddhadhwaja nira piturun saŋ hyaŋ āditya sewu*

akweḥ sāmantaputra aṅiriŋ i sira paḍa atuṅgalan saṙggacāpa,
pantĕs lwiṙ hyaŋ-hyaŋ iŋ sañjata tĕka rumaras māṙ twas iŋ śatru denya,
sewu kweḥnya anwam anwam wruḥ akuda kudan iŋ papraṅan wīraputra,
jihwā niŋ mrĕtyu sākṣāt dhwaja nira dumilaḥ rājasiṅha amarĕmpu*

wīra prajñā juru dyaḥ nira sama-sama gandhaṙwwa denya amawa ambĕk,
ilwa ilwanya anwam  anwam saṅaŋ iwu taruṇa anaknya mantrī narendra,
apriḥ riŋ praŋ sujanma aratha rathan apupul tan saḥ iŋ waṅśa sālas,
wālāṙkkākāra sākṣāt lwiṙ ika n aruṇamegha dhwajanya pradīpta*

sakweḥ-kweḥ niŋ rare jro wani hañaṙ anapuk sañjata agya amriha iŋ praŋ,
rwaŋ lakṣa kweḥnya mĕtta aṅuhuḥ aṅayam-ayam śatru mwaŋ dèwa dꜽtya,
anwam wruḥ riŋ dhanurweda juru nika huwus kāku siṅhanya riŋ praŋ,
dewāṅga aneka tuṅgulnya saṅaŋ iwu kadi indrādi milwa amuka iŋ praŋ*

ambĕk niŋ dāsa śūra apraṅa rumuhun apan kāsatan pwa ṅhatinya,
mattā wīṙyya aṅuhuḥ göŋ ni kamanan ika riŋ praŋ murub tan pahīṅan,
miṅsoṙ mĕntas mariŋ tuṅgaṅan apan ahuyaŋ kweḥnya sewwaṙwwuda aḍĕm,
mātaṅganya apupul mwaŋ dhwaja nika dumilaḥ citramegha akilat mās*

saŋ jurw-a aja abala rwaŋ prayuta pinakasenāpati prāṇa niŋ praŋ,
kapwa adandan rukuḥ mās kawaca minaṇikan lwiṙ samudrāgni muntab,
wadwa aṅjurw-aprameya aratha sayuta gajaḥnya atatā sewu lakṣa,
lāka aneka dhwajanya n pracalita kadi bahni i sĕḍĕŋ niŋ yugānta*

mantrī rwaŋ lakṣa sāmpun ginĕlaṙ i hiriṅan bāhudaṇḍa aṅgakāra,
len tekaŋ pādarakṣa prakaṭa kadi tasik rwaŋ puluḥ duṙgga niŋ praŋ,
aṙppat muṅgw-i i tĕṅaḥ śrī nrĕpasuta mukha niŋ siṅha śāṙddūla śakti,
kady-a agastya aṅuyup sāgara wunuhan ikaŋ byūha sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

aṙppat ikaŋ waragaŋ sahasa siliḥ usī paḍa nora wĕdi,
siŋ sakasambut ikaŋ pinakagada gadānya paḍa amurulu,
umban aliwran arok rĕmĕk iŋ awaŋ-awaŋ kapagut kawaluy,
dukduk ikā kadi saṙppa pakan aṅin aneka hana iŋ gagana*

wwaŋ bahula atuha milw-ajurit alara tĕṇḍas ikā ginutuk,
Ꜽ putu liŋnya nihan laku walĕsi gutuk buru demu pisuḥ,
ndi n wĕnaŋ aṅgutuka aṅrahana tan ubhaya aku putu prihawak,
dwal putu demu palakwan i katigawĕlas tĕṅaha i laku ta*

brāhmaṇa wany-apuliḥ galaḥ apupul aḍĕm pinurugnya rĕbaḥ,
tan wruḥ aweda kuraŋ-kuraŋ aji makapaṅhaḍa timbul ikā,
kepwan ikaŋ musuḥ amraṅa paḍa wĕdi yan raḥ ikā mijila,
ṅhiŋ pamĕdinya pulut-pulutan ika ta hetu nikā malayū*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

nya ŋ sogata anwam ajurit kĕna tan dwa bĕntar,
mojaṙ kutiknya ḍuḥ uḍuḥ pukulun laranya,
ya ika n mijil para cĕṅĕlnya nĕhĕṙ sinuṇḍaŋ,
kadyaṅgan iŋ ghaṭa rĕmĕk tika yan panaṇḍĕm*

śꜽwa apuliḥ kĕna pilis wulaṅun kajuṅkĕl,
mitra anuluŋ mpu mapa teku manaḥta maṅko,
eṅĕt ṅhulun ri kita bhāgya tasim yan eṅĕt,
strī ni ṅhulun kita tulakṣaya ko hada iki*

nā liŋ nira mpu tucapa ŋ prajurit siliḥ praŋ,
Ārok rinok awuṙ-awuṙ paḍa tan wri rātnya,
teg tog ḍaḍap nika bubul ginalaḥ tinaṅkis,
ḍöhak musuḥnya sinuḍatnya pĕjaḥ kasoran*

gĕntöṙ i śabda ni gubaṙnya baṅun siliḥ prĕp,
kady-a acakĕp dhwani nikaŋ kukulan karĕsrĕs,
kaṅsinya lāgi manaḥ ambĕk iŋ ajriḥ iŋ praŋ,
moṅmoṅan aṅgyat anamaṙ macan asriŋ oliḥ*

wadwā nrĕpātmaja tumampuhakĕn gadānya,
rwaŋ lakṣa tan kuraŋ asĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,
akweḥ tikĕl-tikĕl igā ni lawanya rĕmpuḥ,
aṅrwaŋ pulūḥ uliḥ ikā ri patuṅgalanya*

wīra anapuk raṅin apiṇḍa sahasra wrĕnda,
meww-i iwu koṭi pagalaḥnya parĕŋ tumampuḥ,
gĕk ghoṙ rĕbaḥ wiphala siŋ kinayuḥnya runtuḥ,
sawrĕnda māti ginalaḥ sawaneḥ pinökan*

sewwaṙwwuda amana manaḥ mwaŋ ikāŋ agaṇḍi,
tandaŋnya tan dwa kinawĕdyan apan karĕsrĕs,
hrūnya anrik iŋ gagana söḥ kadi megha mĕṇḍuŋ,
saṙ cĕb tiba aṅĕnani siŋ kĕna tan pasāra*

wadwā narendra malayū sawatĕk watĕknya,
peka prawīra kĕna tan dwa yaya praŋ aṅrok,
kombak linūd awalikan kumĕlab dhwajanya,
himpĕṙ nadī kinĕbuṙ iŋ gaja sewu lakṣa*

bhātriṅśa lakṣa ŋ apuliḥ kalulun kawaṅsul,
kālaḥ tibā siliḥ idĕk sinĕsĕb pinökan,
rĕmpak tikĕl wiphala salwiṙ i sañjatanya,
lwiṙ kaywa kaywan asipattra rĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*

wadwā nareśwara inatyan ira iŋ kasiṅhan,
śakti prawīra parapök i musuḥ yan iŋ praŋ,
ya ika apuliḥ tan awĕdi i ripubāṇawaṙṣa,
wany-a anusup tĕpĕt amūk makasoŋ ḍaḍapnya*

kagyat balā nrĕpatiputra maluy-tinaṅkis,
akweḥ an amriha tawan tiki tan kagöman,
mĕṅgĕp kadi jriḥ akikib malayū tan adrĕs,
munduṙ yayā bala nareśwara duṙbala alwaŋ*

tan jriḥ bala nrĕpati dhꜽṙyya saha abhimāna,
apraŋ karuŋ paḍa tumiṅgalakĕn ḍaḍapnya,
de niŋ siliḥ pĕḍĕk arok wĕkasan siliḥ prĕp,
bĕk tĕg hĕhĕḥ kahĕnĕkan jriḥ ikaŋ lumumpat*

awra alayū bala narendrasuta awrĕg awrin,
śakti prawīra kapana n kĕna pakṣa pakṣan,
hamham tĕka aṅamaḥ amaḥ bala saŋ narendra,
apyak tĕkapnya n aṅucap tuhu siṅha riŋ praŋ*

Ꜽ koŋ watĕk raghusuta priḥ awakmu maṅko,
haywa apraŋ unduṙ athawā paṅaliḥ para ṅke,
Āpan ya tan hana sihankwa ri kāsy-asihmu,
kāton pĕjahmu pususĕṅkwa ri sañjataṅku*

nā liŋ nika amutuŋ aṅĕmbuli tan panaṅgĕl,
kweḥnya aprameya kadi sāgara tan papiṅgir,
maṙmmanya wāni sahasa amraŋ amūk tumiṇḍiḥ,
dukduk panaḥ kadi hudan ya ta paṅharĕpnya*

aṅwehi sañjata humuŋ gumuruḥ suraknya,
aṅrok atambĕḥ i harĕp kumucup dhwajanya,
akweḥ pĕjaḥ tan awĕdi i pati maṅkin embuḥ,
lwiṙ laṙwwa laṙwwan arĕbut damaṙ alwaŋ embuḥ*

krūra apuliḥ bala narendrasuta amuk amriḥ,
munduṙ bala nrĕpati śīghra muwaḥ tumampuḥ,
enak siliḥ galaḥ apan paḍa wāni-wāni,
söḥ sāhasa aṅuḍik uḍik praŋ ikā siliḥ sob*

enak mara apraŋ arukĕt paḍa nora mundur,
rwaŋ yojana ŋ pabharatan paḍa söḥ gaja aśwa,
sāmpun rĕbaḥ wukiṙ anaknya watunya kabwaŋ,
akweḥ juraŋ mari juraŋ wĕkasan kahinya*

ṅkāna i ruhuṙ gunuŋ ikaŋ praŋ arok siliḥ sob,
apraŋ sumĕṅka tumurun paḍa rota rodra,
rĕp tan katon hanan awās tĕkap iŋ hima awrā,
ramya atulis praŋ ika konĕŋ unĕŋ tinonton*

brahmaṙṣi śewa sugatādi ri soṙ anonton,
mwaŋ wwaŋ jriḥ iŋ raṇa huwus katuhan wayaḥnya,
kweḥnya atata anudiṅi haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ tumĕṅhā,
akrak paḍa atri gumuruḥ ri paṅadwakĕnya*

rīyūk rĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ rinĕbut sinökan,
rīyūk rĕbaḥ muwaḥ alaḥ kasĕsöḥ ikaŋ lor,
rīyūk rĕbaḥ muwaḥ ikaŋ kidul alwaŋ akweḥ,
rīyūk rĕbaḥ pinĕgatan wĕdi wök ikaŋ lor*

Āḥ uḥ piraŋ juru muwaḥ saka loṙ tumandaŋ,
rīyūk rĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ binurunya kagyat,
kady-a anutuḥ kalapa denya mamöki tĕṇḍas,
nā liŋ nikā hana ta len aṅutū kapūhan*

śīṙṇna ŋ samaṇḍala-samaṇḍala konduran syuḥ,
awrĕg paḍa aṅhili sira mpu tĕka iŋ kaninyan,
aprakprakan di ta kaki hyaŋ ujaṙ nini hyaŋ,
putrī nikā kaburĕṅek-burĕṅek tinaṅguŋ*

sāmpun tĕka i ruhuṙ iŋ agra muwaḥ paḍa awrĕg,
wwaŋ wrĕddha-wrĕddha guru niny-aṅuhuḥ saka i sor,
pāran pinawrĕgakĕn ā mapa liŋ kaki hyaŋ,
wikw-a añaruk wiṣaya rakwa nimitta niŋ wrĕg*

lāwan turun patapan ĕmbuli haywa mundur,
ambĕk ṅwaŋ iŋ kaguru ninyan alaḥ padandan,
ṅwaŋ pwa atuha alaḥ alaḥ ĕmpu buyut ta lampaḥ,
nā liŋ nini mpu kabalik wĕdi wök kaki mpu*

wīra apraŋ iŋ tĕgal ayun paḍa wāni-wāni,
kontab maṅontabakĕn amraŋ amūk añakra,
kedĕṙ paḍa akuliliṅan gumuluŋ rathanya,
lwiṙ nāga moliḥ amĕbĕd gaja matta sālas*

enak dahat praŋ ika kādbhuta riŋ triloka,
Āpan katuhwan atĕwĕk tĕwĕkan paḍa akris,
len taŋ siliḥ tujaḥ amatrĕm amajra maṅduk,
bāhunya runtuḥ asakit trus aṅĕmbak-ĕmbak*

sojaṙnya kātara nĕhĕṙ marahup rahup raḥ,
hāmaḥ śiraḥ hurupa jīwamu haywa ta ajriḥ,
haywa adwa bhoḥ ndya ta śiraḥ mata maḥ ndya jīwa,
bwat kaprawīran iki tan dadi mithyawāda*

nā liŋ nikā tucapa śabda ri de nika apraŋ,
pyak byuṙ kĕpuk kĕtĕlĕbuk kĕḍĕpĕk kĕtug tog,
ceŋ has tĕhap-tĕhap aḍuḥ gĕdĕbĕg ḍĕhak syok,
caṙccab lĕbik bĕk aḍu göŋ gumĕcik gĕlĕmpöŋ*

nāhan taŋ ĕlwan asĕluṙ karĕṅö karĕsrĕs,
maṅde bhayānaka pasaṅgha nikā gumĕntĕr,
len taŋ mahātiśaya rodra paṅalw-alönya,
wīra aṅgĕtĕm nĕhĕṙ aṅohan i meḥnya matya*

<wisaṙjjita> 
– ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓ : 20

śrī magadhādhipa sāhasa mijil abhimāna nira iŋ palagan,
nāgamayāstra laras nira sĕḍĕŋ inayat bhramita ŋ prĕthiwī,
göŋ swara niŋ tali de ny-aṅin ika kumusuḥ mĕtu kātatakut,
hrū nika kādbhuta kātara gunuŋ ahĕlaṙ warakadga murub*

prajwalitāgni cucuknya kagiri-giri dhūma dilaḥnya murub,
sek gumuruḥ paṅawaknya kumisik amĕgat jalada iŋ gagana,
boṙ kumutug śara bajra saŋ aja kumĕtug lĕpas aṅdwiguṇa,
teg tumibā ŋ wihagācala mati pinanaḥ makĕbĕt kĕbĕtan*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

muntab krodha saŋ aṅganātha kadi bahni maṅaraman i puñcak iŋ wukir,
ṅkāna i kūwara niŋ ratha amahayu lañciṅan ira pinisit siniṅsĕtan,
hrū lāwan laras adwitīya sinamādhy-amijilakĕna saṙwwasañjata,
wuntw-i ikaŋ gaganāntarāla tĕkap iŋ panaḥ atip atĕtĕl turuŋ tibā*

dewanya awurahan tĕka aṅamaḥ amaḥ harĕp amususa riŋ nrĕpātmaja,
lwiṙ meghodaya māghamāsa sumaput pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
saŋ hyaŋ bāywanala pracaṇḍa pamanaḥ nrĕpatanaya dumeḥ kawaṅsula,
bĕk gĕk toṙ cĕrĕcĕb tiba iŋ bala nareśwara makasulayaḥ kawaṅsulan*

śakti iŋ praŋ saŋ awantinātha sira mrĕtyu sakala yan i madhya niŋ musuḥ,
maṅgĕḥ buddhi nira apuliḥ nĕhĕṙ aṅakw-amĕjahana nareśwarātmaja,
rāhasya antya nikaŋ kaśaktin inayat nira mĕtu ŋ ayudha agnipaṙwwata,
boṙ muṅgw-iŋ gaganāntarāla paḍa yatna bala saŋ aja kebĕkan panas*

tan kewran saŋ aja apan adbhuta kaśaktin ira tumiru śakti saŋ raghu,
rĕp mārādhana pañcabāyu mĕtu kātaratara gumĕrĕḥ magĕnturan,
kabwaŋ taŋ śara paṙwwata agni kadi handaru sayuta dilaḥnya riŋ laṅit,
bhuṙ tog söŋ prĕkĕtĕk nahan swara nika amĕkasi hurip i madhya niŋ tasik*

maṅsö sāhasa tan surud saŋ anupādhipati manaḥ ira n wani iŋ raṇa,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda len grit iŋ ratha karĕṅw-asĕluṙ i hiriṅan hana i harĕp,
pakrak niŋ balasaṅgha maṅgyat aṅasut ri bala saŋ aja wāni kāmbulan,
teg tok lwiṙ garuḍa aḍahĕm kĕtug ikaŋ gubaṙ asahuran apratidhwani*

sāmpunya n lumĕpas panaḥ saŋ anupādhipa kadi ruga ŋ aṇḍamaṇḍala,
pātālastha samāpta nāga lĕkĕṙ iŋ bhuwana rumĕbuti nrĕpātmaja,
porot boṙ dumilaḥ mara ŋ wiṣa sinĕmburakĕn ika hana atĕmaḥ kukus,
byuṙ laṙ lĕs paḍa mukṣa de ni kuku saŋ garuḍa wahu minuṣṭi riŋ laras*

<sragdhara> 
– – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓ : 21

krodha ambĕk saŋ susenā saha bala sumaput kātara asiṅhanāda,
haṙṣa n ton saŋ narāṙyyātmaja pinakamusuḥ kewala anuṅga nuṅgal,
hrū-hrū śakti iŋ daṅū söḥ linĕpasakĕn ira ataṅkis akrak karĕsrĕs,
Āpan pakṣy-a ahĕlaṙ sañjata kadi garuḍa aneka seww-aṙwwuda ahöm*

sumyaŋ sumyak hĕlaṙnya n kinirigakĕn ika aghāṣa muntab dilaḥnya,
sumyuk tan kāwaran drĕṣṇya kadi dinukakĕn yan tumandaŋ saka iŋ doḥ,
kāṇḍĕg katrĕn dinuk de saŋ aja linud ira iŋ cakra puṅgĕl gulūnya,
perat sok raḥnya saṅka iŋ ḍaḍa nika kawutaḥ mrĕm tiba adoḥ gumĕntĕr*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgada amriḥ-mriḥ apuliḥ i luyuk saŋ susenā katampĕk,
sāmpun kempun sinimpĕn bala saŋ aja paḍa krūra kedran kawuṅkus,
syuḥ tan sārā sa hemāṅgada mati tinĕḍak bĕntaṙ alwaŋ salakṣa,
kāry-aṅlīlā narendra amanahakĕn irikaŋ sāgara atyanta rodra*

śīghra rwabnya aṅgaluntaŋ gaganacara lĕpas māmpuhan matrigañca,
lĕmboranya aṅlayaŋ kābhinawa kadi gunuŋ sewu māliḥ marampak,
sumyūk adrĕs tumĕmpuḥ ri saŋ aja kawaluy-de ni göŋ niŋ kaśaktin,
mawrĕg luṅha astra de hyaŋ baruṇasuta karĕṣṇya n hilaŋ tan paśeṣa*

saŋ pāṇḍya amaḥ gunuŋ sāhasa tĕka rumahab de ni göŋ niŋ kamānan,
sākṣāt guntuṙ saka iŋ paṙwwata tumurun atūt lwaḥ juraŋ duṙggama ajro,
mātaṅga mwaŋ ratha lwiṙ watu gumuluŋ apan tan pararyan lakunya,
krodha amĕṇṭaŋ laras saŋ prabhu mamanahakĕn bahni saṅka iŋ samudra*

lumrā riŋ dik widik teja nika saha panasnya aṅgĕsĕŋ saṙwwawrĕkṣa,
sakweḥ niŋ megha mĕṇḍuŋ pinaṅan ika huwus hĕnti lāwan gĕlapnya,
lwiṙ jihwānya ŋ mahāmrĕtyu dumilata narendrātmaja atyanta rodra,
saŋ hyaŋ kālāgni muṅgw-i i naraca saŋ aja maṙmmanya māti iŋ raṇāṅga*

<basantatilaka> 
– – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓ : 14

saŋ pāṇḍya soṙ titiḥ alaḥ malayū tinaṅkis,
wadwā nira alara hilaŋ kahala awrĕg alwaŋ,
Āpan siliḥ praŋ arĕbut hawan ahrit ewĕḥ,
wadwā nrĕpātmaja maluy-sakarĕŋ mararyan*

saŋ saptarāja sumahab saha bhrĕtyamantrī,
sāmpun sira aṅhabĕtakĕn dhwaja śīghra maṅkat,
saṙ sök prawīra gumuruḥ kadi sāgara rwab,
lwiṙ siṅha sāṙwwuda paḍa akrak asiṅhanāda*

wīra atyan iŋ wani hinatyan inĕṇḍĕm-ĕṇḍĕm,
agya apraŋ aṅgĕtĕm atön maṅusap lĕṅĕnya,
mwaŋ saṙwwasañjata nikā milu haṙṣa riŋ praŋ,
paṅliṅgana aṅiṅis-iṅis kumĕñaṙ wajanya*

hamham tĕka amanaḥ añakra bubak sakāmbaḥ,
rodra amupak cĕṅĕl amūk arĕbut kasiṅhan,
len taŋ paḍa apapatihan kuḍuwak paḍa akre,
saṅhāra kātĕkan i rūpa nika n karĕsrĕs*

śūra amĕrĕḥ kadi surat tĕkap iŋ kaśūran,
kontanya kādbhuta sahasra kuwuŋ kuwuŋnya,
asraŋ kĕtug ni panutugnya ḍaḍap gumĕntĕr,
himpĕṙ prabhāwa ni musuḥnya pĕjaḥ kapökan*

munduṙ bala nrĕpatiputra tinūt cinakra,
awrā rinampak inirup pinanaḥ ginaṇḍi,
ndātan wĕdi iŋ panaḥ atip kadi megha mĕṇḍuŋ,
tahw-a ahudan-hudan i madhya niŋ astrawaṙṣa*

wadwā narādhipati sāhasa tan panaṅgĕl,
śāṙddūla śakti pinakāgramukha iŋ kasiṅhan,
mañjiŋ mara iŋ pakĕkĕs iŋ wunuhan tĕka amraŋ,
tan sāra hĕnti satĕṅaḥ rinakut kadi bras*

kagyat winūk pinĕgatan tinalaṅkup awrĕg,
tiṅgalnya sañjata ratha aśwa sahasra saṅkhya,
kedĕṙ gajaḥnya rinubuŋ dinudut śinūla,
lwiṙ waṅkay-iŋ walaŋ inīrakĕn iŋ sĕmut baŋ*

saŋ saptarāja kadi saptasamudra muntab,
de niŋ kamānawibhawan pinakaswabhāwa,
maṅsö saha aśwa ratha wāhana meru tulya,
apwī saka iŋ panaḥ ira ujwala mumbul-umbul*

meghodaya amaḍĕmi sakṣaṇa tan paśeṣa,
saṅka i panaḥ nrĕpatiputra lawan halisyus,
mĕtw-a amusus-musus anūb ratharĕṅga kabwaŋ,
lāwan gĕlap makasulambĕṙ anambĕṙ aṅgyat*

saŋ saptarāja saha bhrĕtya rĕbaḥ katampĕk,
bĕntaṙ winūk saha gaja aśwa ratha alaḥ awrĕg,
guntuṙ prawīra kumusuḥ katĕḍun mara iŋ lwaḥ,
himpĕṙ gunuŋ pituŋ atus rĕbaḥ iŋ samudra*

saŋ saptarāja kabĕlĕt wĕkasan sira adan,
rĕp sy-andaka awak aśarīra liman sawrĕnda,
saṅka i panaḥ nira mijil tĕkap iŋ kasiddhyan,
wuntu ŋ nabhastala lawan prĕthiwī kasĕṅkö*

śīghra anurumbunuḥ amūk ri narendraputra,
atyadbhuta alimunan iŋ gaganāntarāla,
mĕtta aṅuliŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukūs umaṇḍĕm,
saŋ saptarāja humuŋ atry-asurak gumĕntĕr*

de niŋ maṅadwakĕn apiṇḍa tĕkap niŋ apraŋ,
Āḥ āḥ mati sy-aja mulat muliṅā kaṅelan,
kedran kawuṅkus i tĕṅaḥ kalulun kapĕṇḍĕm,
nā liŋ nira aṅgĕtĕm atön dan asiṅhanāda*

kāla nrĕpātmaja n inambulan iŋ gajendra,
eṅĕt sira amanahakĕn śara hastiśikṣā,
meww-i iwu hĕnti mati śīghra parĕŋ tumĕmpĕk,
himpĕṙ namuk tinĕpak alwaŋ atambĕḥ akweḥ*

riŋ sakṣaṇa nrĕpatiputra kumöl ayoga,
saŋ hyaŋ smarāntakaśarāgni mijil saka iŋ hrū,
śīṙṇna ŋ gajaḥ ginĕsĕṅan paḍa bhasmibhūta,
lumrā hawunya kumutug baṅun andhakāra*

krodha aṅayat śarawarāgni narendraputra,
Āpan musuḥ nira sudhīra mahāprabhāwa,
maṅsö paḍa aṅṅpasakĕn śara nāgapāśa,
tapwan tĕka apan awilĕt pinĕgat nira iŋ hrū*

saŋ saptarāja paḍa śakti widagdha riŋ praŋ,
wil krūra dꜽtya pamanaḥ nira sewu lakṣa,
krodha amupul sĕmut amūk ri narendraputra,
himpĕṙ graha aṅhibĕki rāt marĕbut śaśāṅka*

siṅhaprawīra saŋ aja aṅayat astra śakti,
ḍaṅṣṭrā niŋ antaka minuṣṭi huwus minantran,
dewātmaka amawa gadāyudha mĕtw-arampak,
mawrĕg pĕjaḥ siliḥ idĕk para dꜽtya mukṣa*

an maṅkana praŋ ira tan hana soṙ awantaḥ,
maṅsö nrĕpātmaja lawan naranātha maṅsö,
tĕmpuḥ ni sañjata nira apagut ātirodra,
himpĕṙ gunuŋ madu gumĕntĕṙ inadw-atĕmpuḥ*

liṇḍū bĕlaḥ bhramita bhūmi nikaŋ raṇāṅga,
mwaŋ saptapaṙwwata kadi inayun agraḥ olaḥ,
pātāla sapta kadudut kagiriŋ kagiṅgaŋ,
nya ŋ saptasāgara katumpĕk arok bañunya*

kweḥ niŋ pĕjaḥ saka salakṣa sahasra wrĕnda,
len taŋ paḍa amĕkasi jīwa humūŋ aṅohan,
meḥ matya maṅrĕguŋ ikaŋ gajaḥ asriŋ aṅgro,
abyūran iŋ rudhirasāgara kombakan ṙyyak*

mātaṅga len turaga nūsa nika aṅalimbuŋ,
saṙwwāstra kaywan ika śīṙṇna marok dhwaja akrĕp,
ṅkāna ŋ prawīra marĕbut phala niŋ kasiṅhan,
wetnya alĕyö kasidĕkuŋ sidĕkuŋ siliḥ praŋ*

ṅkāna i pasiṙ-pasiṙ ikā naranāthaputra,
apraŋ lawan ratu kawīśwara riŋ palambaŋ,
hrū muṅgw-i kaṙṇna nira piṇḍa tanaḥ kasumpiŋ,
tapwan warĕg praŋ alaṅö lagi kombakan raḥ*

rudrāyudhāgni pinasaŋ naranāthaputra,
duṙggānala adbhuta mijil pamanaḥ narendra,
trus riŋ laṅit dilaḥ ika asĕmu megha bahni,
lumra awilĕt latu latunya mahāsura akrak*

prodbhūta kātara dahat patĕmunya kāliḥ,
maṅkin tĕka i ruhuṙ aṅambara kaprahāran,
saŋ hyaŋ śiwāṙkka kasuban pan asoṙ sira agyaŋ,
luṅha ahawan kuda lumiṅsiṙ adoḥ maṅulwan*

widyādharī saha wimāna sumaṅgraha akweḥ,
muṅgw-i i tawaŋ wruḥ irikaŋ wani wāni riŋ praŋ,
dukduk hayunya sinahāyan iŋ ambĕk ahyaŋ,
haṙṣa amapag ri para wīra pĕjaḥ kapökan*

sāmbĕk niŋ onĕŋ alawas tinĕkan rarasnya,
kāmīrasa ayam ayamanya sĕḍĕŋ bhinukti,
tan lot dhumāraṇa panas nikaŋ agnibāṇa,
luṅhā lawan priya nikā sukha rāmya māṙgga*

saptaṙṣi dewagaṇa guhyaka siddha-siddha,
anrik hana iŋ gagana sāṙwwuda riŋ sapaṇṭa,
göŋ niŋ praŋ adbhuta ya hetu nira n panonton,
milw-a asurak nĕhĕṙ aṅadwakĕn akrak ahyā*

luṅhā muwaḥ kapanasan paḍa tan hana aṅher,
saŋ nārada asyaŋ aṅuhuḥ ri narendraputra,
Ꜽ putra toḥ bapa wulat ndak apintakāsiḥ,
hrūnta agni śakti paḍĕmĕnta sihanta ri hyaŋ*

mwaŋ paṅrĕṅökw-i kita yan pinakāntaśāpa,
de saŋ priyambada sĕḍĕŋnya gajendrarūpa,
kāruṇya māsiḥ amalĕs ri waluy-nira hyaŋ,
saṅmohana ikaŋ inajinta kĕnoḥ parīkṣan*

an maṅkana ujaṙ ira śīghra narendraputra,
mārādhana amrĕta sinrĕṣṭi ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ hrū,
sumyuk saka iŋ awaŋ-awaŋ kadi riŋ paṅipyan,
dhwasta ŋ śara anala paḍĕm paḍa bhasmibhūta*

saŋ saptarāja paḍa śakti parĕŋ tumandaŋ,
kapwa aṅhudan hudani sañjata bāyubajra,
atyanta tan paṅupama i saŋ aja apan anwam,
muṅgw-iŋ ratha anudiṅi wākcapala awalepa*

Ꜽ rājaputra mapa ta aṅĕn aṅĕnmu maṅko,
Āpan huwus wruḥ aku yan kapalaŋ manahmu,
trĕṣṇan purihmu ri huripmw-apan anwam awri,
nā pādukaṅku pakacāmana sambahĕmwa*

nāhan wuwus nrĕpati senaka ri twas apyak,
pāruṣyaśabda mada tan wruḥ i śakti niŋ len,
krodha nrĕpatmaja sumöŋ i mukha ŋ kamānan,
sabhya aṅucap sahuṙ ira atĕhĕṙ aṅdĕdĕl twas*

sanwam nwamaṅkwa n aku siṅhakula prawīra,
tak nāgata iŋ atuha tiṅhali demu maṅko,
sakweḥ ni sañjatamu tan hana paṅgaritnya,
byakta n pacuṇḍaŋ i bapaṅku kabeḥ kabehmu*

nā liŋ narendrasuta śakty-aṅayat warāstra,
saṅmohana smrĕti nira iŋ kṣaṇa n ekacitta,
nidra aṅaweśa sumaput ri lĕpas nikaŋ hrū,
mrĕm saŋ watĕk ratu huwus kĕna tan pasāra*

sāmānya peka rumuhun para taṇḍa mantrī,
mātaṅga matta turaga aṅrĕpa tan wri rātnya,
mūṙccha aturū kadi tasik wwaŋ ikaŋ raṇāṅga,
mombak raṅin gajaḥ aghaṇṭa karaŋ liman ya*

sāmpun jaya iŋ raṇasabhā naranāthaputra,
saŋ saptarāja kadi māti parĕŋ katurwan,
tĕkwan huwus kacuriṅan raḥ i tuṅtuŋ iŋ hrū,
ya ikā siluṅluŋ ira yan kaparājaya iŋ praŋ*

saŋ hyaŋ sira ajaya jaya iŋ gaganāntarāla,
mwaŋ puṣpawaṙṣa tumibā kadi kasturi mrik,
prīty-a adara nrĕpatiputra sinādhukāra,
sāmpun maṅañjali sahaṙṣa nĕhĕṙ tumĕṅhā*

<jagaddhita> 
– – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

sāmpun byakta kacakrawaṙttyan i nrĕpātmaja ri huwus ira amarājaya,
nora lwaŋ nira pūṙṇna maṅkana sasañjata nira kadi ṅūni dug siṅī,
sakweḥ niŋ bala śūrasaṅgha humatuṙ paḍa maṅarahakĕn lumampaha,
maṅkat śri indumatī lawan nrĕpatiputra paḍa sukha makālihan ratha*

tiṅkaḥ-tiṅkaḥ i de nira apraŋ inucap winarahakĕn ira i suputrikā,
mojaṙ śri indumatī wagus kita kaka apa hamĕṅan ikanaŋ watĕk ratu,
rakryan ya iki panahkw-amuṅwakĕna tan dadi wiphala lĕpasnya riŋ musuḥ,
saṅhārāstra wimohanākhya paṅalaḥ pinakakajayaśatrun i ṅhulun*

nāhan liŋ nrĕpaputra rakwa tadanantara nrĕpati parĕŋ sira awuṅu,
mwaŋ mantrī saha bhrĕtya wāhana turaṅga warurutĕn aṅob ariṅguṅan,
eraŋ de ni kahīnakāyan ira tuccha kacuriṅan alaḥ sira iŋ raṇa,
ry-antuk saŋ prabhu tan kathākĕna kunĕŋ nrĕpasuta sira waṙṇnanĕn muwaḥ*

sāmpun mintaṙ adoḥ laku nrĕpatiputra manĕmu haraṇān ḍusun-ḍusun,
piṅgiṙ-piṅgiṙ ikaŋ hĕnū pakapasan pakalayaran apaṇṭa tan parok,
ewĕḥ tan satinūtakĕn rupit ikāŋ aṅiwa hana nĕṅĕn paḍa agĕnĕt,
tan tuṅgal kasasaṙ humuŋ siliḥ uhuḥ kapasaḥ asahuran siliḥ taña*

duṅhus niŋ palapat kahundul aruhuṙ kabuyutan alawas kinatwaṅan,
pañca aṙṇnik winĕlaŋ sakanya pinakolul ika tawiŋ ikā hibĕk parab,
wwaŋnya akweḥ mapupul hana aṅiduṅakĕn ri gaway-ira nareśwarātmaja,
lantuŋ mambw-awaṅi inasū nika ginanti saha caru sinaṅgaran hañar*

ṅkāna i soṙ talaga ahĕniŋ hana buyut-buyut iwak arĕbut walaŋ tibā,
piṅgiṙnya inasaban paras hawan ikā siniku siku hinambalan watu,
raṅrö kaywan ikā lawan kĕpuḥ agöŋ jaha wijaḥ asĕkaṙ lawan winöŋ,
akweḥ sĕñjaŋ ika ajajaṙ hana kawadwan ana kalanaṅan dinudwakĕn*

meḥ-meḥ rwaŋ puluhaŋ kulĕm lawas ira aṅhinĕp i huwus ira apraŋ iŋ hĕnū,
prāpta iŋ thāni ḍusun kaḍatwan iŋ usāna parawaśa rinampak iŋ musuḥ,
piṅgiṙ niŋ talaga awukiṙ-wukiṙ anak patani nika manumpak aṅṅnaŋ,
ṅkāna śrī naranāthaputra maṅĕnaḥ kakawin uliḥ ira aṅdadak-dadak*

<wikrĕti> 
⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏓ : 23

dinĕlö ku jinarumanan iṅgut iŋ halis i kāla nika wahu mijil,
awuyuŋ miṅay-anirirakĕn susup-susup ika asana nĕhĕṙ ahidu,
irika akw-amĕgati turidaṅku tan wani mulat muwaḥ i mukha nikā,
sahaja aṅhuripakĕn atukup tukup ri pawahinku kadi kaluputan*

<jagadnātha> 
⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓ : 23

tĕwĕknya n inalap ni rena nika tan tahu katĕmu gĕnĕp tigaŋ tahun,
lipuṙ turida ni ṅhulun mari rimaŋ sinapihan i lawasnya tan katon,
kathañcana kapaṅgiḥ iŋ yaśa lawan panuluyan iriya aṅdadak lumuḥ,
pĕpĕt-pĕpĕt ikā ya ta n pinahaliṅsya nika ri paṅawenya ri ṅhulun*

<jagaddhita>
